PRIOR latest ‚Äî **BRK.B Evidence Card ‚Äî catastrophic stale-bars root cause + 4 user-reported issues**: `stocvest/data/polygon_client.py::get_bars` had defaulted `from_date="2000-01-01"` with `sort=asc&limit=N` since the engine was first written. Polygon honors both: this combination returns the OLDEST N bars in the range, not the newest. Live probe before the fix: "give me the 60 most recent BRK.B minute bars" returned 60 minute bars from **2003-09-10** (close ~$50 ‚Äî post-2010-split BRK.B price). Every SMA50 / SMA200 / RSI / MACD / VWAP / EMA / ATR / breakout / volatility / golden-cross computation in production has therefore been running against 22-year-old prices. The "VWAP $50.36 on a $485 stock" the user screenshotted is the smoking gun; the underlying "every name is bullish because today's price > 2003 price" bias is the iceberg. Fixed by splitting `get_bars` into two explicit modes ‚Äî `recent_mode` (both dates None) sends `sort=desc` and reverses results in Python before returning so callers still receive oldest-first chronological order, `range_mode` (any date pinned) keeps `sort=asc` for sector_daily_cache / orb_compute_worker / public bars handler. Live verification post-fix: SMA50=$479.58 (was $59.35), SMA200=$489.78 (was $57.88), BRK.B day-trade verdict flips from misleading "short" to honest "neutral". Same commit also: (a) adds `internals_alignment` chip to `confluence.py` mirroring sector-chip design (a bullish broad market on a short setup now lands as a counterweight chip ‚Äî the user's Issue 4); (b) rewrites `buildVerdictTagReconciler` to lead with the anchor list ‚Äî "Anchored by X and Y; counterweight(s): Z." ‚Äî retiring the "Bullish-leaning context on a short setup" cognitive contradiction (Issue 2); (c) hardens `captureDisplayText` with a 3-tier fallback chain (Anthropic text ‚Üí aiVerdict ‚Üí on-the-fly direction sentence) so the AI Signal Analysis section can never render as empty italic quotes (Issue 5), and removes the dangling `<span>Signal summary</span>` caption that had no value bound to it. Issue 1 (VWAP/EMA chip polarity) and Issue 3 (VWAP $50.36 value) were both consequences of the stale-bars catastrophe and resolve automatically once `get_bars` returns recent data. Broader audit walked every `get_bars` caller and every chip-generation path; no other related bugs found. Lock-in tests: +11 new (3 get_bars wire-level, 7 internals chip including a direct BRK.B regression, 1 singular-counterweight reconciler) plus a full rewrite of the existing 9 reconciler tests. Backend baseline now 1417 passing (+7 over 1410 from row 17). PRIOR ‚Äî **SPY/QQQ/IWM Shared Context tiles ‚Äî line sparkline ‚Üí signed 5-bar daily-returns histogram**: at the ~120px sub-card size in Shared Context ¬∑ Section A, a line sparkline conveyed effectively no information beyond the % label already rendered beneath it. Replaced with a 5-bar signed daily-returns histogram (one bar per regular trading session over the trailing week) that surfaces *intra-week shape* ‚Äî "steady grind up" vs "choppy reversal" vs "one-day gap-and-drift" all read at a glance instead of being collapsed into the same upward-leaning line. **new handler modules** `admin_users.py`, `admin_audit.py`, `admin_system_status.py`; `admin_parameters.py` extended with `admin_parameters_current_handler`. **Entitlement bump**: `_serialize_user_profile` accepts a new `is_admin` flag that OR-bumps `has_full_access` and `has_ai_explanations` so admins transparently get every paid feature for their **own** profile (the flag is intentionally `False` when an admin views **another** user via `admin_beta_access_patch_handler` ‚Äî bumping target flags based on actor's group would be a privilege confusion bug); `ai_explanations_handler` short-circuits via the same `analysis_authorized()` check by overlaying `beta_full_access=True` on a *copy* of the calling profile (never persisted). **IAM**: new `Sid=CognitoAdminUserDirectory` on `lambda_api_execution` scoped to the project Cognito user pool ARN granting the seven Cognito Admin* actions (ListUsers/ListUsersInGroup/AdminGetUser/AdminListGroupsForUser/AdminResetUserPassword/AdminAddUserToGroup/AdminRemoveUserFromGroup). **8 new API Gateway routes** in `infra/apigateway_6e.tf` (`signals` integration for parameters/system-status, `brokers` integration for user-mgmt + audit ‚Äî matching where the underlying IAM blast radius lives). **Bootstrap script** `scripts/grant_admin.py` (boto3 cognito-idp wrapper with `--grant`/`--revoke`/`--list` flags accepting `--email` or `--user-id`, dotenv-loaded pool id + region, `AdminListGroupsForUser` round-trip to verify the mutation reflected) ‚Äî the **only** way to seed the first admin since the UI's group toggle requires admin to call it (cold-start bootstrap problem). **Frontend**: 4 new pages under `/dashboard/admin` ‚Äî `/` Hub Overview with `StatusGrid` tiles (current parameter version + last rotation + pending proposals + admin count + founding members + recent audit), `/users` with email-prefix search + detail panel + four mutation actions (grant/revoke admin, reset password, beta toggle, per-user audit feed), `/audit` with global filterable feed (module + route_prefix dropdowns) + pagination, `/parameters` with read-only current `SignalParameters` table + the relocated `ParameterRollbackSection` (moved from `/dashboard/admin/proposals` ‚Äî proposals page is now review-and-promote only). Server-component pages double-gate via `getDashboardAuthContext()` redirecting `!isAdmin` away to `/dashboard`. **Collapsible Admin sidebar group** in `sidebar.tsx` + `mobile-nav-drawer.tsx` with a new `useAdminNavExpanded` custom hook persisting state in `localStorage` and auto-expanding when the active route starts with `/dashboard/admin`. **Typed clients** under `lib/api/`: `admin-users.ts` (search + detail + reset-password + group add/remove with discriminated `AdminUserMutationOutcome` outcome carrying upstream status + error code), `admin-audit.ts` (`fetchRecentAuditEvents` + `fetchUserAuditEvents` + `statusCodeTone` display helper), `admin-parameters-current.ts`, `admin-system-status.ts`. **9 new BFF routes** under `frontend/app/api/stocvest/admin/*` (verbatim status/body/content-type pass-through on top of `stocvestAuthedFetch`; the missing `beta-access` BFF was also added so the existing `PATCH /v1/admin/users/{user_id}/beta-access` is reachable from the new users page without a curl invocation). **`isDashboardNavItemActive`** updated so `/dashboard/admin` (the hub root) uses exact-match for active highlighting, preventing `/dashboard/admin/users` from highlighting both the parent and the child ‚Äî mirrors the existing exact-match special case for `/dashboard` itself. Prior ‚Äî **Automated weight-tuning proposal pipeline ‚Äî post-rotation accuracy alarm + admin rollback (D10 Phase 4)** ‚Äî closes the human-in-the-loop weight tuning loop with the operational safety net that motivates the whole D10 project. **Daily-scheduled `weight_rotation_monitor` Lambda** computes the trailing-14-day directional accuracy for the live `parameter_version` AND the second-most-recent row in `ParameterHistory` (the previously-live version), via the existing `HistoricalValidationService` so the numbers never drift from `/performance`. The pure-function core in **new `stocvest/api/services/post_rotation_monitor.py`** handles sample-size guards (`MIN_RESOLVED_SAMPLE=30` per side) and a closed-set status discriminator (`ok` / `degraded` / `insufficient_sample` / `baseline_unavailable`). Lambda publishes one custom CloudWatch metric per run: `Stocvest/Signals/PostRotationAccuracyDelta` with `Status` + `Environment` dimensions, value = `current_pct - baseline_pct` in raw pp. **Terraform CloudWatch alarm** in `infra/lambda_weight_rotation_monitor.tf` fires only when `Status="degraded"` AND value ‚â§ `-weight_rotation_degradation_threshold_pp` (default `-5pp`), publishing to a new SNS topic with optional email subscription via the new `weight_rotation_alert_email` var ‚Äî non-degraded runs publish a 0.0 so dashboards stay continuous but the filter prevents nuisance alarms. **Same three-IAM-principal architecture** as Phase 2b: the monitor Lambda has its own dedicated role with NO `secretsmanager:UpdateSecret` (physically incapable of mutating weights), constrained `cloudwatch:PutMetricData` scoped to the `Stocvest/Signals` namespace via condition key, read-only access to `SignalHistory`, `ParameterHistory`, and the `stocvest/signal-parameters` secret. **Two new admin HTTP routes** under `/v1/admin/parameters/*` (gated on `analysis_authorized()` exactly like the Phase-3a proposal routes): `GET /history?limit=N` returns prior `ParameterHistory` rows newest-first with `is_current_live_version` flagged per row so the picker UI can disable no-op rollbacks; `POST /rollback` with body `{target_version}` reconstructs `SignalParameters` from the audit row's `parameters_json` and calls **the same `ParameterStore.save_parameters_sync` primitive** that Phase 3a's promote path uses ‚Äî forward-writing a fresh `ParameterHistory` row whose payload matches the target but with a new monotonic version string (load-bearing: rollback never deletes or rewrites prior history, audit trail stays monotonic). New `stocvest/api/services/parameter_rollback.py` is the orchestration layer; new `stocvest/api/handlers/admin_parameters.py` is the HTTP shell with HTTP error mapping (404 = target version not in history, 409 = already on target = no-op rollback rejected, 500 = secret save failed or audit row corrupt, 400 = missing or non-string `target_version`). `changed_by` audit prefix is **`d10-rollback:<reviewer>`** so audit-log analytics can distinguish a rollback from a forward promotion (which uses `d10-admin:<reviewer>`). **Frontend safety surface**: new `frontend/app/api/stocvest/admin/parameters/{history,rollback}/route.ts` BFF routes proxy verbatim to the upstream Phase-4 backend; new `frontend/lib/api/admin-parameters.ts` typed client mirrors the discriminated-outcome pattern from `admin-proposals.ts` (rollback returns `{kind:"ok"|"error", code, message}` for clean 4xx/5xx UI mapping); new `frontend/components/parameter-rollback-section.tsx` renders a "Parameter rollback" panel on the existing `/dashboard/admin/proposals` page (kept as a separate section file so the 991-line admin proposals client stays untouched except for a one-import + one-element addition). The rollback confirmation dialog explicitly enumerates the **four** production side-effects (new `ParameterHistory` row, ‚â§5-minute engine cache TTL propagation, audit-trail `d10-rollback:` prefix, reversibility via a new promotion or alternate rollback) so the click is never accidental. New `parameter_history_store.py` reader APIs (`list_parameter_history_versions`, `get_parameter_history_version`, `parameters_dict_from_history_row`) are also load-bearing: the original module only exposed `put_parameter_history_version`; rollback needs read access and the lookups are kept best-effort (table unconfigured ‚Üí `[]`/`None`, never raises). D10 is **complete** end-to-end: Phase 1 (data schema) ‚Üí Phase 2a/b (optimizer + scheduled worker) ‚Üí Phase 3a (backend review API) ‚Üí Phase 3b (admin frontend) ‚Üí **Phase 4 (alarm + rollback)**. Previous ‚Äî **Automated weight-tuning proposal pipeline ‚Äî admin review frontend (D10 Phase 3b)** ‚Äî ships the operator-facing half of the human-in-the-loop weight rotation flow first opened by Phase 3a. New `/dashboard/admin/proposals` page sits behind a server-side `isSessionAdmin()` gate that decodes the JWT's `cognito:groups` claim and looks for the `signal-analytics-admin` group; non-admins redirect to `/dashboard`. **The frontend gate mirrors the backend `analysis_authorized()` gate verbatim but the backend is still the real perimeter** ‚Äî every admin BFF call runs through the existing Phase-3a `analysis_authorized()` gate regardless of what the frontend thinks. Four new BFF routes under `frontend/app/api/stocvest/admin/proposals/*` proxy verbatim to the Phase-3a backend (list / get-by-id / promote / reject), preserving HTTP status + content-type so the typed client can surface 403 (non-admin) / 404 (not found) / 409 (proposal not pending) / 500 (secret save failed) envelopes without re-parsing. New typed client `frontend/lib/api/admin-proposals.ts` returns `null` on auth failure for reads and a discriminated `{kind:"ok"|"error", status, code, message, raw}` outcome for the destructive writes so the UI can render calm conflict toasts / error toasts mapped to the upstream's error envelope vocabulary. New `frontend/lib/auth/dashboard-session.ts` (`getDashboardAuthContext() ‚Üí {session, isAdmin}`) is threaded through all 15 dashboard pages so adding a future role is one edit, not 15; `AppShell` / `Sidebar` / `MobileNavDrawer` all gained an optional `isAdmin` prop and the sidebar now renders a divider-separated "Admin" section with the new "Admin ¬∑ Proposals" link (`ShieldCheck` icon) when the server resolves admin=true. The admin UI itself (`frontend/components/admin-proposals-page-client.tsx`) gives the operator status-filter pills (pending / promoted / rejected / superseded), summary-row cards with per-mode val-accuracy lift (green/red tone) + signal counts, a detail panel with `WeightTable` per mode showing the proposed 6-layer weights + thresholds + a Œ£weights running sum + train/val window timestamps + reviewed-by/at/note rows on non-pending proposals + a collapsible `Optimizer evidence` JSON block, an optional rejection-note textarea, and a `PromoteConfirmDialog` modal that **enumerates all four side effects of promotion** (Secrets Manager rotation, `ParameterHistory` row append, proposal-status flip, sibling auto-supersede) before the destructive "Yes, rotate weights" button fires. Successful promotion surfaces a tinted flash toast carrying the new parameter version + count of auto-superseded siblings; failed promotion surfaces the upstream's error code and message. Test results: **411 passed across 46 files (+69)**, zero new TypeScript errors. No backend code changes, no Terraform, no IAM, no DynamoDB schema changes ‚Äî the admin perimeter is entirely the backend's existing `analysis_authorized()` + the existing `lambda_api_data_access` IAM policy from Phase 3a (which already had `secretsmanager:UpdateSecret` for `stocvest/signal-parameters*`). The Phase-2b scheduled worker Lambda remains intentionally read-only on the secret ‚Äî promote is **physically impossible** to trigger from anywhere except these new admin routes. Previous ‚Äî **Automated weight-tuning proposal pipeline ‚Äî scheduled worker (D10 Phase 2b)** ‚Äî ships the Lambda + IAM + EventBridge that wires the Phase-2a optimizer into a weekly scheduled job. New `stocvest/api/services/weight_proposer.py` orchestrates the full flow (load `SignalParameters` baseline ‚Üí scan `SignalHistory` ‚Üí project per-mode ‚Üí optimize ‚Üí gate ‚Üí write `ParameterProposal` rows). New `stocvest/api/handlers/weight_proposer.py` is the Lambda entry point; new `weight_proposer` module branch added to `stocvest/api/lambda_dispatch.py`. **Per-mode error isolation** is load-bearing: a failure in swing's optimizer does not block day from completing ‚Äî each mode produces its own `ModeRunOutcome` with explicit `error`/`acceptance`/`proposal_id` fields. Terraform `infra/lambda_weight_proposer.tf` creates a **dedicated** Lambda function with its OWN minimal-privilege IAM role (NOT the shared `lambda_api_execution` role). The new `lambda_weight_proposer_execution` role gets DDB read on `SignalHistory`, DDB write on `ParameterProposal`, and Secrets Manager **READ-ONLY** on `stocvest/signal-parameters*` ‚Äî explicitly NO `secretsmanager:UpdateSecret`, NO `PutSecretValue`, NO `CreateSecret`, NO `DeleteSecret`. The optimizer Lambda is physically incapable of mutating production weights ‚Äî that's the load-bearing safety property of the three-IAM-principal D10 architecture. EventBridge cron `cron(0 8 ? * MON *)` (Monday 08:00 UTC = ~03:00-04:00 ET, before US market open, after Friday close + 1d outcome resolution). Lambda timeout 300s / memory 512MB. **Still ships dark in production behavior:** the Lambda will write proposals to DDB, but until Phase 3's admin BFF + UI is shipped, no path exists to promote those proposals into the live secret ‚Äî so the running engines continue using the operator-rotated weights from Secrets Manager exactly as today. Previous ‚Äî **Automated weight-tuning proposal pipeline ‚Äî algorithmic core (D10 Phase 2a)** ‚Äî ships the **pure-function walk-forward grid-search optimizer** that scores candidate composite-weight rotations against the historical signal record. Phase 2a is **algorithm-only** ‚Äî no AWS, no IO, no Lambda ‚Äî so the math is testable in isolation and the production code path is still untouched (every existing engine call still uses Secrets-Manager-loaded weights as before). The optimizer takes a chronologically-sorted list of resolved `SignalRecord` rows for one mode and replays the production `CompositeScoreEngine` against each row's stored layer scores with each candidate weight set, comparing the resulting verdict to the actual ¬±0.1% price direction over the resolution horizon (same threshold the live `outcome_from_prices` uses ‚Äî pinned via a cross-module equivalence test). Candidates are generated as a constrained ¬±delta neighborhood around baseline (3^6 = 729 raw ‚Üí filtered + normalized + deduped, ‚â§729 actual); the best-by-val-accuracy candidate is then run through a three-gate acceptance check (val accuracy lift ‚â• +2pp, val signal count ‚â• 30, train/val regime distribution within 20% per regime) before being eligible for proposal. **What's deliberately NOT in scope for Phase 2a:** verdict thresholds aren't rotated (only the six layer weights; thresholds affect gating, not just scoring ‚Äî different change profile); cross-mode weight transfer isn't attempted (swing/day optimize independently ‚Äî that's the entire point of B30 Phase 3's per-mode override blocks); multi-objective optimization is deferred (directional accuracy only ‚Äî Goodhart's law applies, which is why the human-in-the-loop gate exists). **Lossy reconstruction caveat documented:** per-layer confidence isn't persisted on `SignalRecord` rows, so the optimizer reconstructs `LayerSignal` with `confidence=1.0` ‚Äî this is a symmetric assumption across all candidates, so the *relative* ranking is preserved even though absolute val accuracies will differ from what the live engine produced at signal time. Phase 2b (next) wires this core into a scheduled Lambda + Terraform infrastructure (IAM role with NO `secretsmanager:UpdateSecret`, EventBridge weekly schedule, proposal writes via `ParameterProposalStore`). Previous ‚Äî **Automated weight-tuning proposal pipeline ‚Äî foundation (D10 Phase 1)** ‚Äî ships the data-layer foundation for proposal-only weight tuning. Phase 1 ships **dark, zero production behavior change** ‚Äî the table exists and the repo can read/write/transition, but nothing in production calls it yet. The pipeline architecture is **three-IAM-principal**: optimizer Lambda role (Phase 2 ‚Äî writes proposals, NO `secretsmanager:UpdateSecret` IAM); admin endpoint role (Phase 3 ‚Äî reads proposals + writes secrets after admin auth); read-path Lambda roles (existing ‚Äî read-only on secrets). This separation is the load-bearing safety property ‚Äî the optimizer can run unattended, but every rotation requires an admin to explicitly approve from the proposal review UI. **Why proposal-only, not full auto-tune:** 12-dim search space (6 layers √ó 2 modes) with ~150-300 resolved signals per mode = textbook overfitting risk on trailing 60-day data; regime-tied optimization (a bull-market-trained weight set silently underweights geo/internals layers, then fails when the regime flips); Goodhart's law (directional accuracy is one metric ‚Äî optimizing for it degrades expectancy after drawdown, alpha decay in compressed regimes); cascading dependencies (composite weights interact with confluence + suppression gates in ways the optimizer doesn't see); loss of explainability (an optimizer-produced weight set with no narrative is impossible to defend in a postmortem). **Why Secrets Manager remains the live store:** weights aren't a security secret (an attacker who knew them gains ~nothing ‚Äî engine logic + per-symbol data produces the signal, not the weights), but Secrets Manager gives us KMS encryption + IAM-policy-gated writes + CloudTrail audit log + atomic version bumps ‚Äî properties we want for **operational integrity** (preventing accidental rotation, preserving an audit trail, gating who can write). **Phase 1 shipped:** (1) **Terraform** ‚Äî new DDB table `ParameterProposal` in `infra/dynamodb.tf` with `proposal_id` PK + `status_index` GSI (`status` PK + `created_at` SK so the admin UI can list pending sorted by date without scanning) + TTL enabled on `ttl` attribute. Rejected/superseded rows auto-expire after 90 days; promoted rows have NO TTL (they're the audit trail of approvals and must persist alongside `ParameterHistory`). Lambda env in `infra/lambda_6e.tf` gains `DYNAMODB_PARAMETER_PROPOSAL_TABLE` and the new ARN is added to `lambda_dynamodb_resources` flatten. `terraform validate` passes clean. (2) **Settings** ‚Äî `stocvest/utils/config.py` gains `dynamodb_parameter_proposal_table: str = Field("", alias="DYNAMODB_PARAMETER_PROPOSAL_TABLE")` next to the existing `dynamodb_parameter_history_table`. (3) **Repo module** ‚Äî new `stocvest/data/parameter_proposal_store.py`: `ParameterProposal` dataclass with closed-set status values (`PROPOSAL_STATUS_PENDING` / `_PROMOTED` / `_REJECTED` / `_SUPERSEDED` + `PROPOSAL_STATUS_VALUES` tuple). `new_pending` factory validates at least one per-mode override block is set ‚Äî a proposal with neither swing nor day overrides carries no actionable information and would just clutter the pending queue. `to_item`/`from_item` round-trip with JSON-encoded nested fields (`evidence`, `proposed_swing_composite`, `proposed_day_composite`) ‚Äî sidesteps boto3's Decimal coercion + audit-friendly when an operator reads the row in the AWS console. `ParameterProposalStore` class with injected `table` for testability: `put` (idempotent for EventBridge retry-safety), `get` (returns None for missing), `list_by_status` (closed-set status validation, DESC by `created_at` via the GSI, asserts the right GSI name is queried), `mark_promoted` / `mark_rejected` / `mark_superseded` with **atomic DDB `ConditionalCheckExpression` on the `status` attribute** ‚Äî load-bearing guarantee that a rejected proposal cannot be silently re-promoted by a racing admin click. `mark_rejected` and `mark_superseded` stamp a TTL ~90 days out; `mark_promoted` deliberately does NOT (audit trail). `build_default_proposal_store` for production wiring (raises ValueError on missing table env var since Phase 1 ships dark ‚Äî no production paths should invoke it yet). (4) **Tests: +24 lock-ins** in new `tests/data/test_parameter_proposal_store.py` (uses an in-process `_FakeTable` that implements `put_item` / `get_item` / `query` / `update_item` with realistic semantics including `ConditionalCheckFailedException`): factory invariants (`test_new_pending_requires_at_least_one_per_mode_block`, `test_new_pending_accepts_swing_only_proposal`, `test_new_pending_accepts_day_only_proposal`, `test_new_pending_auto_generates_id_and_timestamp`), round-trip serialization (`test_to_item_round_trip_preserves_every_field`, `test_to_item_omits_optional_fields_when_unset`, `test_to_item_encodes_nested_dicts_as_json_strings`, `test_from_item_tolerates_raw_dict_in_nested_fields`), CRUD (`test_put_then_get_returns_equivalent_proposal`, `test_get_returns_none_for_missing_id`, `test_put_is_idempotent_for_same_id`), GSI semantics (`test_list_by_status_returns_desc_by_created_at`, `test_list_by_status_filters_by_status`, `test_list_by_status_rejects_invalid_status_loud`, `test_list_by_status_honors_limit`), transitions + atomicity (`test_mark_promoted_transitions_pending_to_promoted` ‚Äî verifies promoted rows have NO TTL, `test_mark_rejected_transitions_pending_to_rejected_with_ttl` ‚Äî verifies TTL ‚âà +90 days, `test_mark_superseded_transitions_pending_to_superseded_with_pointer`, `test_cannot_promote_already_promoted_proposal`, `test_cannot_reject_already_rejected_proposal`, `test_cannot_promote_rejected_proposal` ‚Äî the load-bearing atomicity guarantee, `test_cannot_transition_missing_proposal`), closed-set invariants (`test_proposal_status_values_closed_set`, `test_proposal_ttl_days_documented_invariant`). Backend baseline **1093 ‚Üí 1117 passed** (+24, zero regressions). No Terraform / IAM / API contract / DynamoDB-schema changes that affect existing production paths ‚Äî the new table + IAM grant are purely additive. **Phases 2-4 deferred** to subsequent commits: Phase 2 = weekly optimizer Lambda + walk-forward CV + grid search + EventBridge schedule; Phase 3 = admin BFF + minimal admin UI for proposal review + promote/reject endpoints + admin role gating; Phase 4 = CloudWatch alarm on post-rotation accuracy degradation + one-click rollback. Previous shipment ‚Äî **Gap-card mode-fit classifier + per-row Evidence routing (B30 Phase 4)** ‚Äî closes the last three B30 Severity-2 items in one shipment: (1) `scannerSetupMode === "both"` gap-card default routing, (2) "Best evaluated as: swing / day / either" advisory tag on gap cards, (3) per-row classifier-driven engine selection (no longer mirrors `panelNewsTradingMode` blindly). **The problem before Phase 4:** in `Both` view every gap card opened the swing engine (the `resolveEvidenceTradingMode("both") === "swing"` collapse rule from B30 Phase 2), regardless of whether the gap's character pointed to a swing-engine question (5% earnings gap with high narrative score ‚Äî classic continuation play) or a day-engine question (2.5% gap with no catalyst and 3√ó volume ‚Äî classic intraday tape play). The user reading the Evidence modal saw the swing engine's verdict on a gap the day engine should have answered. **Fix is a classifier seam + per-row routing:** (1) **Backend classifier** ‚Äî new public `classify_mode_best_fit(*, gap_pct, volume_vs_avg, has_catalyst, catalyst_category, catalyst_narrative_score) -> tuple[str, list[str]]` in `stocvest/signals/gap_intelligence.py` counts swing-tilt signals (`structural catalyst (earnings|merger|insider)`, `large gap (‚â•3%)`, `high-conviction catalyst (narrative ‚â•60)`) vs day-tilt signals (`heavy volume (‚â•2√ó avg)`, `tradable intraday range ([1.5%, 5%))`, `momentum gap (no fundamental anchor)` OR `tape-level catalyst (macro|analyst)`). Decision rule: margin ‚â•2 picks the winner; anything closer (including the symmetric 2-vs-1, 1-vs-2 case) returns `"either"`. Returns reasoning chips so the verdict is auditable. Closed-set return values pinned as module-level constant `MODE_BEST_FIT_VALUES = ("swing", "day", "either")`. (2) **Backend wire-up** ‚Äî `build_gap_intelligence_items` now stamps every row with `mode_best_fit: "swing" \| "day" \| "either"` + `mode_best_fit_reasons: list[str]`. The fields are added at the bottom of the row dict so older clients ignore them gracefully (back-compat). (3) **Frontend type + helper** ‚Äî `GapIntelligenceItem` in `frontend/lib/api/scanner.ts` gained optional `mode_best_fit?: GapModeBestFit` + `mode_best_fit_reasons?: string[]` (optional because cached pre-Phase-4 responses don't carry them). New exported type `GapModeBestFit = "swing" \| "day" \| "either"`. New `resolveGapCardTradingMode(scannerSetupMode, modeBestFit)` helper in `frontend/lib/scanner-mode-resolution.ts` is the single source of truth for the per-row routing rule: explicit scanner mode (`"swing"` / `"day"`) ALWAYS wins; `"both"` view honors the classifier verdict; `"either"` or undefined verdict in `"both"` view falls back to swing (preserves the pre-Phase-4 default). (4) **Frontend wire-up** ‚Äî `openGapEvidence` in `scanner-page-client.tsx` line 891-924 now computes `gapCardMode = resolveGapCardTradingMode(scannerSetupMode, item.mode_best_fit)` once at the top of the callback and threads it into `enrichEvidenceWithComposite(base, gapCardMode)`. `evidenceTradingMode` is no longer a dependency of the callback ‚Äî `scannerSetupMode` is the new dep, since the per-row mode is derived from it + the row's `mode_best_fit`. (5) **Tag rendering** ‚Äî gap cards now render a "Best evaluated as: Swing (multi-day) / Day (intraday) / Either desk" pill between the catalyst block and the action-button row, with role-colored background tint (swing ‚Üí accent blue, day ‚Üí caution amber, either ‚Üí neutral muted) and a 1px solid border in the role color. Underneath, the reasoning chips render as a single muted line joined by middle-dots so the verdict is transparent. An `InfoTip` next to the pill explains the routing rule: when the user is in explicit `"swing"` / `"day"` scanner mode, the tooltip clarifies that the explicit mode overrides the verdict; when the user is in `"both"` mode and the verdict drives routing, the tooltip says "View Signal opens this engine"; when the verdict is `"either"` in `"both"` mode, the tooltip explains it falls back to swing and suggests switching to Day mode to evaluate the gap with the day engine instead. The pill is HIDDEN when `item.mode_best_fit` is `undefined` (cached pre-Phase-4 response) ‚Äî no guess shown. **Tests: +13 backend + +6 frontend lock-ins, zero regressions.** Backend (`tests/signals/test_gap_intelligence.py`): `test_mode_best_fit_returns_closed_set_value` (defensive: every input combo resolves to a valid value), `test_mode_best_fit_earnings_catalyst_with_large_gap_picks_swing` (3 swing signals fire + day chips DO NOT leak into reasoning), `test_mode_best_fit_merger_catalyst_is_structural_swing`, `test_mode_best_fit_insider_catalyst_is_structural_swing`, `test_mode_best_fit_no_catalyst_with_heavy_volume_picks_day` (3 day signals + swing chips DO NOT leak), `test_mode_best_fit_macro_catalyst_with_heavy_volume_picks_day` (tape-level catalyst classification), `test_mode_best_fit_analyst_catalyst_with_heavy_volume_picks_day` (symmetric), `test_mode_best_fit_balanced_signals_returns_either` (1-vs-1 ‚Üí either, reasons concat both sides), `test_mode_best_fit_margin_below_two_returns_either` (2-vs-1 still either ‚Äî margin-2 rule), `test_mode_best_fit_unknown_catalyst_category_does_not_score_as_structural` (only earnings/merger/insider count as structural), `test_mode_best_fit_quiet_market_micro_gap_returns_either` (0-vs-0 default), `test_mode_best_fit_negative_gap_uses_absolute_magnitude` (gap-down treated symmetrically), `test_mode_best_fit_huge_gap_no_volume_still_swing` (9% earnings gap with 1.1√ó vol still swing ‚Äî magnitude alone doesn't flip to day), `test_mode_best_fit_in_build_gap_intelligence_items` (end-to-end wire-up: the new fields are present on the row dict and a 5% gap surfaces a `large gap` chip in `mode_best_fit_reasons`). Frontend (`frontend/tests/scanner-mode-resolution.test.ts`): `explicit scannerSetupMode 'day' wins regardless of classifier verdict` (4-way: swing/day/either/undefined verdict all collapse to `"day"`), `explicit scannerSetupMode 'swing' wins regardless of classifier verdict` (symmetric), `'both' view honors classifier 'swing' verdict`, `'both' view honors classifier 'day' verdict (cross-engine routing)` (the load-bearing branch ‚Äî without it, the day verdict would be cosmetic and every gap card on `"both"` view would still open swing), `'both' view with 'either' verdict falls back to swing`, `'both' view with undefined verdict (legacy / cached response) falls back to swing` (back-compat for the cache TTL window during deploy). Backend baseline **1079 ‚Üí 1093 passed** (+14, zero regressions). Frontend baseline **336 ‚Üí 342 passed** (+6, zero regressions). **B30 Severity-2 status: all three product-decision items now CLOSED.** No Terraform / IAM / API contract / DynamoDB-schema changes ‚Äî the `/v1/scanner/gap-intelligence` response gained two optional fields (additive). The classifier is intentionally heuristic + small ‚Äî it could grow more sophistication later (e.g. premarket volume ratio vs full-day volume vs avg, relative-to-ATR check, options activity confirmation) but the current 6-signal/3-each design is the right starting point: it covers the canonical patterns, every signal has plain-English reasoning, and the margin-2 rule preserves `"either"` for legitimately ambiguous gaps so the classifier never over-claims. Previous shipment ‚Äî **Per-mode composite weight overrides (B30 Phase 3 ‚Äî Suggestion 4 audit)** ‚Äî closes the Severity-2 audit item from B30 ("Audit whether layer weights themselves should differ between engines ‚Äî today both share `CompositeParameters`"). Audit finding: both the swing engine (`stocvest/api/services/swing_composite_engine.py`) and the day engine (`stocvest/api/services/real_composite_engine.py`) ‚Äî plus the legacy client-supplied-scores swing handler (`stocvest/api/handlers/signals.py:301-340`) ‚Äî read the **same** `params.composite` block (tech 0.30 / news 0.20 / macro 0.15 / sector 0.15 / geo 0.10 / internals 0.10). The per-layer **inputs** already diverge by mode (swing reads 120h news / 14d macro / 168h geo / weekly sector / daily-bar tech with `mode="swing"`; day reads 8h news / 1d macro / 8h geo / daily sector / intraday tech with `mode="day"`) but the **blend weights** stamped on every `SignalRecord.parameter_version` are identical, which is a known asymmetry: macro and sector deserve more weight for swing (multi-day holds carry through Fed days and sector rotation), while technical / internals / news deserve more weight for day (intraday confirmation IS the day-engine's primary truth and fresh 8h news has not yet absorbed). **Proposed rotation** (recorded in `docs/BACKLOG.md` row B30 Phase 3 with reasoning, NOT shipped as the default ‚Äî operators rotate in Secrets Manager when ready): swing tech 0.28 / news 0.15 / macro 0.20 / sector 0.18 / geo 0.12 / internals 0.07; day tech 0.32 / news 0.25 / macro 0.10 / sector 0.12 / geo 0.08 / internals 0.13. Verdict thresholds (`bullish_threshold=+0.20` / `bearish_threshold=-0.20`) and confluence parameters intentionally NOT in scope ‚Äî those are higher-stakes product-decision dials and ride a separate audit cycle. **Implementation is additive infrastructure only ‚Äî zero production behavior change today.** (1) Schema: `stocvest/config/signal_parameters.py` `SignalParameters` gained two optional override fields `swing_composite: CompositeParameters | None = None` and `day_composite: CompositeParameters | None = None`. Both default to `None` so any Secrets Manager JSON without `swing_composite` / `day_composite` keys (i.e. every existing secret today) leaves the per-mode blocks unset and the engine falls back to the shared `composite` block ‚Äî the **load-bearing back-compat invariant**. The dataclass field docstring explicitly documents this seam + the operator-rotation flow + the resolver function that consumes the fields. (2) Parser: `signal_parameters_from_dict` in `stocvest/config/parameter_store.py` now parses `data["swing_composite"]` / `data["day_composite"]` via the new `_parse_optional_composite_block` helper, which returns `None` for absent / null / non-dict values (defensive) and a fully-coerced `CompositeParameters` for dict values (unknown keys ignored per the existing `_coerce_dataclass` contract ‚Äî forward-compat). (3) Resolver: new public `resolve_composite_block(params, mode)` in `stocvest/signals/composite_score.py` is the single source of truth for mode-aware composite parameter selection ‚Äî if `mode == "swing"` and `params.swing_composite is not None` return it, else if `mode == "day"` and `params.day_composite is not None` return it, else return `params.composite`. Exported from `stocvest.signals.__init__`. Unknown mode strings (`"options"`, `""`, case-mismatched `"SWING"`) fall through to the shared block defensively. (4) Builder: `build_composite_score_engine_from_params(params, *, mode=None)` gained a keyword-only `mode` argument that threads through the resolver. `mode=None` preserves the legacy back-compat path (always returns the shared block) so any caller that forgets the kwarg still gets the previous behavior verbatim. (5) Call-site wiring: all three production callsites now declare their mode explicitly ‚Äî `swing_composite_engine.py` line 251 + 261 + 262 use `resolve_composite_block(params, mode="swing")` for `min_available_layers` / `bullish_threshold` / `bearish_threshold` and pass `mode="swing"` to the builder; `real_composite_engine.py` line 335 + 366 + 367 use `mode="day"` symmetrically; `signals.py:339` (the legacy `swing_composite_handler` client-supplied-scores path) passes `mode="swing"` to the builder. The local variable `swing_composite` / `day_composite` is bound once per request so the engine and the threshold check are guaranteed to be derived from the same resolved block (closes the operator-rotates-secret-between-two-reads race as a bonus, same pattern as the D3 first slice). **Tests: +18 backend lock-ins, zero regressions.** **+11 in `tests/signals/test_composite_score.py`** under a new "B30 Phase 3 ‚Äî per-mode composite override blocks" section covering: (a) `test_resolve_composite_block_falls_back_to_shared_when_no_per_mode_block` ‚Äî pins the no-op default contract for all three mode values (swing / day / None) against a fresh `default_signal_parameters()` whose override fields are both `None`; (b) `test_resolve_composite_block_returns_swing_block_when_set` ‚Äî when only `swing_composite` is set, `mode="swing"` returns the override, `mode="day"` falls back to shared, `mode=None` falls back to shared (cross-mode isolation); (c) `test_resolve_composite_block_returns_day_block_when_set` ‚Äî symmetric; (d) `test_resolve_composite_block_handles_both_overrides_independently` ‚Äî both blocks set, each mode picks its own; (e) `test_resolve_composite_block_ignores_unknown_mode` ‚Äî defensive case-sensitive lock for `"options"` / `""` / `"SWING"` all falling through to shared; (f) `test_build_engine_swing_and_day_identical_when_no_override` ‚Äî end-to-end no-op default lock (with shared block only, both modes build engines with identical `_base_weights` + thresholds ‚Äî this is the **production behavior guarantee** until operators rotate); (g) `test_build_engine_swing_mode_uses_swing_override_weights` ‚Äî verifies all six weights + both thresholds flow through the builder from the swing override; (h) `test_build_engine_day_mode_uses_day_override_weights` ‚Äî symmetric; (i) `test_build_engine_swing_mode_does_not_pick_up_day_override` ‚Äî cross-mode isolation at the builder layer (closes the regression where someone refactors the resolver to look at both blocks); (j) `test_build_engine_day_mode_does_not_pick_up_swing_override` ‚Äî symmetric; (k) `test_per_mode_overrides_actually_change_composite_score` ‚Äî wire-is-live end-to-end test: rotate swing override to heavily-bullish-technical / low-news, swing engine score moves significantly while day engine score (no override) stays anchored to the shared baseline. **+7 in `tests/config/test_parameter_store.py`** under a new "B30 Phase 3" section covering: (a) `test_signal_parameters_from_dict_legacy_secret_has_no_per_mode_blocks` ‚Äî pins the back-compat contract that existing Secrets Manager JSON (no `swing_composite` / `day_composite` keys) parses with both override fields `None`; (b) `test_signal_parameters_from_dict_with_swing_composite_block` ‚Äî new JSON with a `swing_composite` dict parses into a `CompositeParameters` instance with all six weights + thresholds; (c) `test_signal_parameters_from_dict_with_day_composite_block` ‚Äî symmetric; (d) `test_signal_parameters_from_dict_with_both_per_mode_blocks` ‚Äî both blocks coexist; (e) `test_signal_parameters_from_dict_per_mode_null_explicit` ‚Äî JSON-`null` parses as `None` (defensive); (f) `test_signal_parameters_from_dict_per_mode_unknown_keys_ignored` ‚Äî forward-compat for fields we don't know yet; (g) `test_signal_parameters_to_dict_round_trip_with_per_mode_blocks` ‚Äî serialize ‚Üí parse round-trip preserves both override blocks. Backend baseline **1061 ‚Üí 1079 passed** (+18, zero regressions). Frontend baseline **336** unchanged (no frontend changes ‚Äî backend infrastructure only). No Terraform / IAM / API contract / DynamoDB-schema changes ‚Äî `Secrets Manager` `stocvest/signal-parameters` payload schema is forward-compatible (the new optional keys are additive). **Operator runbook for actually rotating weights when ready:** edit `Secrets Manager` `stocvest/signal-parameters`, add a `swing_composite` and/or `day_composite` object to the JSON payload with the proposed weights below, bump `version`, and `ParameterStore.invalidate_cache()` (or wait `CACHE_TTL_SECONDS = 300`). All visual hardening additive in terms of contracts; previous shipment ‚Äî **Signal card explanation refinements (B29 Phase 1)** ‚Äî closes four user-reported clarity / data-trust issues on the Evidence card surfaced by the GOOGL screenshot review. (1) **VWAP sanity guard:** `stocvest/signals/technical_analyzer.py` now wraps `_calculate_vwap` with a `_vwap_is_plausible(vwap, price)` defensive guard ‚Äî when the computed intraday VWAP deviates from the latest close by more than `_VWAP_PRICE_DEVIATION_MAX_PCT = 0.30` (30%), the analyzer drops the value, logs a single-line `vwap_anomaly_suppressed` WARNING (carrying `symbol`, `computed`, `price`, `bars`, `max_deviation_pct` for triage), and the UI falls back to the existing "VWAP Forming" chip + tooltip. This protects users from misleading numbers like the reported `VWAP $28.77` on a stock trading near $389 while we triage the underlying upstream cause (mis-aligned bars cache, unadjusted prices crossing a corporate action, etc.). (2) **Verdict-tag reconciler:** new `buildVerdictTagReconciler(direction, confirming, conflicting, geopoliticalDragActive)` helper in `frontend/lib/signal-evidence.ts` produces a single calm sentence under the Confirming Signals chip group when the composite verdict polarity disagrees with the chip polarity ‚Äî e.g. a long setup whose composite resolves bearish surfaces "Bullish inputs present, but overridden by VWAP conflict + Weak Volume + geopolitical drag." Parenthetical chip detail (`(0.42√ó avg)`) is stripped from the reconciler so the sentence reads cleanly; precision is preserved on the chip itself. The helper is symmetric (bullish verdict + bearish-conflicting chips also renders) and returns `null` for the neutral verdict or when no dissonance exists. Rendered under the chip group with `data-testid="verdict-tag-reconciler"`. (3) **Geopolitical drag badge:** when `evidence.layers` includes a geopolitical layer with `geoHasLiveEvents === true` AND `exposureBand !== "low"`, the Evidence card now renders a bearish-tinted `GEOPOLITICAL DRAG` pill in the verdict hero row (next to `NOT INVESTMENT ADVICE`), tying high-tier headline risk back to the composite verdict visually instead of leaving it stranded inside the geopolitical layer card. Pill carries `data-testid="geopolitical-drag-badge"`. The reconciler also auto-appends "geopolitical drag" to the override list when the badge is active and "geopolit" is not already present. (4) **Weak/Strong Volume precision:** new `_format_rel_vol(ratio)` helper in `stocvest/signals/confluence.py` replaces the lossy `:.1f` format on the volume confluence chips ‚Äî ratios in `[0.05, +‚àû)` now render with two-decimal precision (`0.42√ó`, `1.83√ó`), the `(0, 0.05)` sliver floors to `<0.05√ó` so labels never collapse to a misleading `0.0x avg`, and the multiplication sign `√ó` replaces the ASCII `x` everywhere so the label is visually distinct from a stray letter. Mirrors a real user-reported case where `0.04` volume ratio rendered as `0.0x avg` and triggered doubt. Previous shipment ‚Äî **Assistant on-card CTA routing rule (B28 Phase 2c follow-up)** ‚Äî closes a user-reported chatbot UX regression. The user was on the scanner page looking at the GOOGL Gap Intelligence card (which has an inline "View Signal" button that opens the Evidence modal in place) and asked the chatbot "can you explain what googl card is saying". The chatbot's response was structurally wrong: "I can't see the GOOGL card details from the scanner view... To see GOOGL's complete analysis, click into the symbol on the Signals page." This routed the user off the page they were already on and asked them to re-find the symbol on a different surface, when the card right in front of them already had a button that does exactly the thing they were asking for. **Fix is prompt-side, no code-side changes:** added a new `ON-CARD CTAs ‚Äî REFER USERS TO THE BUTTON ON THE CARD THEY'RE LOOKING AT` sub-section inside CONTEXTUAL MODE RULES in `stocvest/signals/assistant_prompts.py`. The section enumerates a per-surface CTA map (Scanner Gap Intelligence ‚Üí "View Signal", Scanner setup card ‚Üí "View Evidence" + "Open Signals", Dashboard Swing Desk row ‚Üí "View Evidence", Dashboard Day Desk row ‚Üí "Open Day Signals ‚Üí", Performance ledger ‚Üí "Open full ledger (Swing / Day) ‚Üí", Signals page ‚Üí no referral needed because the full Evidence card is already rendered) with each button label quoted verbatim so the LLM can reference the exact on-screen wording the user can scan for. The section ends with a CRITICAL one-line restatement: "when the page context indicates a multi-symbol overview (scanner, dashboard) and the user asks for a deeper read on one symbol on that page, the next step is the on-card CTA ‚Äî NOT a navigation instruction. Do not say 'click into the symbol on the Signals page' or 'go to the Signals page and enter the symbol'. The symbol is already on the card the user is asking about; the card has the button." The fix also adds two new GOOD example responses (scanner-page user asking about a GOOGL gap card; dashboard Swing Desk user asking why a row is in Monitor only) and pins the exact failed production response shape as a BAD example with a parenthetical explanation tying the failure to the rule, plus a GOOD counterpart with the correct **View Signal** verbatim button label. **Tests:** +4 backend lock-ins in `tests/signals/test_assistant_prompts.py` covering (1) the section header + behavioral rule + critical one-line restatement; (2) the per-surface CTA map with verbatim button labels (six surfaces: Gap Intelligence "View Signal", setup card "View Evidence" + "Open Signals", Swing Desk row "View Evidence", Day Desk row "Open Day Signals ‚Üí", Performance "Open full ledger (Swing / Day) ‚Üí"); (3) the banned-shape lock-in for the exact GOOGL scanner regression + the GOOD counterpart that names the on-card **View Signal** button + reassures the user they don't need to leave the page; (4) the Signals-page carve-out (no CTA referral needed because the Evidence card is already rendered) so the LLM doesn't tell a Signals-page user to "click View Evidence" ‚Äî that button on that page just re-renders what they already see. Backend baseline **1051 ‚Üí 1055 passed (+4, zero regressions)**, frontend **301/41 unchanged** (no frontend code touched). `tsc --noEmit` zero new errors. No Terraform / IAM / API contract / DynamoDB-schema changes. The prior 2026-05-12 entry was **Sector behavioral reframe + Signal Validation Ledger moved off dashboard + sub-card highlighted borders (B28 Phase 2c)** ‚Äî closes three concrete user directives layered on top of Phase 2b. (A) **Signal Validation Ledger off the dashboard.** Per the user's one-sentence test "a data element belongs in Shared Context if and only if it answers what kind of market environment are all traders operating in right now," tracked outcomes fail that test (they describe "did past signals work?", not market environment). The `SignalValidationLedgerTertiarySurface` component was removed from `frontend/components/dashboard-redesign.tsx` (the dashboard stack now contains exactly `SharedContextMasterCard` + `Swing Desk` + `DayDeskPanel` + `EarningsCalendar`; nothing about historical outcomes lives anywhere on the dashboard) and the export was deleted from `frontend/components/shared-context-master-card.tsx`. The full stratified ledger surface now lives on the logged-in **Performance page** (`/dashboard/performance`) as a `data-testid="performance-validation-ledger-link"` panel rendered only when `showHomeLink={false}` (i.e. authenticated traffic only ‚Äî the logged-out `/performance` mirror deliberately does NOT render this link surface because the stratified breakdown is gated behind login at the API layer (Phase 3c-1) and the UI now matches that gating). The Performance page panel carries Performance-appropriate framing ("Validation ledger ¬∑ stratified outcomes" eyebrow, "Open full ledger (Swing / Day) ‚Üí" anchor pointing at `/dashboard/signal-validation`, explicit Mode Separation reminder, "tracked outcomes only ‚Äî not a brokerage account" disclaimer). (B) **Sector Rotation behavioral reframe in Shared Context Section C.** Per the user's directive ("If sector rotation explains why the market feels the way it does, it's Shared Context. If it suggests where to put risk, it isn't"), Section C had been showing a per-sector chip row with raw % numbers (XLK +1.5%, XLE -0.6%, XLF +0.4%, ‚Ä¶) ‚Äî a relative-strength ranking explicitly banned ("No % rankings, no bars sorted by performance, no heatmap with winners"). The chip row was deleted entirely; ETF symbol names (XLK / XLC / XLE / XLF / XLY / XLI / XLV / XLP / XLU / XLB / XLRE) no longer appear anywhere inside the Shared Context master card. Section C now renders **two behavioral categorical readouts** instead: (1) **Rotation profile** ("Concentrated" / "Rotational" / "Mixed" / "Unknown") via the new `classifyRotationProfile(sectorPct5d: Array<number | null>)` pure helper ‚Äî Concentrated when spread ‚â• 3.0% AND only 1-2 sectors meaningfully positive (the "narrow leadership" pattern with broad follow-through unlikely), Rotational when mixed signs across sectors AND spread ‚â• 1.5% (capital cycling, no single sector controlling), Mixed for the fallthrough, Unknown for fewer than 3 valid data points; (2) **Participation** category (the existing Broad / Mixed / Narrow / Unknown). Section C is retitled "Sector Participation (Last ~5 Sessions)" (was "Participation / Breadth Tone") ‚Äî time-anchored and behavioral, per the user's exact wording. The `rotationProfilePlainLine` helper produces strictly descriptive sentences ("Narrow leadership ‚Äî a few sectors carrying the move; broad follow-through unlikely", "Capital rotating across sectors ‚Äî no single sector controlling the move; expect inconsistent follow-through", "Mixed sector behavior ‚Äî partial leadership, no dominant pattern") with banned words (trending / leading / bullish / bearish / winners / losers / buy / sell / allocate / should / setup) enforced by tests. (C) **Highlighted borders on the requested cards.** Section A's three index tiles (SPY / QQQ / IWM) now carry **direction-aware highlighted borders**: green at 1.5px when `pct5d > 0.1` (the same threshold the existing `getChangeColor` uses for the % number, so the tile border and the % color are always in lockstep), red when `pct5d < -0.1`, neutral slate at 1.5px otherwise. Each tile also stamps a `data-tile-direction="up" | "down" | "flat" | "unknown"` attribute for stable test selectors. The role-color (slate rail) lives on the master card boundary; the direction-color lives on the inner tiles ‚Äî orthogonal channels by design. New `indexTileBorderForDirection(pct5d, colors)` helper centralizes the threshold + color logic. Sections B / C / D / E each now render inside a `SubsectionCard` wrapper (new internal component) with a 1.5px slate-tinted border + linear-gradient surface + drop-shadow ‚Äî each section reads as a discrete information unit instead of a paragraph in a wall of text. Section A is intentionally NOT wrapped (it already IS a row of three direction-bordered tiles; double-wrapping would create card-in-card-in-card nesting that defeats the at-a-glance scan). Each sub-section also stamps `data-subsection-card="B" | "C" | "D" | "E"` for test selectors. The Swing Desk's **"Primary read" card** (the dominant decision surface when no setups are firing) bumped from `1px solid color-mix(border 72%, transparent)` to `1.5px solid color-mix(roleAccents.swing.borderAccent 65%, border)` ‚Äî picks up the swing role's bright violet `borderAccent` (same hue the master card uses on its rail-line border) plus a linear-gradient surface and a halo shadow, so the Primary read card reads as a structural unit not a paragraph. The card also stamps `data-testid="swing-desk-primary-read-card"` for the lock-in test. **Tests:** Frontend baseline **285 ‚Üí 301 passed (+16)**, zero regressions, no new test file. **In `tests/dashboard-role-color-language.test.tsx`** the failing `section_C_renders_a_participation_CATEGORY_plus_the_sector_chip_row` was rewritten to assert (a) Section C now has BOTH `shared-context-rotation-profile-category` + `shared-context-participation-category` testids, (b) `shared-context-sector-chip-row` is NULL (the chip row removal contract), (c) NO sector ETF NAMES (XLK, XLC, XLE, XLF, XLY, XLI, XLV, XLP, XLU, XLB, XLRE) leak through the section text content (anti-naming-leakage); Think 'rail lines', not soft shadows." Phase 2b consolidates the dashboard to the user's exact specification: ONE Shared Context master card with five strictly-ordered sub-sections (A-E), ONE Swing Desk master card, ONE Day Desk master card, and a tertiary low-prominence Signal Validation Ledger surface below them. Nothing else lives at the same hierarchy level. **(A) ROLE-COLOR LANGUAGE ‚Äî bright rail-line borders.** `frontend/lib/design-system.ts` `RoleAccent` interface gained a third field `borderAccent: string` ‚Äî distinctly BRIGHTER than the surface `accent` so the master-card boundary is visible in peripheral vision without reading any text. Dark theme: shared border `#22d3ee` (electric cyan-steel) over slate surface, swing border `#a78bfa` (bright violet) over indigo surface, day border `#67e8f9` (bright aqua) over teal surface. Together the three edge anchors mean the user can answer "which family am I looking at?" from any peripheral glance without text. **(B) SHARED CONTEXT MASTER CARD.** New file `frontend/components/shared-context-master-card.tsx` (~470 lines) is the single owner of all environmental context the two desks read. It absorbs four previously-separate dashboard cards (Short-Horizon Market State, Market pulse, Sector rotation, Upcoming earnings) and replaces them with five strictly-ordered sub-sections inside ONE master card with header "Shared Context ¬∑ All timeframes ¬∑ used by both desks" and subtitle "Market environment and constraints used by all desks. Not a trade signal." Sub-sections: (A) **Recent Session Market State (Last ~5 Sessions)** ‚Äî three index sub-cards SPY/QQQ/IWM, each with a small inline neutral-stroke SVG sparkline (5 daily closes, no axes, no labels) + net % change number; (B) **Volatility Environment** ‚Äî CATEGORY-ONLY readout ("Contained / Expanding / Compressed / Unknown") derived from VIX level + VIX session %, NO ATR numbers per directive; (C) **Participation / Breadth Tone** ‚Äî CATEGORY-ONLY readout ("Broad / Mixed / Narrow / Unknown") derived from sector rotation + index breadth, with sector chip row as supporting evidence ‚Äî "Broad" requires BOTH ‚â•4-of-5 sectors positive AND ‚â•2-of-3 indices positive (the narrow-leadership-trap anti-leak); (D) **Risk / Event Horizon** ‚Äî TIME-BASED, not directional. Category ("Elevated / Active / Quiet / Unknown") derived from macro warning + upcoming earnings count, with earnings list as supporting detail; (E) **Environment Summary** ‚Äî single human-readable sentence joining A+B+C+D ("Short-horizon price drift up, volatility contained, participation broad, macro risk approaching."), followed by the `SHORT_HORIZON_TIMEFRAME_LINE` + `SHORT_HORIZON_WHY_THIS_MATTERS` guardrail clauses (both still exported from `weekly-market-context-widget.tsx` for back-compat). All four classification functions (`classifyVolatility`, `classifyParticipation`, `classifyRiskHorizon`, `buildEnvironmentSummary`) are exported as pure helpers for direct test coverage. The new file also exports `SignalValidationLedgerTertiarySurface` ‚Äî a low-prominence link surface (no role color, no rail-line border) rendered BELOW the three master cards. Tracked outcomes are neither shared context (market facts) nor a decision engine, so they cannot live inside Shared Context AND cannot be a peer master card; tertiary placement is the honest answer. **(C) SPARKLINES.** New file `frontend/components/index-sparkline.tsx` is a 90-line lightweight SVG component: single `<polyline>` normalized to [0,1] of (min, max) closes, neutral desaturated stroke (`color-mix(in srgb, textMuted 70%, text)`), 80√ó22 default canvas, no axes, no labels, with a `<title>` element for screen-reader accessibility. Flat-session edge case renders the line midway down the canvas ‚Äî never divide-by-zero. The dashboard `WeeklyIndexRow` type gained `closes5d?: number[]` (last 5 daily closes oldest ‚Üí newest) and `dashboard-page-content.tsx`'s `buildWeeklyRows` slices `closes.slice(-5)` from the already-fetched 8-bar daily array ‚Äî no new backend fetches required. **(D) DASHBOARD RESTRUCTURE.** `frontend/components/dashboard-redesign.tsx` lost ~250 lines: the 7fr/13fr grid containing 7 cards collapsed into a clean `<div className="dashboard-stack grid grid-cols-1 gap-7">` containing exactly `<SharedContextMasterCard /> + <DashboardCard role="swing">Swing Desk + <DayDeskPanel /> + <SignalValidationLedgerTertiarySurface /> + <EarningsCalendar />`. The prior 2026-05-11 entry was **Dashboard role-color language + Shared Context copy redesign (B28 Phase 2)** ‚Äî closes the two visual-design regressions the user surfaced after Phase 1 shipped: (a) "the color combination is very confusing" ‚Äî the Swing Desk and Shared Context cards rendered with the same theme-accent surface so the user had to read labels to know which family a card belonged to; (b) the Shared Context card's headline read as evaluative swing-coded language ("Constructive 5-session tape (background)") and the parent card was titled "Weekly market context" ‚Äî both implied swing posture/holding-period intent on a surface that should describe what the market has been doing, not how a trader should trade it. Two intertwined fixes, one commit. **(A) ROLE-COLOR LANGUAGE.** Three orthogonal channels of meaning on the dashboard: (1) PRICE DIRECTION green/red (locked to `colors.bullish` / `colors.bearish`), (2) CAUTION amber (locked to `colors.caution`), (3) **DESK ROLE ‚Äî new third channel ‚Äî slate/indigo/teal** introduced in `frontend/lib/design-system.ts` as `roleAccents: Record<ThemeName, Record<CardRole, RoleAccent>>` with `CardRole = "shared" | "swing" | "day"` and `RoleAccent = { accent, accentStrong, pillLabel }`. Dark theme: shared `#64748b` (slate-500) + label `"SHARED CONTEXT"`; swing `#818cf8` (indigo-400) + label `"SWING ¬∑ MULTI-DAY"`; day `#2dd4bf` (teal-400) + label `"DAY ¬∑ INTRADAY"`. Light theme: slate `#475569`, indigo `#4f46e5`, teal `#0d9488` with the same verbatim pill labels. Teal was deliberately chosen over amber for the Day Desk so desk identity does not visually shout "warning" when posture is calm (amber is already locked to `colors.caution`). Hue families are intentionally distant from `colors.accent` (#3b82f6 / #2563eb) so the global interaction-cue blue cannot be confused with swing identity. **`frontend/components/dashboard-card.tsx`** extended with an optional `role?: CardRole` prop: when set, the card surface gradient leans on the role accent (9% tint into surface instead of the global 7% accent tint), the border picks up a 20% role-accent blend, the shadow halo uses the role accent for its 1px outer ring, a 3px-wide solid stripe is painted along the left edge (`<span data-testid="dashboard-card-role-stripe">`), and a top-anchored uppercase role pill (`<span data-testid="dashboard-card-role-pill" data-card-role-pill={role}>`) renders the verbatim label so screenshots are self-explanatory. The card also stamps `data-card-role={role}` on the wrapping `<article>` for stable test selectors. Omitting `role` preserves the legacy theme-accent surface for non-desk-taxonomy pages (settings, legal, future surfaces). **Role application across the dashboard:** `shared` on Short-Horizon Market State (renamed below), Market pulse, Sector rotation (5 sessions), Upcoming earnings this week, Signal validation ledger ‚Äî five cards now form a single slate-tinted family of shared infrastructure both desks read; `swing` on the Swing Desk card (eyebrow trimmed from "Swing desk ¬∑ Multi-day (evaluated on daily closes)" to "Multi-day ¬∑ evaluated on daily closes" ‚Äî the role pill carries the desk identity, so the eyebrow can shed the redundant "Swing desk" prefix); `day` on the Day Desk panel (eyebrow trimmed from "Day desk ¬∑ Intraday (session-bound)" to "Intraday ¬∑ session-bound" by the same logic). Cards that previously had no explicit `data-testid` (Market pulse, Sector rotation, Upcoming catalysts, Signal validation ledger) gained `data-testid="shared-{market-pulse|sector-rotation|upcoming-catalysts|signal-validation-ledger}-card"` for the new role-attribution tests. **(B) SHARED CONTEXT COPY REDESIGN.** `frontend/components/weekly-market-context-widget.tsx` retitled and rewritten. The parent card's title flips from `"Weekly market context"` ‚Üí **`"Short-Horizon Market State (Last ~5 Sessions)"`** (timeframe-anchored, cadence-neutral ‚Äî the user's directive: "Even though '~5 sessions' ‚âÝ calendar week, the word weekly causes friction"). Subtitle replaced with the verbatim user-supplied: `"Daily-close price behavior across major indices. Shared background input for all desks; not a trade signal."` Eyebrow flips from `"Shared context"` ‚Üí `"Recent Market State"` (the role pill now carries the SHARED CONTEXT label, freeing the eyebrow to carry the OBSERVATIONAL category). The status-line bucket function was renamed `weekTone` ‚Üí `shortHorizonStatusLine` and its three labels were rewritten from evaluative ("Constructive 5-session tape (background)" / "Defensive 5-session tape (background)" / "Mixed 5-session tape (background)") to strictly observational: avg ‚â• +0.6% ‚Üí `"5-Session Outcome: Net upward price progress"`; avg ‚â§ ‚àí0.6% ‚Üí `"5-Session Outcome: Net downward price progress"`; otherwise ‚Üí `"5-Session Outcome: Mixed direction across indices"`. The `(background)` softening suffix is dropped ‚Äî the role pill now carries that disambiguation. Two new verbatim guardrail constants are EXPORTED from the widget so a refactor cannot drop them and tests pin the exact wording: `SHORT_HORIZON_TIMEFRAME_LINE = "Timeframe: Calculated from daily closes over the last ~5 trading sessions. Purpose: Provides background bias only; does not imply trade duration."` and `SHORT_HORIZON_WHY_THIS_MATTERS = "Why this matters: Multi-session price direction influences risk appetite, follow-through probability, and position sizing across all trading horizons."` These two lines render under the index grid as footnote material (`data-testid="short-horizon-guardrails"`) and explicitly disclaim trade-duration intent ‚Äî the single sentence that does the heavy lifting preventing day traders from misreading shared context as swing intent. The status line itself is stamped with `data-testid="short-horizon-status-line"`. The widget root carries `data-testid="short-horizon-market-state"`. The prior 2026-05-11 entry was the four-phase Mode Separation UI compliance shipment described below. **Mode Separation UI compliance shipment (four-phase frontend cleanup)** ‚Äî closes the screen-level violations of the mode-separation safety perimeter that was added to `ASSISTANT_SYSTEM_PROMPT` earlier the same day. The prompt declared the design rule ("Swing trading and Day trading are independent decision engines that share market context but never share decisions, readiness, validation, or activity permission"); this shipment makes the UI obey that rule structurally so the existing screens can no longer regress. Four sequential commits (`e7c9fe0` ‚Üí `122ddc8` ‚Üí `0f31098` ‚Üí `7bf3775`) each addresses one screen-level violation surfaced by the post-prompt audit. **Phase A1 ‚Äî Scanner "Both" split (commit `e7c9fe0`):** `scanner-page-client.tsx` previously merged swing+day setups into a single ranked list sorted by score and sliced to top 10 (`rankedSetups = [...overview.setups].filter(...).sort((a,b) => b.score - a.score).slice(0,10)`), so a day setup with score 0.9 ranked above a swing setup with score 0.7 even though they belong to different engines. The fix partitions by `setup.scanner_mode === "swing_daily"` and renders TWO mode-labelled sections in `both` mode ("Swing setups (daily cadence)" / "Day setups (intraday cadence)"), each top-5, each with its own mode-vocabulary empty-state copy ("No swing setups ‚Äî regime and structure not aligned." / "No day setups ‚Äî intraday confirmation and session timing not aligned."). Single-mode views (`swing` or `day`) keep the existing single-list rendering. The "Open Signals" deep link per row now appends `&trading_mode=${setup.scanner_mode === "swing_daily" ? "swing" : "day"}` so the user lands in the engine they clicked, never the other one's localStorage default. **Phase A2 ‚Äî Signals page mode plumbing (commit `122ddc8`):** previously `tradingMode` was restored from `localStorage` only on mount (URL was not authoritative), `fetchUserEvaluatedSignals({ days: 30 })` was called without `mode` so the past-signal-states history could mix swing and day rows on a single-engine view, and the `signal_id` URL-strip after resolve nuked the entire query string (any `?trading_mode=` query was lost). Fix: (a) `app/dashboard/signals/page.tsx` reads `searchParams.trading_mode` server-side and passes `initialTradingMode: "day" | "swing" | null` on `signalsPrefill`; (b) `signals-page-client.tsx` initialises `tradingMode` state from `initialTradingMode ?? "swing"`, gates the localStorage-restore useEffect so it only runs when the URL did NOT specify a mode (URL beats localStorage), and `updateTradingMode` now mirrors the new mode into the URL via `window.history.replaceState` preserving other query params; (c) `fetchUserEvaluatedSignals({ days: 30, mode: tradingMode })` carries the mode and `tradingMode` is added to the effect deps so engine switches refetch; (d) the signal_id strip preserves `trading_mode` instead of nuking it; (e) `signal-validation-page-client.tsx` ledger-row deep links append `trading_mode=${tab}` (both tabs). **Phase C ‚Äî Historical Validation no-combined-headline (commit `0f31098`):** `historical-validation-panel.tsx` previously defaulted to `mode = "all"` which omitted the mode filter from the API call and rendered a single "Overall directional accuracy" hero card averaging swing+day signals into one number ‚Äî a direct violation of "Statistics, hit-rates, and outcomes must never be combined into a single headline number." Fix narrows `ModeFilter` from `"all" | "swing" | "day"` to `"swing" | "day"` (TypeScript-level guard), `MODE_OPTIONS` becomes `["swing", "day"]`, default mode is `swing` (the first-class engine in product framing), the fetcher always sends a concrete mode, and the hero card title is mode-specific ("Swing directional accuracy (multi-day cadence)" / "Day directional accuracy (intraday cadence)") with a `data-mode` attribute on the accuracy node. Dropdown labels expanded to "Swing (multi-day)" / "Day (intraday)" so the engine attribution is visible even without the cadence label. **Phase D ‚Äî Performance no-combined-headline (commit `7bf3775`):** three surfaces ‚Äî `/performance` dashboard top metric row, the `/performance` 90-day public validation block, and the homepage `landing-performance-section.tsx` ‚Äî each rendered a single combined-engine accuracy number ("Directional Accuracy", "Overall accuracy (1d)", "Overall directional accuracy (resolved 1d)"). Fix: (a) `performance-tracking-content.tsx` top metric row drops the "Directional Accuracy" card (grid shrinks lg:grid-cols-4 ‚Üí lg:grid-cols-3), and `PublicValidationSection` drops the "Overall accuracy (1d)" card (grid shrinks sm:grid-cols-3 ‚Üí sm:grid-cols-2; only "Swing track (1d, multi-day cadence)" + "Day track (1d, intraday cadence)" remain; `overall` is no longer destructured from the validation summary so there is no path that can leak a combined number into the DOM); (b) `landing-performance-section.tsx` removes the fallback "Overall directional accuracy (resolved 1d): X.X% ¬∑ n=Y" line (this was the most promotional violation since it lived on the LOGGED-OUT homepage) and replaces it with a mode-agnostic volume line plus a handoff pointing users at per-engine track records on the Signal Tracking page; the unused `overallPct = summary?.directional_accuracy_percent ?? 0` derivation is dropped. **Lock-in tests (+13 total):** Phase A1 +2 in `tests/scanner-swing-toggle.test.tsx` (two-section render with mode-isolated DOM order + mode-specific empty-state copy), Phase A2 +5 in new `tests/signals-page-mode-plumbing.test.ts` (`fetchUserSignalHistoryPage` forwards `mode=swing` / `mode=day` to URL query; omits mode when caller omits it (legacy contract preserved); `fetchUserEvaluatedSignals` forwards mode to EVERY paginated page request (no mid-pagination swap)), Phase C +2 in new `tests/historical-validation-panel-mode.test.ts` (`MODE_OPTIONS` exposes ONLY `["swing", "day"]`; `ModeFilter` type narrowness via TS-level guard), Phase D +4 in new `tests/performance-no-combined-headline.test.tsx` (`LandingPerformanceSection` does NOT contain "Overall directional accuracy" or "70.0%"; renders the new per-engine handoff line; `PerformanceTrackingContent` top row does NOT include "Directional Accuracy"; `PublicValidationSection` does NOT contain "Overall accuracy" and renders both "Swing track (1d, multi-day cadence)" + "Day track (1d, intraday cadence)" with the per-engine percentages from `by_mode`). Frontend baseline **208 ‚Üí 221 passed (+13, zero regressions)**, backend **1038/3** unchanged (no backend changes). `tsc --noEmit` zero new errors (24 pre-existing). **Explicit non-goals deferred to backlog rows M1 + M2 below:** (1) Dashboard Day Desk ‚Äî `dashboard-redesign.tsx` is intentionally swing-first today (per the comment in `dashboard-page-content.tsx:13-16`); adding a parallel Day Desk with its own posture (Active / Monitor / Suppressed), top day signals, and "what would re-enable" copy is a NEW product surface that requires a product decision + day-engine posture API, not a compliance refactor. (2) Portfolio + Journal mode attribution ‚Äî `portfolio-page-client.tsx` positions and `journal-page-client.tsx` entries have no `strategy_trading_mode` field on the wire today; the journal's `is_day_trade` is a PDT-style flag, not an engine attribution; making either surface honour mode-isolation requires a backend schema change (new column on `JournalEntry` + `Position`, mode-filtering on analytics endpoints, backfill plan for legacy rows), not a frontend cleanup. **Prior commit (2026-05-11) ‚Äî D3 first slice ‚Äî composite-engine parameter wiring closes a real integrity gap** (backend-only, no Terraform, no IAM, no new dependencies, no frontend changes). Three composite-scoring callsites existed: `swing_composite_engine.py` and `real_composite_engine.py` already pulled layer weights + thresholds from `ParameterStore`-loaded `SignalParameters` (correct), but the legacy `swing_composite_handler` in `stocvest/api/handlers/signals.py` ‚Äî the thin `POST /v1/signals/swing/composite` path that accepts client-supplied per-layer scores ‚Äî called `CompositeScoreEngine()` with **no arguments** while still stamping `parameter_version = ParameterStore.get_parameters_sync().version` onto every recorded `SignalRecord`. The metadata claimed "rules vN" but the engine actually computed against the hardcoded `DEFAULT_BASE_WEIGHTS` constants from `composite_score.py`, which differ from `CompositeParameters` defaults on five of six layers (news 0.18 vs 0.20, sector 0.12 vs 0.15, macro 0.16 vs 0.15, geopolitical 0.12 vs 0.10, internals 0.12 vs 0.10). Phase 4's cross-version diff would have surfaced this drift as a phantom "v1 vs v2" delta even when no parameters had actually changed, because the recorded version string was untethered from the weights the engine used. **Fix:** new `build_composite_score_engine_from_params(params)` helper in `stocvest/signals/composite_score.py` is the single source of truth for translating a `SignalParameters` instance into a live `CompositeScoreEngine` (reads `params.composite.{technical|news|macro|sector|geopolitical|internals}_weight` + `bullish_threshold` + `bearish_threshold`, coerces ints to floats for operators editing JSON in Secrets Manager). All three production callsites ‚Äî `swing_composite_handler`, `real_composite_engine.py`, `swing_composite_engine.py` ‚Äî now route through this helper, and `swing_composite_handler` reads `active_params = ParameterStore.get_parameters_sync()` once so the engine and the stamped `parameter_version` are guaranteed to be derived from the same parameter snapshot (closes the operator-rotates-secret-between-two-reads race as a bonus). `DEFAULT_BASE_WEIGHTS` remains in the module as a documented test/no-args fallback so the existing engine-unit tests (`tests/signals/test_composite_score.py`, `test_composite_scorer.py`, `test_risk_factors.py`, `test_risk_reward.py`, etc.) keep working unchanged; the docstring on the helper explicitly states this contract. **Tests:** +6 backend lock-ins. **4 in `tests/signals/test_composite_score.py`** ‚Äî helper produces weights matching `params.composite.*_weight` and explicitly NOT matching `DEFAULT_BASE_WEIGHTS` (regression guard against the drift coming back), helper threads `bullish_threshold` / `bearish_threshold` from params not engine defaults, identical-payload + different `SignalParameters` produces different composite scores end-to-end (the wire-is-live test that would catch any silent fallback to `DEFAULT_BASE_WEIGHTS`), helper coerces integer weights to float so a `technical_weight: 1` in the Secrets Manager JSON cannot crash the engine. **2 in `tests/api/test_signal_recorder.py`** ‚Äî `swing_composite_handler` stamps the same `parameter_version` whose `.composite.*` weights it just used (closes the integrity gap end-to-end by writing a record with `parameter_version="9.9.9-d3-test"` via a custom params monkeypatch and asserting the stored `SignalRecord.parameter_version` matches), identical payload + two different parameter versions through `ParameterStore.get_parameters_sync` produces detectably different `response_body["score"]` values (proves the legacy handler is no longer reading hardcoded `DEFAULT_BASE_WEIGHTS` regardless of `parameter_version`). Backend baseline **1015 ‚Üí 1021 passed (+6, zero regressions)**, frontend **208** unchanged (no frontend code touched). `tsc --noEmit` zero new errors (24 pre-existing). **D3 first slice closes the data integrity contract for the cross-version diff view shipped in Phase 4** ‚Äî operators can now actually rotate `stocvest/signal-parameters` in Secrets Manager and the resulting `SignalRecord` rows will carry an honest `parameter_version` that reflects the actual scoring weights that produced them. **Still pending in D3:** wire the rest of the tunables (technical analyzer thresholds, news lookback hours, macro VIX bands, sector scoring tables, swing-technical SMA periods) through to their respective analyzer constructors; optional Claude prompts in Secrets Manager (P2).
