New handler `historical_validation_summary_handler` in `stocvest/api/handlers/signals.py` requires `rc.user_id` (every query is scoped to the calling user, so one tenant cannot read another tenant's tracked outcomes ‚Äî locked in by `test_scope_isolates_users`) and parses five query parameters: `horizon` ‚àà `{"1h","1d"}` (required), `from` / `to` as ISO-8601 datetimes (required; trailing-`Z` accepted as JavaScript's `Date.toISOString()` emits it; naive treated as UTC), optional `mode` ‚àà `{"swing","day"}` (other values silently ignored ‚Äî matches the existing `/v1/signals/me/history` convention), optional `symbol` (uppercased single ticker), optional `by_version` ‚àà `{"1","true","yes"}`. Returns either `{ summary: <HistoricalValidationSummary> }` (default) or `{ by_parameter_version: { "__all__": ..., "v1": ..., "v2": ... } }` (when `by_version=true`), plus echoed `horizon` / `from` / `to` / `mode` / `symbol` and the standing `HISTORICAL_VALIDATION_DISCLAIMER = "Historical signal accuracy does not guarantee future results."` from `stocvest/api/legal_copy.py` (newly added; single-sourced so the dashboard tab (Phase 3b), public mirror, and assistant cannot drift from the verbatim wording). **JSON safety:** Phase 1's `BucketStats.accuracy` is `math.nan` when there are no resolved-non-neutral rows, and Python's default `json.dumps` emits the literal `NaN` (invalid JSON, crashes browsers). The handler's `_bucket_stats_to_dict` converts NaN ‚Üí `None` at serialization time so the wire response is valid JSON and the UI renders "‚Äî" instead of a misleading "0%" ‚Äî locked in by `test_empty_window_serializes_nan_accuracy_as_null` which asserts both `body["summary"]["overall"]["accuracy"] is None` AND `"NaN" not in resp["body"]`. **Validation contract:** invalid / missing `horizon` ‚Üí `400 { error: "bad_request", message: "horizon must be '1h' or '1d'." }`; unparseable / missing `from` or `to` ‚Üí `400` with a message naming the missing field; inverted window (`to <= from`) ‚Üí `400 { ..., message: "to must be strictly after from." }`; no auth ‚Üí `401`. **Route registration:** `signals_http_dispatch` in `signals.py` dispatches the new route; `infra/apigateway_6e.tf` adds `"GET /v1/signals/historical-validation/summary" = { module_key = "signals", authorizer = true }` (one new `aws_apigatewayv2_route.http` resource ‚Äî Terraform `plan` showed exactly `1 to add, 0 to change, 0 to destroy`; applied 2026-05-11). **No new DynamoDB tables, no new Lambda functions, no new IAM** ‚Äî the route lands on the existing `aws_lambda_function.api["signals"]` integration that already serves the rest of `/v1/signals/*`. **No BFF route or UI in this commit** ‚Äî those are Phase 3b. **Tests:** +14 in `tests/api/handlers/test_signals_historical_validation.py` covering auth requirement, missing/invalid `horizon`, missing/invalid `from`, inverted window 400, trailing-Z ISO acceptance, happy-path 2/3 directional accuracy with disclaimer + `parameter_versions = ["v1"]`, empty-window NaN‚Üínull JSON serialization, per-user scope isolation, `mode=day` filter passthrough, lowercase `symbol=msft` ‚Üí uppercased + filtered, horizon `1d` routing for rows with only `outcome_1h` populated, and the `by_version=true` per-version map shape (v1=2/2, v2=1c+1i, `__all__`=3/4 with `parameter_versions=["v1","v2"]`). Backend baseline **970 ‚Üí 984 passed (+14)**, frontend **176** (unchanged ‚Äî no UI yet). **Prior commit (2026-05-11) ‚Äî D2 Historical Signal Validation Phase 2 (service layer over `SignalHistory`):** Phase 1 (commit `7d0faf4`) shipped a pure aggregator over an in-memory list of `SignalRecord`; this commit shipped the thin seam between that aggregator and the live store. New module `stocvest/api/services/historical_validation_service.py` exposes a `HistoricalValidationService` built on a narrow `SignalHistoryReader` Protocol ‚Äî both `InMemorySignalRecorder` and `DynamoDBSignalRecorder` already satisfy it via their existing `get_signal_history(user_id, symbol, days, limit, mode, ledger_qualified_only)` signature, so production wiring is one constructor call (`HistoricalValidationService(get_signal_recorder())`) and tests use a list-backed `_StubStore` double with no boto3. The service takes an absolute `[from_at, to_at)` window (**lower bound inclusive, upper bound exclusive ‚Äî same semantics as the GSI `scope_generated_at` predicate** `generated_at >= cutoff_iso`, so a caller passing `from_at = midnight ET today, to_at = midnight ET tomorrow` gets "today's signals" with no off-by-one), translates it into the recorder's trailing-N-day convention (computes `days_back = ceil((now - from_at) / 1 day) + 1` and clamps at `MAX_LOOKBACK_DAYS = 366` so a buggy "last 10 years" call cannot drain the GSI), then post-filters to the requested window. `MAX_ROWS_PER_QUERY = 1000` is a deliberate guardrail ‚Äî typical per-user windows are a few hundred signals over 30 days; cursor-based pagination for admin cross-user analytics is a Phase 3+ concern. Two methods: `summarize(user_id, from_at, to_at, horizon, mode=None, symbol=None) ‚Üí HistoricalValidationSummary` returns the Phase 1 summary for the window directly, and `summarize_by_parameter_version(...)` groups the same window by `parameter_version` and returns `{"__all__": <combined>, "v1": <...>, "v2": <...>, "unknown": <...>}` so Phase 3 can render a "v1 vs v2 vs all versions" diff without recomputing ‚Äî rows with `parameter_version is None` or empty/whitespace land in `UNKNOWN_VERSION_KEY = "unknown"` so legacy rows (emitted before the column shipped) are never silently dropped. Inverted / zero-width windows (`to_at <= from_at`) short-circuit to an empty summary without touching the store. `user_id` / `symbol` / `mode` pass straight through to the store unchanged ‚Äî the store is the auth perimeter and the service does not silently change scope. **No HTTP route, no BFF route, no UI in this commit** ‚Äî those are Phase 3. **No DynamoDB schema changes** ‚Äî the existing GSI `scope_generated_at` already supports the date-range query we need. Test surface: `tests/api/services/test_historical_validation_service.py` adds 14 lock-in tests covering empty-store NaN, inverted-bounds short-circuit, equal-bounds short-circuit, happy-path 2/3 accuracy with neutrals excluded from the denominator, **inclusive-lower / exclusive-upper window edge cases** (rows at `from_at` kept, rows at `to_at` dropped, before / after / inside boundary rows behave correctly), naive-`generated_at` UTC normalization, `user_id`/`symbol`/`mode` passthrough, `days_back` computed to cover `from_at`, `MAX_LOOKBACK_DAYS` clamp, horizon routing (a row with `outcome_1h` populated but `outcome_1d` pending counts at 1h, not 1d, but still shows in `rows_examined`), the `__all__` combined aggregate alongside per-version buckets, `unknown` bucketing for missing/blank `parameter_version`, an empty window producing only an `__all__` bucket with NaN accuracy, and window-filter-before-version-split (out-of-window v1 rows must not inflate the v1 bucket). Backend test baseline: **956 ‚Üí 970** (+14 new, zero regressions). Frontend test baseline unchanged at 176 (frontend-only work was prior commit). **Prior commit (2026-05-11) ‚Äî sliding-session refresh (Cognito REFRESH_TOKEN_AUTH):** the user reported being signed out while actively working. Root cause was a three-part architecture flaw: (a) `infra/cognito.tf` never sets `id_token_validity` so Cognito's default of 60 minutes was in effect, (b) `frontend/lib/auth/cognito.ts:signIn()` captured only the `IdToken` and silently discarded the `RefreshToken` from the same Cognito response, and (c) `SessionExpiryWatcher` decoded the JWT `exp` claim and scheduled `setTimeout(() => markSessionExpired("expired"), exp)` ‚Äî firing at exactly the wall-clock moment regardless of how active the user was. The fix implements a proper sliding-session contract: a continuously-active user with a valid Cognito refresh token stays signed in indefinitely (default 30-day refresh-token lifetime), while a truly-inactive user is signed out only when the refresh token expires or is revoked. **Implementation:** (1) **server-side** ‚Äî `frontend/lib/auth/cognito.ts` now captures `RefreshToken` from both `signIn()` and `respondToNewPasswordChallenge()` and exposes a new `refreshIdToken(refreshToken)` that calls Cognito with `AuthFlow: REFRESH_TOKEN_AUTH`. `frontend/lib/auth/session-cookies.ts` now writes a third httpOnly cookie `stocvest_refresh_token` (`maxAge = 30 * 24 * 60 * 60` matching Cognito's default refresh-token validity) alongside the existing `stocvest_auth_token` (httpOnly) and `stocvest_ws_token` (non-httpOnly mirror), and clears all three on `clearSessionTokenCookies()`. `frontend/lib/auth/refresh-token-cookie.ts` (new) exposes `refreshTokenCookieName()` + `readRefreshTokenCookie()` for server-only consumers. The login (`frontend/app/login/actions.ts`) and new-password (`frontend/app/new-password/actions.ts`) actions thread the refresh token through to the cookie setter. (2) **BFF route** ‚Äî `frontend/app/api/auth/refresh/route.ts` (new) is a `POST` handler that reads the refresh-token cookie, calls Cognito `refreshIdToken()`, rewrites the ID + mirror cookies via `setSessionTokenCookiesFromIdToken(idToken)` (no `refreshToken` argument ‚Äî Cognito does not rotate refresh tokens on `REFRESH_TOKEN_AUTH` in our pool config, so the existing 30-day cookie stays valid), and returns `200 { exp }` on success. On any failure (no cookie, Cognito throws, Cognito returns 200 without `IdToken`) it clears all three cookies and returns `401 { error: "refresh_failed" | "no_refresh_token" }` so the client falls back to the calm `SessionExpiredBanner`. Same-origin only, no request body read, runtime "nodejs" because the AWS SDK requires Node APIs. (3) **client refresh helper** ‚Äî `frontend/lib/auth/refresh-session.ts` (new) exposes `refreshSession()` with **single-flight coalescing** (parallel callers ‚Äî e.g. five concurrent 401s on a busy dashboard ‚Äî all await the same in-flight POST so we never kick off a refresh storm; the in-flight slot clears on `setTimeout(0)` so callers that resolved against the same promise can still observe the result) and a **5-second failure cooldown** (after a refresh fails, subsequent calls short-circuit to `false` without hitting the BFF, because the calm banner is already the right UX surface and we don't want to hammer Cognito with a refresh-storm). (4) **proactive watcher** ‚Äî `frontend/components/auth/session-expiry-watcher.tsx` is rebuilt: instead of firing `markSessionExpired()` at `exp`, it schedules a `setTimeout` to fire `refreshSession()` `REFRESH_LEAD_MS = 2 minutes` *before* `exp`, re-evaluates on `visibilitychange ‚Üí visible` + `focus`, and only marks expired if the refresh call returns `false`. On a successful refresh it re-runs `evaluate()` to reschedule from the new `exp` automatically. (5) **reactive 401 retry** ‚Äî `frontend/lib/api/browser-api-fetch.ts` now attempts `refreshSession()` on 401 and retries the original request **once** with the freshly-rewritten mirror cookie; only marks expired if the refresh itself fails OR the retry also returns 401. **403 is unchanged** ‚Äî STOCVEST uses 403 for product-rule denials (PDT lockout, margin, paid-tier gating) where the user IS authenticated, and those must never trigger refresh-or-expire (locked in by `tests/browser-api-fetch-refresh.test.ts` and `tests/surface-auth-error.test.ts`). (6) **shared fallback** ‚Äî `frontend/lib/auth/surface-auth-error.ts` (used by the six client fetch helpers that don't go through `browserApiFetch` ‚Äî `fetch-symbol-bars`, `fetch-symbol-snapshot`, `fetch-macro-context`, `ticker-news-panel`, `public-signals`, the STOCVEST Assistant) is now async and attempts a refresh first; on success it returns `true` without marking expired (the caller's next interaction picks up the new cookie automatically) and only marks expired if the refresh fails. The six callers were updated to `await` it (the assistant uses the return value to short-circuit) or `void` it (the five fire-and-forget helpers). **No Terraform changes** ‚Äî `ALLOW_REFRESH_TOKEN_AUTH` is already in `infra/cognito.tf` `explicit_auth_flows` for both app clients, and the 30-day refresh-token validity is Cognito's default which matches the cookie `maxAge`. **Dev mock unchanged** ‚Äî `loginAsDevUser` mints an unsigned JWT with `exp = now + 365d` and never goes through Cognito, so it has no refresh token; the refresh route gracefully returns `401 { error: "no_refresh_token" }` if a dev-mock session ever hits it, and the watcher never schedules a refresh because the dev `exp` is a year out. **Behavior contract:** continuously-active user ‚Üí stays signed in indefinitely up to the 30-day refresh-token lifetime, never sees the banner. Inactive for the full 60-minute ID-token lifetime ‚Üí next interaction refreshes silently, user does not notice. Inactive ‚â• 30 days OR refresh token revoked / Cognito rejects ‚Üí calm `SessionExpiredBanner` appears, user clicks "Sign in", lands on `/login?reason=expired&next=...`. **Prior commit (D2 Historical Signal Validation Phase 1 ‚Äî `7d0faf4`, 2026-05-11):** pure aggregation module over `SignalRecord` rows producing a frozen `HistoricalValidationSummary` stratified six ways (renamed from "Backtesting" at the user's request to mirror the assistant's verbatim disclosure phrase "Historical signal accuracy does not guarantee future results"); the new framing mirrors the assistant's verbatim disclosure phrase "Historical signal accuracy does not guarantee future results" and the existing `/dashboard/signal-validation` page. The deliberate rename also de-risks the legal posture: the module **measures real emitted signals** (the rows `signal_recorder.resolve_signals` populates with `outcome_1h` / `outcome_1d` against real subsequent Polygon prices) ‚Äî it does not generate synthetic signals against historical bars, and `BucketStats` is restricted to directional accuracy (`correct / (correct + incorrect)` with neutrals excluded from the denominator, matching the existing `GET /v1/signals/performance/summary` definition so the historical view and live tracked-outcomes view never disagree on the same data). Implementation: `stocvest/signals/historical_validation.py` ‚Äî a pure, deterministic aggregator that takes a list of `SignalRecord` and a horizon (`1h` or `1d`) and returns a frozen `HistoricalValidationSummary` with `overall` plus six stratifications: Decision state at entry (`actionable` / `monitor` / `blocked` / `unknown`), Macro regime at entry (`risk_on` / `neutral` / `risk_off` / `avoid` / `unknown` ‚Äî engine vocabulary, matches what `regime_label_at_entry` actually stores), trading Mode (`swing` / `day`), Pattern family (`swing_composite` / `orb` / `vwap` / `momentum` / `gap_with_catalyst`; unknown patterns overflow into `other` so nothing silently vanishes), Trade Readiness bucket (`high` ‚â• 70 / `moderate` 40‚Äì69 / `low` < 40 ‚Äî same thresholds as the Evidence card), and Direction (`bullish` / `bearish` / `neutral`). Empty / all-neutral strata return `accuracy = NaN` so the UI renders "‚Äî" rather than a misleading "0%". `rows_examined` and the sorted set of observed `parameter_versions` ride along on the summary so the UI can show users exactly which rules-bundle the number describes. **No new I/O, no new infra, no UI in this commit** ‚Äî the next phases plug this aggregator into a thin service layer (Phase 2 ‚Äî date-range slice from `SignalHistory` keyed by `parameter_version`), then into `GET /v1/signals/historical-validation/summary` + a new tab on `/dashboard/signal-validation` and an optional public mirror on `/performance` for the overall + by-mode bucket only (Phase 3), then into cross-version diffs (Phase 4 ‚Äî rules-bundle A vs B). **Explicit non-goals:** win-rate / expectancy / dollar P&L (product never publishes these); re-resolution at synthetic horizons (T+5d, T+10d, T+30d) using simulated bars; anything that frames validation as a forecast. **Prior commit (B26 STOCVEST Assistant ‚Äî in-memory-only conversation state ‚Äî `1e0e4a6`, 2026-05-11):** removed the `sessionStorage`-backed conversation persistence so a fresh conversation starts on every page load / cross-surface navigation / login / logout / session expiry; see ¬ß2 below. STOCVEST Assistant is now mounted in the **root layout for every visitor** (logged-in and anonymous) ‚Äî authenticated traffic hits `POST /v1/signals/assistant/chat` with the JWT + page context, and anonymous marketing visitors hit the new **`POST /v1/public/assistant/chat`** (no authorizer) so prospects on `/`, `/login`, `/signup`, etc. can ask what STOCVEST is, how it differs from signal-alert services, and for explanations of finance terms while the locked system prompt's PUBLIC MODE section refuses all trade advice, predictions, and accuracy claims. **2026-05-11 latest ‚Äî in-memory-only conversation state:** the assistant no longer persists conversation history to `sessionStorage`. A fresh conversation starts on every page load (including hard refresh), every cross-surface navigation, every login/logout, every session expiry, and every explicit "Sign out" click. This closes two regressions reported by the user: (1) on refresh, stale conversation re-appeared even when the user expected a clean surface, and (2) on in-place login (auth flip without navigation), the previous hydrate effect was clobbering `prevAuthRef` ‚Äî the ref the auth-change reset effect depended on ‚Äî so the homepage public-mode conversation survived into the authenticated context. The simplest, safest fix was to remove the persistence layer entirely so no stale state can survive any kind of transition. Implementation: `stocvest-assistant.tsx` drops the `readPersistedState`/`writePersistedState`/`removePersistedState` helpers and the hydrate-on-mount + persist-on-change `useEffect`s; the component now has one one-shot mount effect that opportunistically wipes legacy `sessionStorage` data (`stocvest_assistant_state_v1`) for existing tabs, plus the three reset effects (pathname-change, auth-flip, session-expiry/explicit-clear) that already existed but now own `prevAuthRef` exclusively so the auth-flip detection is reliable. `lib/assistant/session-reset.ts` still exports `clearAssistantSession()` (logout buttons call it before the server-action redirect) and the `stocvest:assistant-reset` event ‚Äî both continue to fire because they are defensive against any legacy data and against any future re-introduction of persistence. **2026-05-11 (earlier same day) ‚Äî two-context safety perimeter:** the locked prompt now opens with a CRITICAL CONTEXT AWARENESS RULE that splits the world into two top-level safety contexts (LOGGED-OUT = `session_mode=public`, LOGGED-IN = `session_mode=authenticated`) and forbids the LLM from implying access to features unavailable in the current context. PUBLIC MODE RULES was strengthened with an explicit per-symbol MUST-NOT list (no evaluating any specific stock, no Evidence card reference for a specific stock, no Trade Readiness score for a specific symbol, no naming a specific layer as "currently blocking" a specific ticker, no sounding like a live demo of unavailable features) keyed by concrete ticker examples (AAPL / TSLA / NVDA / MSFT) so the LLM pattern-matches any ticker the visitor names. A HOMEPAGE-SAFE REFUSAL TEMPLATE ‚Äî "I can't assess individual stocks here, and I don't give buy or sell answers. What I can explain is how STOCVEST decides whether trading conditions are aligned once a symbol is evaluated inside the platform." ‚Äî is in the prompt verbatim so the LLM falls back to it for any per-symbol question on the homepage rather than improvising. The LOGGED-OUT GOLDEN RULE ‚Äî "explain the FRAMEWORK, not the DECISION" ‚Äî is also in the prompt verbatim. TONE & STYLE now also says "When refusing a request, explain WHY the boundary exists" so refusals build trust instead of feeling dismissive. The locked system prompt has now been **upgraded to an explanatory-voice contract** (2026-05-11 earlier the same day): it opens with PRIMARY GOAL + CORE PRODUCT PHILOSOPHY ("STOCVEST does not attempt to predict markets ‚Äî STOCVEST evaluates alignment, risk, and confirmation, and decides WHEN trading is statistically worth risking capital", "Silence is an intentional system state"), enumerates the six real layers by their product names (Technical / News / Macro / Sector / Geopolitical / Market Internals), references the verbatim Decision lines from `lib/signal-evidence/trade-decision.ts` (`‚úÖ Actionable ‚Äî passes risk/reward and confirmation thresholds`, `‚öÝÔ∏è Monitor only ‚Äî confirmation and/or risk gates are not fully cleared`, `üö´ Blocked ‚Äî fails minimum synthesis and risk gates`), describes the shipped Macro pulse states (Unavailable / Elevated / Upcoming / Known and absorbed), the shipped sector chip labels (Confirming / Non-confirming / Mixed; Risk-on / Defensive / Mixed / Narrow), the real Trade Readiness 0-100 scale, the Layer alignment High/Moderate/Low buckets, and adds dedicated SUPPRESSION & GATING LOGIC, REGIME TRANSITIONS, BACKTESTING & VALIDATION, USER INTERACTION RULES (MAY / MUST NOT), and PAYWALL AWARENESS sections ‚Äî while **explicitly forbidding invented concepts** that do not ship in STOCVEST: "System Confidence", "VIC", "Volatility Control", "Supportive / Neutral / Hostile" volatility states, "Symbol Readiness Score", "Sector Fragmented", a 0.0-1.0 readiness scale, or any made-up X% accuracy figure (the only validated outcomes live on `/performance` and `/dashboard/signal-validation` with the standing disclaimer "Historical signal accuracy does not guarantee future results."). All existing operational guardrails are preserved: the banned self-limitation phrases ("I don't have", "I can't see", "at this moment", "right now I lack", ‚Ä¶), the banned response shapes block with the production BAD/GOOD pair, the three-mode structure (General / Contextual / Public), and the foundational principle "To help users understand how STOCVEST thinks ‚Äî not to tell them what to do." Every dashboard page (`dashboard`, `dashboard/scanner`, `dashboard/signals` (+ history), `dashboard/watchlists`, `dashboard/signal-validation`, `dashboard/earnings`, `dashboard/portfolio`, `dashboard/journal`, `dashboard/performance`, `dashboard/options`, `dashboard/futures`, `dashboard/crypto`, `dashboard/settings`, `dashboard/legal`) calls `usePublishAssistantContext`; **cross-surface conversations now isolate by URL pathname** ‚Äî the assistant pulls `usePathname()` from `next/navigation` and wipes the persisted conversation the moment the pathname changes, so navigating from `dashboard/signals/layers` (TTD) to `/`, `/dashboard`, `/dashboard/scanner`, `/login`, or any other route starts a fresh conversation. Pathname-based detection also catches routes that publish no page context at all (marketing surfaces like `/`, `/login`, `/signup`), which a `pageContext.page`-only signal would have missed. Hydrate also force-clears any legacy persisted state whose `isAuthenticated` field is missing (data written by a build before the field existed), so a logged-in conversation can never re-surface on the anonymous home page. The conversation also resets on logout (sign-out buttons fire `clearAssistantSession()` before the server action) and on session expiry (the assistant subscribes to `subscribeSessionExpired`).

the asymmetry plus contrasting backgrounds make the two roles unmistakable even in monochrome), **six-layer constellation context strip**, word-fade reveal on fresh assistant turns (respects **`prefers-reduced-motion`**), explicit **General / Contextual** mode badge; ## 2. Implemented (where to look)

**Backend (`stocvest/`)**  
**Also shipped:** **STOCVEST Assistant chatbot** ‚Äî **`stocvest/signals/assistant_prompts.py`** (system prompt held verbatim as `ASSISTANT_SYSTEM_PROMPT`; **2026-05-11 explanatory-voice upgrade** restructured the prompt into product-anchored sections ‚Äî PRIMARY GOAL, CORE PRODUCT PHILOSOPHY ("Silence is an intentional system state"), ANALYSIS LAYERS (the six real product layer names ‚Äî Technical / News / Macro / Sector / Geopolitical / Market Internals), MARKET REGIME (UI Bullish/Neutral/Bearish + engine risk_on/risk_off/neutral/avoid), SECTOR CONFIRMATION (Confirming / Non-confirming / Mixed; Risk-on / Defensive / Narrow), MARKET PULSE (Unavailable / Elevated / Upcoming / Known and absorbed; pulse never authorizes trades), INTERNALS & VOLATILITY (VIX is a signal inside Internals, NOT a standalone "VIC"), TRADE READINESS (0-100 scale, never 0.0-1.0), DECISION STATES (verbatim lines from `lib/signal-evidence/trade-decision.ts`), ALIGNMENT & CONFIDENCE (Layer alignment buckets + Trade Readiness, never an invented "System Confidence"), SUPPRESSION & GATING LOGIC (with the dashboard's exact empty-state copy: "No active swing setups right now", "System posture: Waiting for alignment", "Swing suppressed ‚Äî risk-off tape", "Signal suppressed ‚Äî regime not cleared"), REGIME TRANSITIONS (probabilistic language only ‚Äî never forecast a flip), BACKTESTING & VALIDATION (route to `/performance` and `/dashboard/signal-validation` with the standing disclaimer; never invent a hit-rate), USER INTERACTION RULES (MAY / MUST NOT lists), PAYWALL AWARENESS (swing_pro / swing_day_pro / active beta ‚Äî the LLM knows it's the paid path and never describes the deterministic free-tier fallback as an error), TONE & STYLE (frame inactivity as intentional and protective; frame silence as discipline; frame patience as skill), END GOAL & FOUNDATIONAL PRINCIPLE; **explicitly forbids invented concepts that do not ship**: "System Confidence", "VIC", "Volatility Control", "Supportive / Neutral / Hostile" volatility states, "Symbol Readiness Score", "Sector Fragmented", a 0.0-1.0 readiness scale, or any made-up "X% accuracy" figure; forbids bullet lists / numbered lists / section headings / markdown formatting in replies by default; **expanded ban-list of self-referential phrases** ("I don't have", "I can't see", "I can't access", "I would need to see", "to give you a precise explanation I would need", "at this moment", "right now I lack", etc.) with an explicit "stop and rewrite" instruction so the LLM cannot fall back to "I don't have access to live page data" even when the conversation history contains a different symbol than the current page; preserves the **banned response shapes** block with the concrete BAD/GOOD pair drawn from the exact failure mode we saw in production (LLM apologizing about TTD swing details after the user navigated to the home page); adds an explicit fallback rule when only a symbol/page is in context: explain STOCVEST in calm general terms instead of refusing; `sanitize_messages` drops any non-`user`/`assistant` turn so a client cannot inject a fake `system` role, caps single message at **2000 chars**, trims history to **12** turns; `serialize_page_context` whitelist-emits only known keys, including the new **`analysis_status`** = `loaded` \| `loading` \| `unavailable` \| `insufficient_data` so the assistant can distinguish "decision visible on screen" from "user has selected a symbol but the analysis has not loaded yet"), **`stocvest/signals/assistant_chat.py`** (`AssistantChatService.reply` builds `system = ASSISTANT_SYSTEM_PROMPT + serialize_page_context(...)` and posts to Anthropic Messages API with the proper top-level `system` parameter; free users ‚Äî no `has_ai_explanations` ‚Äî receive deterministic copy and never reach Claude; no conversation cache), **`assistant_chat_handler`** in **`stocvest/api/handlers/signals.py`** dispatched under **`POST /v1/signals/assistant/chat`** (returns `text`, `source`, `mode`, `upgrade_available`, `disclaimer`). **Tests:** **`tests/api/handlers/test_signals_assistant_chat.py`** (unauth 401, invalid body 400, free-user deterministic path, mode-from-context, paid-user AI path with service mock, sanitizer drops client-injected `system` role). **`AuditEvent`** + **`api/services/audit_store.py`** / **`api/services/audit_capture.py`** (writes when **`DYNAMODB_AUDIT_EVENTS_TABLE`** is set); swallowed errors), **`services/gap_intelligence_news.py`** global + per-ticker Polygon news merge, **`POST /v1/scanner/gap-intelligence`**, structured **`POST /v1/signals/day/briefing`** / **`POST /v1/scanner/briefing`**, **`POST /v1/signals/swing/composite`** (client-supplied layer scores) and **`POST /v1/signals/composite/real`** (intraday bars, server-side layers via `real_composite_engine.py`) and **`POST /v1/signals/composite/swing`** (`swing_composite_engine.py`, daily bars, extended news/macro/geo windows) return **`status: insufficient_data`** (HTTP 200) when fewer than three layers are available ‚Äî no composite record or alert; **`lambda_dispatch.py`** now routes SQS news-consumer events; **`workers/news_worker.py`** is the long-running ECS entrypoint and **`workers/news_consumer_lambda.py`** is the SQS-triggered Claude scoring consumer; journal **`GET /v1/journal/analytics`** + entry by id + PATCH notes, auth, `legal_copy.py`, order safety integration), **`utils/log_privacy.py`**. **Sliding-session auth surface** (2026-05-11) ‚Äî the user's "I was actively working and got logged out" regression is fixed by **`frontend/lib/auth/refresh-token-cookie.ts`** (server-only refresh-cookie name + reader), **`frontend/lib/auth/refresh-session.ts`** (client-side `refreshSession()` with single-flight coalescing + 5-second post-failure cooldown), **`frontend/app/api/auth/refresh/route.ts`** (BFF POST handler that reads the httpOnly `stocvest_refresh_token` cookie, calls Cognito `REFRESH_TOKEN_AUTH` via `refreshIdToken()` in `frontend/lib/auth/cognito.ts`, rewrites the ID + mirror cookies, returns `200 { exp }` on success or `401` after clearing all cookies on failure), and a **rebuilt `frontend/components/auth/session-expiry-watcher.tsx`** that schedules a refresh ~2 min before the JWT `exp` instead of firing the expired event at `exp`. `frontend/lib/api/browser-api-fetch.ts` now does refresh-and-retry on 401 (one retry); `frontend/lib/auth/surface-auth-error.ts` (used by `fetch-symbol-bars`, `fetch-symbol-snapshot`, `fetch-macro-context`, `ticker-news-panel`, `public-signals`, and the STOCVEST Assistant) is async and attempts a refresh before marking expired. **403 is intentionally not treated as auth failure** ‚Äî STOCVEST uses 403 for product-rule denials (PDT, margin, paid-tier gating) where the user IS authenticated. Tests: `frontend/tests/refresh-session.test.ts` + `frontend/tests/browser-api-fetch-refresh.test.ts` + `frontend/tests/surface-auth-error.test.ts` (+15 over the 161 baseline). **`stocvest/signals/historical_validation.py`** ‚Äî **D2 Historical Signal Validation (Phase 1)**: pure deterministic aggregator over a list of `SignalRecord` rows, returns a frozen `HistoricalValidationSummary` per horizon (`1h` / `1d`) with `overall` + six stratifications (Decision state at entry, Macro regime at entry ‚Äî engine vocabulary `risk_on` / `neutral` / `risk_off` / `avoid`, trading Mode, Pattern family, Trade Readiness bucket high‚â•70 / moderate 40-69 / low<40, Direction); accuracy is `correct / (correct + incorrect)` with neutrals excluded from the denominator and NaN for empty / all-neutral strata; carries `rows_examined` + sorted `parameter_versions` provenance; no I/O ‚Äî Phase 2 wraps this with a thin service layer (`stocvest/api/services/historical_validation_service.py`) that slices `SignalHistory` by date range and parameter version. Phase 3a exposes it at `GET /v1/signals/historical-validation/summary` (auth-gated, in `stocvest/api/handlers/signals.py::historical_validation_summary_handler`); Phase 3b ships the dashboard tab (`frontend/components/historical-validation-panel.tsx` + `frontend/lib/api/historical-validation.ts` + BFF route at `frontend/app/api/stocvest/signals/historical-validation/summary/route.ts`); Phase 3c-1 ships the public mirror (`GET /v1/signals/historical-validation/public-summary` in the same handler module, surfaced on `/performance` via `frontend/components/performance-tracking-content.tsx::PublicValidationSection` with a trimmed `overall + by_mode + rows_examined` projection enforced by `_public_summary_to_dict` so per-decision / per-regime / per-pattern / per-readiness / per-direction / per-symbol detail can never reach a logged-out visitor ‚Äî `symbol` is explicitly 400-rejected at the public endpoint). **Phase 3c-2 (2026-05-11)** ‚Äî the assistant chatbot is now aware of the user's per-user summary on the LOGGED-IN path: `stocvest/api/handlers/signals.py::assistant_chat_handler` fetches `HistoricalValidationService(...).summarize(user_id=rc.user_id, horizon="1d", from_at=now-90d, to_at=now)` on every authenticated chat turn (defensive try/except ‚Äî a slow / unavailable signal-history store must NOT break the chat reply, and on failure the handler forwards `historical_validation_summary=None` so the prompt's "if absent, do not comment" rule activates); `stocvest/signals/assistant_chat.py::serialize_historical_validation_summary` emits a calm tail block `=== HISTORICAL VALIDATION ===\nwindow_days=90\nhorizon=1d\noverall=<pct>% (<correct> correct of <resolved> resolved; <neutral> neutral; <total> total)\nswing=...\nday=...\nrows_examined=<n>` ‚Äî same trimmed projection as the public mirror but scoped to the calling user (overall + by_mode only, no per-decision / per-regime / per-pattern / per-readiness / per-direction stratifications reach the LLM); NaN accuracy renders as the em-dash `‚Äî` and is NEVER rendered as `"0.0%"` or the literal `"NaN"` string; empty `by_mode` buckets are omitted from the serialized text (Phase 1 pre-seeds the vocabulary so swing/day always appear as keys even when zero rows, but the serializer drops them to avoid the LLM paraphrasing zero-rows as "your day track has no data"); the `=== HISTORICAL VALIDATION ===` sentinel is referenced inside the new `HISTORICAL VALIDATION CONTEXT (LOGGED-IN ONLY)` section of `stocvest/signals/assistant_prompts.py::ASSISTANT_SYSTEM_PROMPT` so the LLM knows what to pattern-match on. The new prompt section enumerates what the assistant **MAY** reference (the user's overall directional accuracy with denominator transparency, the swing-vs-day shape in qualitative terms, the sample size as a small-window caveat, and a redirect to `/dashboard/signal-validation` for the stratified breakdown) and what it **MUST NOT** do (translate accuracy into dollar P&L / expected returns / win-rates ‚Äî "Directional accuracy is NOT a return number"; predict whether the trend will continue or mean-revert ‚Äî "descriptive, not predictive"; compare to "the market" / other users / a benchmark; recommend mode choice based on accuracy ‚Äî "Mode choice is not an advice surface"; use the figures to claim the system "works" ‚Äî "evidence of behavior, not promotion"; discuss per-symbol / per-pattern / per-regime / per-decision-state / per-readiness-bucket / per-direction performance because those are "deliberately withheld" from the assistant's context; reference any validation figures when the block is absent ‚Äî "No block means no comment; never invent a number, never recall a number from a previous turn"). The public chat path (`AssistantChatService.reply_public`) is untouched ‚Äî it refuses the kwarg by signature, never carries the sentinel block, and the public prompt path's `session_mode=public` marker still routes the LLM into PUBLIC MODE RULES where per-user numbers cannot be discussed regardless. **Phase 4 (2026-05-11)** ‚Äî cross-version diff view on `/dashboard/signal-validation`'s Historical accuracy tab. Purely a dashboard UI + math-helpers slice; reuses the existing Phase 3a `GET /v1/signals/historical-validation/summary?by_version=true` endpoint and the Phase 3b `fetchHistoricalValidationByVersion` client without any backend / Terraform / IAM / BFF changes. `frontend/lib/api/historical-validation.ts` grew four pure helpers (`diffBucketStats(a, b)` returns a `BucketDelta` with `accuracyDelta` / `totalDelta` / `resolvedDelta` / `neutralDelta` / `smallSampleA` / `smallSampleB`; `formatAccuracyDelta(delta)` renders percentage-point strings; `selectComparableVersions(map)` excludes `__all__` and sorts `v<n>` numerically with `unknown` always last; `defaultCompareSelection(map)` picks the last two comparable versions) and exposed the constants `SMALL_SAMPLE_THRESHOLD = 10` / `ALL_VERSIONS_KEY = "__all__"` / `UNKNOWN_VERSION_KEY = "unknown"`. `frontend/components/historical-validation-panel.tsx` grew an inline **Compare versions** checkbox (off by default ‚Äî the panel still opens to the calm single-version view) that swaps the fetch from `fetchHistoricalValidationSummary` to `fetchHistoricalValidationByVersion` and replaces the body with a `CompareBody` component: two version selectors (defaulting to the latest pair via `defaultCompareSelection`, preserving the user's explicit selections when only the window changes), an A / B / Œî tri-column overall hero card, a stratification grid with `CompareStratificationCard`s that union the keys across the two versions (a pattern family that only fired on one side still shows as a row with `‚Äî` on the side it did not fire), and a `CompareBucketRow` per stratum showing A's accuracy + `(correct/resolved)`, B's accuracy + `(correct/resolved)`, and the Œî formatted as `+5.2pp` / `-3.1pp` / `0.0pp` / `‚Äî`. Empty / not-meaningful states are handled inline: fewer than two comparable versions in the window renders a calm "need at least two parameter versions in this window to compare ‚Ä¶ widen the window" message; same-version-on-both-sides renders an italic "pick a different version on either side to see a delta" banner; user-changes-A-or-B while in compare mode does not refetch (selections are pure local state). Small-sample annotations (`< 10` resolved-non-neutral signals on either side) attach a muted "small sample" pill next to that side's cell without obscuring the delta. Color discipline matches the rest of the validation surface ‚Äî no red/green (accuracy isn't profit), all calm accent tints and monospace deltas. The same verbatim `HISTORICAL_VALIDATION_DISCLAIMER` from the backend response renders below the compare body so the wording cannot drift between the single-version and compare views. The assistant chatbot is deliberately **NOT** wired to consume cross-version diffs ‚Äî parameter_versions are an engine implementation detail and surfacing them through the LLM would be a leaky abstraction; the Phase 3c-2 user-scoped historical summary already covers the LLM's needs. **No Terraform, no backend, no BFF, no new dependencies.** Tests: +14 in `tests/historical-validation-api.test.ts` (covered in the frontend baseline cell above). Backend baseline 1015/3 unchanged. **D2 functionally complete end-to-end** with Phase 4 shipped (Phase 1 aggregator ‚Üí Phase 2 service ‚Üí Phase 3a auth API ‚Üí Phase 3b dashboard tab ‚Üí Phase 3c-1 public mirror ‚Üí Phase 3c-2 assistant awareness ‚Üí Phase 4 cross-version diff). **`composite_score.py`**: layer/verdict contradiction penalty, **`alignment_ratio`**, **`conflicted_layers`**; **`swing_composite_evidence.py`**: reference-level completeness, R/R quality + warning, catalyst headline pass-through, derived **`risk_factors`** / **`risk_factors_detailed`**; **`user_profile_store`**: lazy singleton (no boto3 on handler import); **`tests/conftest.py`**: Windows **`platform.uname()`** prime to avoid botocore/WMI stderr noise with Python 3.14. **Tests:** **`tests/api/test_article_relevance.py`**, **`tests/services/test_news_relevance.py`**, **`tests/api/services/test_news_panel_format.py`**, **`tests/api/handlers/test_market_data.py`**, **`tests/data/test_edgar_client.py`**, **`tests/data/test_news_triage.py`**, **`tests/signals/test_composite_scorer.py`**, **`tests/signals/test_signal_validation.py`**, **`tests/signals/test_risk_reward.py`**, **`tests/signals/test_catalyst_headlines.py`**, **`tests/signals/test_risk_factors.py`**. **Signal validation ledger:** DynamoDB **`SignalHistory`** only (**`SignalRecord`**); optional ledger columns (**`closed_at`**, **`ledger_entry_date_et`** / **`ledger_exit_date_et`**, **`entry_rationale`**, **`exit_reason`**, **`decision_state_entry`** / **`decision_state_exit`**, **`market_regime_exit`**, **`gate_status_json`** ‚Üí API **`gate_status`**, **`setup_type`**, **`exit_rule`**, **`max_adverse_excursion_pct`**, **`max_favorable_excursion_pct`**, **`hold_duration_minutes`**) are populated when enrichment jobs write them; **`signal_resolution`** runs **D1** 1h/1d outcome resolution only. UI: **`/dashboard/signal-validation`** (Swing/Day tabs). The retired notional model book (**`ModelPortfolio`**, signals-lambda **`/v1/portfolio/*`**, portfolio reversal / composite sidecar jobs) has been removed from code and infra.

**Frontend (`frontend/`)**  
**STOCVEST Assistant chatbot UI** lives under **`frontend/components/assistant/`** + **`frontend/lib/assistant/`**: **`stocvest-assistant.tsx`** (top-level orchestrator ‚Äî open state, conversation state, sessionStorage hydration, `surfaceAuthErrorIfAny` on 401, **status-aware fallback copy** when the API call fails; **auth-aware endpoint switching** ‚Äî when the server-rendered `isAuthenticated` is true the component POSTs to `/api/stocvest/signals/assistant/chat` with the full page-context payload, when false it POSTs to the new `/api/stocvest/public/assistant/chat` with `messages` only; **pathname-based cross-surface isolation** ‚Äî the conversation is anchored to the URL pathname via `usePathname()` and wiped the moment the pathname changes, so a TTD answer on `/dashboard/signals/layers` cannot leak into a question on `/`, `/dashboard`, `/dashboard/scanner`, `/login`, or anywhere else; the hydrate effect also force-clears persisted state when (a) `persisted.isAuthenticated` is missing entirely (legacy build), (b) `persisted.isAuthenticated` does not match the current session, or (c) `persisted.lastPathname` differs from the current pathname ‚Äî together these three conditions guarantee the anonymous home page never re-hydrates a logged-in dashboard conversation; **session reset** ‚Äî the assistant subscribes to `subscribeSessionExpired` and `subscribeAssistantReset` so logout / token expiry / any 401 from any fetch clears messages + composer + sessionStorage; the empty state on the marketing surface now opens with a welcoming three-paragraph pitch ‚Äî "Welcome to STOCVEST" ‚Üí the six-layer thesis ‚Üí the kinds of questions visitors can ask ‚Äî instead of the old one-line "ask me anything"), **`lib/assistant/session-reset.ts`** (shared `clearAssistantSession` + `ASSISTANT_STORAGE_KEY` + `stocvest:assistant-reset` custom event; sign-out buttons in `sidebar.tsx` + `mobile-nav-drawer.tsx` call `clearAssistantSession()` in their `onClick` before the server logout action runs so the next visitor on the same tab never sees the prior conversation), **`assistant-launcher.tsx`** (custom concentric-ring lens glyph + slow 3.6s pulse + tone dot when contextual), **`assistant-panel.tsx`** (glassmorphism panel, header with **Mode badge**, **constellation context strip** showing the six signal layers tone-colored from page state, quick-prompts that change with mode ‚Äî anonymous visitors get marketing-flavored prompts like "What is STOCVEST?" / "How is STOCVEST different from signal-alert services?" / "Explain risk/reward in plain terms"; calm composer + disclaimer footer), **`assistant-conversation-rail.tsx`** (no-bubble vertical timeline with gradient rail, small filled speaker nodes, **role-colored speaker labels** ‚Äî accent blue for `YOU`, page-tone for `STOCVEST` ‚Äî and **a 2px role-tinted left ribbon** on each message body with a faint user-only tint so input vs output is unmissable at a glance; **word-fade reveal** for the latest assistant turn). **`lib/assistant/context.tsx`** exposes **`AssistantContextProvider`**, **`useAssistantContext`**, and **`usePublishAssistantContext`** so any dashboard page can publish a whitelisted page-context payload while mounted. **`lib/signal-evidence/trade-decision.ts`** is the **shared source of truth** for `synthTradeDecision` / `deriveDecisionRationale` ‚Äî `signal-evidence-card.tsx` and the signals-page assistant context both read from it, so the Decision shown on the Evidence card and the context handed to the chatbot can never drift. Motion is gated behind **`prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`** in **`app/globals.css`**. BFF proxy at **`app/api/stocvest/signals/assistant/chat/route.ts`** forwards to **`/v1/signals/assistant/chat`** via **`stocvestAuthedFetch`**. The launcher is mounted globally in **`app/dashboard/layout.tsx`** inside **`AssistantContextProvider`**, so it follows the user across every dashboard route. App router pages (dashboard **`layout.tsx`** wraps routes with **legal acknowledgment** + **onboarding** gate; **`dashboard-page-content.tsx`** uses time-bounded **`fetchMarketOverview`** / scanner / earnings loads so the shell is not blocked by a slow BFF; incl. **`/dashboard/performance`**, scanner (**`/dashboard/scanner`** server page: **`fetchDefaultWatchlistSymbols`** in parallel with **`fetchPdtStatus`**, then **`fetchScannerOverview(..., watchlistSymbols)`**), **`/dashboard/watchlists`**, signals with **Signal history** tab (BFF history + record fetch) + **`POST /api/stocvest/signals/composite/real`** or **`/api/stocvest/signals/composite/swing`** per **Day trade / Swing trade** toggle (and legacy **`swing-composite`**) check for **`insufficient_data`** (amber ‚ÄúMarket Data Unavailable‚Äù callout when fewer than three layers have live scores); **`hasValidSignal`** now hides stale AI/radar/reference/evidence when status is insufficient and clears signal state; closed-session insufficient path renders **`components/signals-after-hours-panel.tsx`** with last-session levels/news/watchlist CTA; **Docs**  
`docs/API_CONTRACTS.md` ‚Äî HTTP + broker contracts. **`docs/BACKLOG.md`** ‚Äî detailed planned work (no duplicate of this file‚Äôs status tables). **`docs/SIGNAL_ENGINE.md`** ‚Äî real composite + layer contracts/limitations (incl. **sector SIC** resolution chain and **`SicMappingTier`**: `exact` ‚Üí `prefix` ‚Üí `coarse` ‚Üí `fallback_spy`, optional **`sic_mapping_tier`** on composite sector layer rows). **`docs/DEPLOYMENT.md`** ‚Äî SES / email alert setup for production. **`docs/TUNING_PLAYBOOK.md`** ‚Äî monthly signal-parameter review using **`GET /v1/signals/analysis`** and Secrets **`stocvest/signal-parameters`**. **DynamoDB `ParameterHistory`** (Terraform) stores versioned parameter JSON + audit fields. **User-facing tooltips:** copy for circled‚Äëi **InfoTip** / related dashboard strings is centralized in **`frontend/lib/ui-tooltips.ts`**; **`frontend/components/info-tip.tsx`** renders multiline tips with **`white-space: pre-line`**. **Detailed file-by-file history was removed from this file** to avoid drift; use README + git.

**Public signal API (trust)**  
`GET /v1/signals/recent` (last **50** public `SignalRecord` rows as JSON array when `landing` is absent; **`?landing=true`** returns **`{ "items": [...] }`** with up to **5** rows where **`outcome_1h`** is set ‚Äî allowlisted fields for marketing only, **`ai_summary`** truncated to **120** chars), `GET /v1/signals/performance/summary` ‚Äî directional accuracy from **1d** outcomes; JSON **`correct_direction_count`**, **`incorrect_direction_count`**, **`neutral_direction_count`** (and related totals); accuracy = correct √∑ (correct + incorrect). **`GET /v1/signals/founding-members`** ‚Äî public JSON **`founding_member_count`**, **`founding_spots_total`** (**100**), **`founding_spots_remaining`** (paid subscribers only; see **¬ß1** HTTP row). Authenticated **`GET /v1/signals/me/history`** (optional **`mode`**, **`days`**, **`limit`**, **`symbol`**) and per-id **`GET /v1/signals/me/records/{signal_id}`** for user-scoped rows; optional ledger fields (`closed_at`, `gate_status`, `exit_rule`, MAE/MFE, ‚Ä¶) appear when stored on the row (see **`docs/SIGNAL_ENGINE.md`** ¬ß Signal validation ledger). Responses use `signal_strength`, `disclaimer`, etc. (see Legal section).

## 3. Pending (near-term ops / engineering)

**Deploy checklist (after you push to `main`):** GitHub Actions runs tests, then **`deploy-lambda`** (zip ‚Üí S3 ‚Üí `update-function-code` for every `stocvest-development-api-*` module, including **`signal_resolution`**) and optionally **`deploy-vercel`** (production deploy hook). Full secret/variable names and IAM needs: [root `README.md` ¬ß CI/CD](../README.md#cicd-github-actions).

| Step | Action |
|------|--------|
| 1 | **Terraform:** `cd infra && terraform apply` for the target env so DynamoDB (incl. **`SignalHistory`**, **`TradeJournal`**, **`PDTState`**, **`AuditEvents`**, ‚Ä¶), **every** `api_handler_modules` Lambda (incl. **`signal_resolution`** ‚Üí name `stocvest-development-api-signal_resolution`), API Gateway (incl. **`GET /v1/signals/founding-members`**, admin **beta** / **audit** / **`GET /v1/admin/users/{user_id}/activity-errors`** routes), and Lambda env (**`DYNAMODB_AUDIT_EVENTS_TABLE`**, etc.) exist. CI updates **code** only (`update-function-code`); it does **not** create functions. If Actions fails with `ResourceNotFoundException` for that name, apply Terraform **before** re-running deploy. |
| 2 | **GitHub:** Repository **variable** `STOCVEST_LAMBDA_S3_BUCKET`; **secrets** `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `AWS_REGION`; optional `VERCEL_DEPLOY_HOOK_URL`. |
| 3 | **Push `main`:** Open **Actions** ‚Üí confirm backend, frontend, `deploy-lambda`, and `deploy-vercel` (or skip if hook unset). |
| 4 | **Smoke:** `GET /v1/health` on the HTTP API base URL; optional `GET /v1/signals/recent` if D1 table is applied. |

| 11 | **Tier 1.A dashboard prefetch storm ‚Äî SHIPPED (frontend only) ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change). Direct cause of the user's **16.78s `/dashboard/signals?symbol=AAPL&ref=dashboard-ribbon` request with 14.61s "Content Download"** captured via DevTools on 2026-05-13. Root cause: every `<Link>` in `components/dashboard-active-signal-ribbon.tsx` (ribbon chips + empty-state "Open scanner"), `components/day-desk-panel.tsx` (per-row "Open Day Signals ‚Üí" + footer "View day scanner ‚Üí"), and `components/dashboard-redesign.tsx` (swing-desk footer "View swing scanner ‚Üí") omitted `prefetch={false}`. Next.js 14.2's default `prefetch="auto"` therefore fired one full SSR prefetch per visible link on dashboard mount ‚Äî 5‚Äì10 parallel prefetches of `/dashboard/signals` and `/dashboard/scanner`, each running `fetchPdtStatus` + `fetchMarketOverview` + `fetchScannerOverview` + `fetchEarningsCalendar` server-side just to warm cache for pages nobody asked for. Fix: `prefetch={false}` on every such `<Link>`. Lock-in: `frontend/tests/dashboard-prefetch.test.tsx` (5 tests) with a `next/link` mock that surfaces the prefetch prop as `data-prefetch="‚Ä¶"` so a future regression fails CI loud with a pointer at **`docs/PERFORMANCE.md` ¬ß3.1 + ¬ß4**. |
| 12 | **Tier 1.B streaming Suspense islands on `/dashboard/signals` ‚Äî SHIPPED (frontend only) ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change). Follow-up to row 11: once Tier 1.A killed the dashboard's prefetch storm, the next bottleneck became the signals page's own load. Pre-Tier-1.B, `app/dashboard/signals/page.tsx` `await`-ed `Promise.all([fetchPdtStatus, fetchMarketOverview, fetchScannerOverview])` + sequential `await fetchEarningsCalendar(symbols, 3)` before rendering ANYTHING, so a ribbon-chip click left the previous page's UI frozen for seconds. Refactor: split the page into an outer fast shell (auth + URL parsing + `<AppShell>` chrome) and an inner async server child (`SignalsPageData`) that owns the four heavy fetches; wrap the inner in `<Suspense fallback={<SignalsPageShell />}>`. Added `app/dashboard/signals/loading.tsx` rendering the same shell for the inter-route transition window. The negative half of that invariant is the load-bearing assertion: any future refactor that moves a fetcher back to the outer page fails this test loud with a pointer at `docs/PERFORMANCE.md` ¬ß4B. Frontend baseline now **745 passing tests across 73 files** (was 733/72). |
| 13 | **Layer 4 (first slice) ‚Äî SWR client cache + hover-prefetch ‚Äî SHIPPED (frontend only) ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). Follow-up to rows 11‚Äì12 and the third performance tier shipped today. Decision: **SWR over TanStack Query** ‚Äî SWR is ~5KB vs ~13KB gzipped, has a smaller API surface that exactly fits our Layer-4 use case (pure GET-and-cache), and is authored by Vercel (same shop as Next.js). TanStack Query is reserved for a future feature that needs mutations / optimistic updates / infinite scroll ‚Äî it can co-exist for that surface without rip-out. Added `swr@^2.4.1` to `frontend/package.json`. **New module `frontend/lib/swr/`** with three files: (a) `config.ts` exports `STOCVEST_SWR_DEFAULTS` (the load-bearing defaults `revalidateOnFocus:false` ‚Äî our data isn't tick-by-tick so refetching on every alt-tab burns API budget without adding signal; `revalidateOnReconnect:true` ‚Äî refresh once after a wifi blip ends; `dedupingInterval:30_000` ‚Äî 30s is the sweet spot so rapid clicks across the ribbon don't fan out to N calls for the same symbol; `errorRetryCount:1` ‚Äî Lambdas are mostly stateless so a 5xx is usually a code issue not a flake, retrying 3+ times just makes the user wait longer for the error; `keepPreviousData:true` ‚Äî switching symbols keeps showing the previous symbol's snapshot until the new one resolves, no blank flash; `shouldRetryOnError` predicate **never retries on 401** which would re-fire `surfaceAuthErrorIfAny` and re-surface the session-expired banner ‚Äî the exact UX bug fixed in the prior session-expiry PR) plus the `STOCVEST_SWR_CACHE_NS = "stocvest:"` namespace prefix; (b) `fetcher.ts` exports `swrFetcher<T>(input, init?)` which always sends `credentials:"include"` + `accept:application/json`, throws a typed `SwrFetcherError` carrying status + parsed body on non-2xx, AND fires `surfaceAuthErrorIfAny(response)` on 401 before throwing (so the auth-error banner fires AND SWR's error slot is populated so the hook can render properly); (c) `provider.tsx` exports the client `<StocvestSwrProvider>` wrapping `<SWRConfig>` with defaults + fetcher. Mounted once in `app/layout.tsx` between `<ThemeProvider>` and `<CrispChat>`. **New module `frontend/lib/hooks/`** with two files: (a) `use-symbol-snapshot.ts` exports `useSymbolSnapshot(symbol)` ‚Äî wraps the existing imperative `fetchSymbolSnapshot` (which reads a non-HttpOnly WS token from `document.cookie` and adds a Bearer header ‚Äî keeping that auth plumbing in one place is why we wrap rather than have SWR call the URL directly). Cache key: `["stocvest:symbol-snapshot", upperCaseSymbol]`. Empty/whitespace symbol skips the fetch. Preserves the upstream ticker-mismatch guard from the original effect (upstream sometimes returns a snapshot for a different symbol on ambiguous queries ‚Äî hook returns `null` instead of misleading data). Returns `{ snapshot, isInitialLoading, isRevalidating, error }`. (b) `use-hover-prefetch.ts` exports `useHoverPrefetch(href, options?)` returning `{ onMouseEnter, onFocus, onPointerDown }` handlers ‚Äî each calls `router.prefetch(href)` exactly **once** per hook instance (re-hovering does NOT re-fire); optional `router` override for tests; optional `enabled:false`; errors from `router.prefetch` swallowed (best-effort). **Refactored callsites**: (i) `components/signals-page-client.tsx` dropped the `symbolSnapshot` useState + the `useEffect ‚Üí fetchSymbolSnapshot` block, replaced with `useSymbolSnapshot(symbolForSwr)` where `symbolForSwr` is `""` whenever the market overview already carries the snapshot ‚Äî preserving the original short-circuit. (ii) `components/dashboard-active-signal-ribbon.tsx` extracted `<RibbonChip>` sub-component (each chip calls `useHoverPrefetch(href)` independently without violating Rules of Hooks in a `.map`). Both chips AND empty-state "Open scanner" CTA carry `data-prefetch="false"` (Tier 1.A) AND `data-hover-prefetch="true"` (Layer 4). (iii) `components/day-desk-panel.tsx` added hover-prefetch to both per-row "Open Day Signals ‚Üí" links and the desk footer "View day scanner ‚Üí". (iv) `components/dashboard-redesign.tsx` added hover-prefetch to the swing-desk footer "View swing scanner ‚Üí". **`vitest.setup.ts` now ships a default `next/navigation` mock** so every test that renders a dashboard subtree containing `useHoverPrefetch` works in jsdom without each test file declaring its own ‚Äî six existing tests that explicitly mock `next/navigation` for richer router behaviour continue to win via vitest's hoisting precedence. **The Tier 1.A ‚Üî Layer 4 contract** is now locked in: every heavy-target dashboard `<Link>` carries BOTH `data-prefetch="false"` AND `data-hover-prefetch="true"` ‚Äî no mount-time speculation but warm-on-intent. Lock-in tests: 34 new tests across **5 new files** ‚Äî `tests/swr-config.test.ts` (10 ‚Äî every default pinned individually, retry predicate tested against 401/5xx/4xx-non-401/non-status errors), `tests/swr-fetcher.test.ts` (7 ‚Äî 2xx parses JSON, non-2xx throws `SwrFetcherError`, 401 fires surface helper, 200 doesn't, 500 doesn't, credentials + accept header always sent), `tests/use-symbol-snapshot.test.tsx` (6 ‚Äî empty/whitespace short-circuit, happy path, case + whitespace normalisation, ticker-mismatch guard, SWR dedupe of two hooks for same symbol ‚Üí fetcher called once), `tests/use-hover-prefetch.test.tsx` (6 ‚Äî fires on first onMouseEnter, never re-fires, onFocus/onPointerDown equivalent, null/empty/undefined href no-op, `enabled:false` no-op, swallows router.prefetch throws), `tests/dashboard-hover-prefetch.test.tsx` (5 ‚Äî ribbon chip / ribbon empty-state CTA / day-desk per-row / day-desk footer / swing-desk footer ALL carry BOTH markers; the critical invariant ‚Äî any future PR dropping either marker fails loud with pointer at `docs/PERFORMANCE.md` ¬ß4C). Frontend baseline now **779 passing tests across 78 files** (was 745/73). |
| 14 | **Admin Users empty-pool regression fix + sticky TopBar ‚Äî APPLIED ‚úÖ** **`terraform apply -target='aws_lambda_function.api' -auto-approve`** completed **2026-05-13** (**0 added, 17 changed, 0 destroyed**) ‚Äî every API Lambda picked up three new env vars `COGNITO_USER_POOL_ID=us-east-1_Jl8gQgR2p`, `COGNITO_REGION=us-east-1`, `COGNITO_APP_CLIENT_ID=2ruog68jh83frp7unduufbvgm2`. Commit lands the env wiring + a defense-in-depth backend gate + frontend error-envelope plumbing + a sticky page chrome. **Root cause** of the user's "**No users found in the pool yet.**" screenshot on `/dashboard/admin/users`: the `lambda_common_env` block in `infra/lambda_6e.tf` exported every DynamoDB table name but had never carried the Cognito identifiers, so `settings.cognito_user_pool_id` resolved to `""` inside the brokers Lambda; `admin_user_directory._pool_id()` returned empty; `list_users_page` returned `UserSearchPage(records=[], next_token=None)` from the `if not pool: return UserSearchPage(records=[], next_token=None)` early-out; the BFF round-tripped a 200 with `items: []`; the React empty state rendered the misleading "No users found in the pool yet." copy. **Fix (a) ‚Äî infra**: added `COGNITO_USER_POOL_ID = aws_cognito_user_pool.main.id`, `COGNITO_REGION = var.aws_region`, `COGNITO_APP_CLIENT_ID = aws_cognito_user_pool_client.frontend.id` to `lambda_common_env`. Values are non-secret (already published via `outputs.tf` for the Vercel `NEXT_PUBLIC_*` rails) so they live in the function environment, not in the `stocvest/lambda-runtime` Secrets Manager payload. **Fix (b) ‚Äî backend gate**: new helper `_require_cognito_pool()` in `stocvest/api/handlers/admin_users.py` returns a 503 with body `{ "error":"config_error", "code":"cognito_pool_unset", "message":"‚Ä¶", "hint":"Run `terraform apply` from /infra‚Ä¶" }` whenever `settings.cognito_user_pool_id` is empty, AND logs at `error` level so the misconfig shows up in CloudWatch. Wired into all four admin user handlers (search, detail, reset_password, _mutate_group) **after** `_require_admin()` so a non-admin still gets 403 first (defense-in-depth ordering). `admin_user_directory.list_users_page` keeps the empty-page silent fallback for back-compat (tests + the best-effort admin-system-status tile still call it) but now logs at `error` level too. **Fix (c) ‚Äî frontend error envelope plumbing**: new `readAdminErrorEnvelope(response)` in `frontend/lib/api/admin-users.ts` reads the JSON body on every non-2xx admin response and prefers the backend's `message` / `hint` over the generic `classifyAdminReadStatus` copy. The 503 `cognito_pool_unset` case maps to `code:"not_deployed"` so the existing `AdminApiErrorCard` styles it identically to a 404-route-not-deployed (same "fix the infra" affordance). `searchUsersDiagnostic` and (transitively, in a future tightening) `fetchUserDetail` go through this helper. **Fix (d) ‚Äî sticky page chrome**: previously `<header>` in `components/top-bar.tsx` scrolled away with the body. Two changes together produce sticky behaviour: (i) `<header>` gains `className="sticky top-0 z-30 ‚Ä¶ backdrop-blur-sm ‚Ä¶"` ‚Äî `z-30` sits below modals/drawers at 40+ but above page content, `backdrop-blur-sm` softens content scrolling under the chrome; (ii) `components/app-shell.tsx` right-column wrapper drops the legacy `overflow-x-hidden` (which promoted the wrapper to a scroll container and captured `position: sticky` against itself instead of the viewport) and moves that protection to `<main>` so wide content still cannot blow the column out. The wrapper also gains `data-testid="app-shell-right-column"` and `flex flex-col` to lay out the chrome + scroll content vertically. **Tooling**: `frontend/vitest.config.ts` aliases `server-only` to `tests/mocks/server-only-stub.ts` (an empty file) so test suites that render dashboard chrome whose transitive imports touch `lib/auth/cognito.ts` no longer fail at the `import "server-only";` line. **Lock-in tests**: (i) Python `tests/api/handlers/test_admin_users.py` gains autouse fixture `_cognito_pool_configured` that monkeypatches `_require_cognito_pool` to `lambda: None` so the 23 existing tests don't have to set `cognito_user_pool_id` individually, **plus** three new gate tests at the bottom ‚Äî `test_require_cognito_pool_returns_503_with_actionable_body_when_unset` (uses captured `_REAL_REQUIRE_COGNITO_POOL` to bypass the autouse override and asserts the full body shape: `error:"config_error"`, `code:"cognito_pool_unset"`, message mentions `COGNITO_USER_POOL_ID`, hint mentions `terraform apply`), `test_require_cognito_pool_passes_when_id_is_set`, and a 5-case parametrised `test_admin_handlers_short_circuit_to_503_when_pool_unset` that pins every admin user handler routing through the gate. (ii) New `frontend/tests/admin-users-error-envelope.test.ts` (7 tests) ‚Äî `readAdminErrorEnvelope` 503 ‚Üí not_deployed mapping, generic 5xx with body, body without message/hint, non-JSON body, 404 with body, plus end-to-end `searchUsersDiagnostic` 503 + happy-path. (iii) New `frontend/tests/top-bar-sticky.test.tsx` (3 tests) ‚Äî `<TopBar>` header carries `sticky top-0 z-30`; `<AppShell>` right column does NOT carry `overflow-x-hidden` / `overflow-hidden` / `overflow-auto` / `overflow-y-auto`; `<main>` still carries `overflow-x-hidden`. Backend baseline holds at **257 passing tests in `tests/api/handlers/` + `tests/api/services/test_admin_user_directory.py`** (was 254; +3 gate tests). Frontend baseline now **789 passing tests across 80 files** (was 779/78). **Why this matters operationally**: the previous silent-empty-page failure mode cost a debugging round-trip ‚Äî the new 503 envelope means the next analogous misconfig (Cognito region pinned wrong, new admin route forgets the gate, etc.) surfaces in `AdminApiErrorCard` with an actionable hint instead of as a misleading "no users" empty state. The sticky header keeps page chrome (page title, theme toggle, mobile menu) on screen during long scrolls ‚Äî important on long admin pages and the long dashboard. |
