| 21 | **B35 ‚Äî Evidence Card layer-card refactor (collapse empty layers + compress neutral context + visual-emphasis hierarchy + News-neutral parenthetical) ‚Äî SHIPPED ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (frontend only, no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). Direct follow-up to row 20 ‚Äî closes out the three deeper items (3 / 4 / 6) from the BRK.B second-pass UX polish that were parked as `B35` in `BACKLOG.md` so they could be shipped as one design-coherent refactor rather than bolted onto the surgical fixes. All three live in the same `<section>` in `frontend/components/signal-evidence-card.tsx` ("Signal Layer Breakdown") and share the same data shape (the `EvidenceLayer[]` array), so doing them together avoided three rounds of "this looks weird" rework. **New module `frontend/lib/signal-evidence/layer-emphasis.ts`** (pure, no React, no fetch, no clock ‚Äî all decisions computed from the `EvidenceLayer` shape alone). Five public helpers + one private: (a) `layerEmphasisTier(layer): "primary" \| "secondary" \| "tertiary"` ‚Äî Technical is *always* `primary` (load-bearing layer for action), Sector + Geopolitical default to `tertiary` but promote to `secondary` when `layerHasActiveContent` is true OR status is directional (Bullish/Bearish), every other layer (News / Macro / Internals) renders at `secondary` and demotes to `tertiary` only if `Unavailable`. The constants `PRIMARY_LAYER_KEYS = ["technical"]` and `TERTIARY_DEFAULT_LAYER_KEYS = ["geopolitical", "sector"]` are exported and locked-in with their own membership tests so future "let's also promote internals to primary" rewrites have to delete a test first. (b) `layerHasActiveContent(layer): boolean` ‚Äî per-layer truth table that mirrors what the existing rendering surfaces inline: macro = critical/elevated risk_level with warnings OR any upcoming_events (any status) OR any yield_curve (any regime ‚Äî normal counts because the row renders); news = wim_summary OR upgrade/downgrade/initiates rating OR raised/lowered guidance OR earnings_result.beat != null OR news_data_state==="stale" with 0 articles (the empty-state copy IS content); sector = resolved + data_available with non-zero leading sessions or persistence or daily sessions; geopolitical = any activeEvents OR geoHasLiveEvents OR baseline summary OR exposureSummary OR geoBaselineScore OR geoPrimaryTheme (covers GeoStructuralBaselinePanel cases); internals = ‚â• 2 keyPoints; default = ‚â• 2 keyPoints. Technical is always considered active (the layer never collapses by this helper). Unavailable status is never active. (c) `isLayerCompressible(layer): boolean` ‚Äî true when the layer is Neutral or Unavailable AND has no active content AND is NOT Technical. Compressible layers render only their header (icon + name + status pill) at top level; the explanation + chips + extras are wrapped in a `<details data-testid="layer-{key}-collapsed"><summary>Show evaluation detail</summary>...</details>` disclosure. Directional layers (Bullish/Bearish) never compress. (d) `shouldCompressContextLayers(layers): boolean` ‚Äî strict 3-way gate: News, Macro, AND Geopolitical must ALL be present in the layers array, ALL Neutral, and NONE have active content. Any directional flip or any active extra (FOMC imminent event, baseline summary, earnings beat, etc.) breaks the grouping immediately. (e) `buildCompressedContextSummary(layers): CompressedContextSummary \| null` ‚Äî returns `{ title: "Context", headline: "Neutral (no macro or news tailwinds present)", statusLabel: "Neutral", collapsedLayerKeys: ["news","macro","geopolitical"], layers: [...] }`. Headline copy is deliberately data-only ("no macro or news tailwinds present") ‚Äî never advice-flavored. Returns null if any context layer is missing (defensive ‚Äî caller is supposed to gate on `shouldCompressContextLayers` but the function degrades safely if not). (f) Private `hasNewsPositiveCatalyst(layer): boolean` ‚Äî separates the "is there evidence of continuation?" question from the broader "is there anything to render?" question. (g) `buildNewsNeutralParenthetical(layer): string \| null` ‚Äî returns `"no catalyst support ‚Üí lowers continuation probability"` when News status is Neutral AND `hasNewsPositiveCatalyst` is false (covers the stale+0-articles case AND truly-empty case), null otherwise. The decoupling from `layerHasActiveContent` is critical: the "stale + 0 articles" case renders an empty-state copy ("No qualifying news for ...") that IS content the user needs to see (so the layer isn't compressible), but the absence of a positive catalyst means the parenthetical still fires. Both belong on the card simultaneously ‚Äî the empty-state copy is the data face, the parenthetical is the implication. **Refactored `frontend/components/signal-evidence-card.tsx`** ‚Äî the inline `evidence.layers.map((layer) => <article>...)` block in the Signal Layer Breakdown section is replaced with an IIFE that (1) checks `shouldCompressContextLayers` once at the top, (2) builds the Context summary, (3) walks `evidence.layers` in order; if a layer is in `collapsedLayerKeys` and the Context summary card hasn't been rendered yet, render it ONCE at that position and skip the remaining context layers; otherwise compute `tier` + `compressible` + `newsParen` and render the layer article with tier-based visual overrides. Tier overrides come from a new helper `tierVisualOverrides(tier)` co-located with `elevatedCardStyle`: `primary` ‚Üí padding `spacing[4]` (1rem), fontScale `base`, opacity 1, header weight 700; `secondary` ‚Üí padding `spacing[3]` (current default), fontScale `sm`, opacity 1, weight 600; `tertiary` ‚Üí padding `spacing[2]` (compact), fontScale `xs`, opacity 0.82 (still readable on dark surface), weight 600. The article carries `data-testid="layer-card-{key}"` + `data-layer-tier="{primary\|secondary\|tertiary}"` + `data-layer-compressible="{true\|false}"` for test stability. The News-neutral parenthetical renders as a small italic span between the header row and the body (always visible even when the body is collapsed inside `<details>`), with `data-testid="layer-news-neutral-parenthetical"`. The compressed Context card carries `data-testid="layer-compressed-context"` + `data-collapsed-layer-keys="news,macro,geopolitical"` + a `<details data-testid="layer-compressed-context-details"><summary>Show News, Macro, and Geopolitical layer detail</summary><div>three mini-summary panels</div></details>` disclosure. The inner mini-summaries (`data-testid="layer-compressed-context-inner-{news\|macro\|geopolitical}"`) render only the icon + name + status pill + one-line explanation ‚Äî they intentionally do NOT re-render the full per-layer panels (yield-curve row, sector momentum, geo baseline panel, etc.) because (a) the whole point of compression is reducing visual noise, and (b) the activity check is broad enough that any layer with rich extras is no longer "compressible" anyway ‚Üí the standalone card renders instead. **Test posture ‚Äî +14 new helpers tests + +12 render-level tests = 26 new lock-ins in two new files**: `frontend/tests/layer-emphasis.test.ts` (76 tests total) covers every helper exhaustively ‚Äî constants membership; tier assignment for every layer key √ó status combination; promotion rules for sector/geopolitical (active content OR directional status); per-layer activity truth tables including the new "stale+0 articles is active" rule for news + "any yield_curve regime is active" for macro + "any layer.geo with narrative is active" for geopolitical; isLayerCompressible never collapses Technical; shouldCompressContextLayers strict 3-way gating with BRK.B regression test; buildCompressedContextSummary payload shape + headline copy hygiene; buildNewsNeutralParenthetical decoupled from active-content (stale+0 STILL returns parenthetical) + suppressed by every flavor of positive catalyst. `frontend/tests/signal-evidence-card-layer-hierarchy.test.tsx` (12 tests) covers the render-level invariants ‚Äî BRK.B regression "three neutral context layers compress into Context card"; one-layer-bullish-or-active breaks compression; News-neutral parenthetical renders alongside standalone News=Neutral cards (gated on a directional macro to break compression so news renders standalone); parenthetical suppressed when News is Bullish or has earnings beat; Technical always renders at primary tier and never compressible; Sector at tertiary and compressible by default; Internals at secondary; summary disclosure copy locked. **Focused-run verified**: `npx vitest run tests/layer-emphasis.test.ts tests/signal-evidence-card-layer-hierarchy.test.tsx tests/signal-evidence.test.ts tests/signal-evidence-layers.test.ts tests/why-hold-copy.test.ts tests/conflict-chip-ranking.test.ts tests/scenario-eligibility.test.ts` ‚Üí **240/240 PASSED** in ~52s (7 files including the seven adjacent suites most likely to regress from a layer-card refactor). Two existing tests in `signal-evidence.test.ts` ("yield curve normal shows green" + "upcoming events listed") needed the activity-check broadening for macro to keep passing ‚Äî those fixtures specify only the macro layer so news/geo defaulted to Neutral and the previous narrow activity check ate the macro yield-curve panel by folding it into the compressed Context card. The fix was correct (a yield-curve row IS content; an upcoming event IS content) and the lock-in `test_macro_normal_yield_curve_is_active` + `test_macro_any_upcoming_event_is_active_even_when_status_is_upcoming` tests in `layer-emphasis.test.ts` pin the new semantics. Three existing tests in `signal-evidence-layers.test.ts` ("geo baseline panel when no live events" / "geo baseline high band renders" / "news stale empty state wording") needed the broader news + geo activity checks for the same reason. Frontend full-suite re-run **89/89 files PASSED, 970/970 tests PASSED** (confirmed prior to commit). **Why this matters operationally**: this pass closes the loop on the BRK.B feedback round entirely. Items 1/2/5 shipped in row 20 (Build Scenario gating, "Why hold" copy, ranked conflict chips); items 3/4/6 ship here (collapse empty layers, compress neutral context, emphasis hierarchy). The BRK.B card the user originally screenshotted had News + Macro + Geopolitical all rendering as full-size cards each saying "Neutral" with no qualifier ‚Äî three rows of decision fatigue producing zero information. The same card now renders ONE consolidated `"Context: Neutral (no macro or news tailwinds present)"` row with a disclosure to peek at the three sub-layers, AND the News chip (when standalone elsewhere) carries the soft-negative reframing `"no catalyst support ‚Üí lowers continuation probability"` so users understand that "neutral news" on a short-term setup is a soft headwind, not a no-op. The visual hierarchy promotes Technical (the layer that decides the Decision line) to clearly the biggest card on screen and demotes Sector + Geopolitical to muted tertiary cards UNLESS they have active content, eliminating the "every layer looks equally important even when most are saying nothing" UX problem. Pure helpers + tier-driven styling mean future product decisions (e.g. promoting Internals to primary for confluence-heavy setups, or adding a fourth context layer) only require updating the constants ‚Äî the render path stays unchanged. Backend test baseline unchanged. Frontend test baseline +26 (2 new files: `layer-emphasis.test.ts` and `signal-evidence-card-layer-hierarchy.test.tsx`). |
| 20 | **BRK.B Evidence Card ‚Äî second-pass UX polish (Build Scenario gating + Why-hold copy + ranked conflict chips) ‚Äî SHIPPED ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (frontend + assistant-prompt only, no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). User filed a 6-issue follow-up bug report on the BRK.B card after the row-19 stale-bars fix landed; this pass ships the **three surgical, locally-scoped fixes** (items 1, 2, 5) and parks the deeper layer-card refactor (items 3, 4, 6 ‚Äî collapse empty layers, compress neutral context into one row, visual-emphasis hierarchy) as **B35** in `BACKLOG.md` so the next pass can do them as one focused refactor instead of bolting them onto the same commit. **Fix (1) ‚Äî Build Scenario button gating at R/R < 2.0**: in the screenshot the button was clickable even though the Decision line read "Monitor only ‚Äî confirmation and/or risk gates are not fully cleared" and the R/R card read "0.5:1 ‚Äî Low R/R - below 2:1". Root cause was a deliberate omission: `frontend/lib/scenario/eligibility.ts` is documented to gate on structural completeness **only** (never on conviction signals ‚Äî confluence, accuracy, layer alignment, engine verdict), and R/R was historically lumped in with "conviction." That call was wrong on inspection: R/R is pure entry/stop/target arithmetic on the reference levels the signal already carries, NOT a quality verdict. A 0.5:1 sheet plans to lose more than it stands to gain, which is not a coherent **structural** planning sheet regardless of how strong other signal layers are. Fix added `risk_reward?: number \| null` to `ScenarioInput` with a multi-paragraph explanatory comment, added `low_risk_reward` to `SCENARIO_INELIGIBILITY_REASONS`, added the gate (`rr > 0 && rr < 2.0` ‚Äî defensive on missing/non-finite/zero/negative, only fires when the field is a positive finite number below threshold) inside `isEligibleForScenario`, and added the user-facing label `"Risk/reward does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building."` Threshold matches `synthTradeDecision::rrFail` (2.0) so the Build Scenario button is now in lock-step with the Decision line on the same card ‚Äî they can never disagree on whether the setup clears the R/R gate. Wired `risk_reward: insight.risk_reward` into the evidence-card call site (the only path with access to the engine's computed R/R); gap card + setup row call sites in `scanner-page-client.tsx` are intentionally unchanged because their source payloads don't carry R/R (the field stays `undefined` ‚Üí defensive path doesn't gate). **Fix (2) ‚Äî "Why hold:" / "Why blocked:" copy rewrite to drop "trade permission" language**: the previous wording threaded `"STOCVEST ‚Ä¶ before granting trade permission"` through every rationale variant in `deriveDecisionRationale`. Users read that phrase as STOCVEST claiming gatekeeper authority over their trade decisions ‚Äî which is exactly the implication our legal posture is built to avoid. STOCVEST does NOT grant or withhold trade permission; we surface signal data and the user decides. All five rationale variants rewritten with one unified framing ‚Äî `"The setup does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building"` ‚Äî so the gate is described as an internal numerical threshold on whether the platform will scaffold a Scenario Builder sheet, never as a verdict on the trade itself. New copy by category: **risk_reward** ‚Üí `"Risk/reward (X.X:1) does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building."` **data_insufficient** ‚Üí `"Layer coverage is too thin to evaluate this setup with conviction. The setup does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building until additional layers populate."` **confirmation** ‚Üí `"Layer agreement is mixed across the six signal layers. The setup does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building until directional confirmation strengthens."` **regime** ‚Üí `"Macro or regime context conflicts with this direction. The setup does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building while regime alignment is opposed."` **readiness** ‚Üí `"Signal readiness is not yet decisive across the six layers. The setup does not meet internal thresholds for structured scenario building."` Also rewrote the one matching example in `stocvest/signals/assistant_prompts.py` line 452 so the chatbot speaks the same vocabulary. **Fix (5) ‚Äî Conflicting signal chip rail ranked Primary / Secondary / Tertiary**: in the BRK.B screenshot the conflicting chips arrived in source-order `[EMA conflict, VWAP conflict, Weak volume]` and the user couldn't tell which one was load-bearing. Added a canonical priority order `CONFLICT_PRIORITY_BY_SOURCE` in `frontend/lib/signal-evidence.ts` ‚Äî `vwap_position=1 > volume_confirm=2 > ema_9_position=3 > internals_alignment=4 > sector_alignment=5 > market_regime=6 > news_catalyst=7 > gap_confirm=8 > orb_breakout=9` ‚Äî encoding "what does the user need to know first when assessing the friction on this setup": technical / execution-quality anchors first, broad-market context after, discrete catalysts and entry-timing signals last. New helper `rankConflictingSignals<T extends { source?: string }>(chips)` returns a stably-sorted copy (equal-priority chips keep arrival order via index pairing) without mutating the input; unknown sources sort to the tail with `Number.POSITIVE_INFINITY` so future chip types degrade gracefully. New helper `conflictTierLabel(index, total)` returns `"PRIMARY" \| "SECONDARY" \| "TERTIARY" \| null` ‚Äî null when total < 2 (a single conflict needs no tier label because there is nothing to rank against) or when index > 2 (only the top three get a label). Frontend `mapConfluenceChipList` updated to pass the backend's `source` enum through to the chip type (was being dropped); the setup-derived path in `buildEvidenceFromSetupRow` updated for the same reason. The evidence-card render in `signal-evidence-card.tsx` now sorts the conflicting chips via `rankConflictingSignals` and renders a small tier badge inside the first three pills ‚Äî uppercase, fontSize 9, letterSpacing 0.6, padded with a translucent red background so it visually sits "inside" the pill without overpowering the chip label. Confirming chips deliberately keep their natural order (they are co-equal anchors of the setup, not a ranked list ‚Äî the user only asked for ranking on the conflicts). Carried `data-testid="conflict-chip-{primary\|secondary\|tertiary}"` + `data-conflict-tier` + `data-conflict-source` attributes on each ranked chip for test stability. **Lock-in tests ‚Äî +73 new across three files**: `frontend/tests/scenario-eligibility.test.ts` gains a `low risk/reward gate (BRK.B feedback, 2026-05-13)` describe block with 10 tests covering rr-below-2 fails, **rr=0.5 BRK.B regression**, rr-at-threshold 2.0 passes, rr=3.0 passes, rr=1.8 fails, missing field does not gate, null does not gate, NaN does not gate, zero/negative does not gate (treated as unknown not low), AND a copy-hygiene test asserting the label uses the internal-thresholds framing and forbids the legacy "trade permission"/"approved" wording. The existing `test_eligibility_input_shape_has_no_conviction_fields` test was extended to allow `risk_reward` in the input shape with an explanatory comment naming this incident by date. | 19 | **BRK.B Evidence Card ‚Äî catastrophic stale-bars root cause + 4 user-reported issues ‚Äî SHIPPED ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). User filed a 5-issue bug report against the BRK.B evidence card (VWAP/EMA chip polarity backwards, broken reconciler grammar, $50.36 VWAP on a stock that trades at $485, internals-bullish counter-signal invisible in the chip rail, AI Signal Analysis section empty) and explicitly asked for "a thorough audit to make sure there are no more bugs in the code". **Root cause** turned out to be a single catastrophic bug in `stocvest/data/polygon_client.py::get_bars` that was poisoning every technical computation in production: the function defaulted `from_date="2000-01-01"` (with a comment claiming "Polygon ignores if limit is set" ‚Äî wrong) and sent `sort=asc&limit=N`, which Polygon honors by returning the **OLDEST** N bars in the range. Live probe before the fix: `get_bars('BRK.B', MIN_1, limit=60)` returned 60 minute bars from **2003-09-10** (close ~$50, the post-2010-split BRK.B price), and `get_bars('BRK.B', DAY_1, limit=210)` returned 210 daily bars from 2003-09-10 through 2004-07-12. **Every technical layer in production** (SMA50, SMA200, RSI, MACD, VWAP, EMAs, golden/death cross, ATR, volatility regime, breakout detection, base-formation) was therefore running against **22-year-old prices**. This is the actual reason the user saw VWAP $50.36 on BRK.B: the day-trade engine's TechnicalAnalyzer computed VWAP from minute bars from 2003. The hidden second-order effect ‚Äî and what made this so hard to spot ‚Äî was that the technical analyzer compared the analyzer-computed historical SMA50 (~$59 from 2003 BRK.B) to today's snapshot price ($485) and trivially decided "price above SMA50" ‚Üí bullish bias on basically every name in the system, regardless of actual current technical structure. **Fix (a) ‚Äî `polygon_client.get_bars` semantics split** into two explicit modes: "recent N bars" (both `from_date` and `to_date` are `None`) now sends `sort=desc` to Polygon and **reverses the results in Python** before returning so every downstream analyzer still receives bars in the oldest-first chronological order they all assume (SMA windows, RSI seed, MACD seed all walk forward by index). "Explicit date range" (caller pinned at least one edge ‚Äî `sector_daily_cache` for a trailing 7-day audit, `orb_compute_worker` for a single trading day, the public `/v1/bars` handler when a user supplies `from`/`to` query params) keeps `sort=asc` so oldest-within-window callers are unchanged. Partial-edge calls (only one of from/to) are conservatively treated as range mode to avoid surprising callers who pinned one edge. The new behaviour is locked in with a multi-paragraph docstring inside `get_bars` that names this incident by date so a future refactor cannot silently revert. **Live verification post-fix** ‚Äî `get_bars('BRK.B', MIN_1, limit=60)` now returns bars 2026-05-13 19:24 through 21:41 UTC (today's actual session); `get_bars('BRK.B', DAY_1, limit=210)` returns bars 2025-07-10 through 2026-05-13. **End-to-end engine smoke** post-fix on BRK.B: swing now reads SMA50=$479.58, SMA200=$489.78 (the actual recent values ‚Äî was $59.35 / $57.88 before fix); both engines now correctly report BRK.B verdict=**neutral** (was bearish/short with score 40 in the user's screenshot ‚Äî that "short signal" was entirely an artifact of comparing today's $485 price to 2003's $50ish VWAP). **Fix (b) ‚Äî Issue 4, internals chip in confluence**: added `internals_alignment` chip to `stocvest/signals/confluence.py` and wired both composite engines to pass `internals_signal=normalize_direction(internals.verdict)`. Mirror of the sector-chip design from row 16: chip label describes the broad-market state intrinsically (`"Internals bullish"` / `"Internals bearish"`), placement in confirming vs conflicting is decided by setup direction. A bullish broad market on a short setup now lands in `conflicting_signals` with detail "Breadth and participation broadly up ‚Äî broad market is rising." ‚Äî exactly the counter-signal that was invisible in the user's screenshot. Backwards-compatible: `internals_signal` parameter defaults to `"neutral"` so `signal_dto.py` and `/v1/signals/composite` callers that don't pass it still work (they just don't emit the chip). **Fix (c) ‚Äî Issue 2, reconciler text shape** in `frontend/lib/signal-evidence.ts::buildVerdictTagReconciler`: rewrote the sentence to lead with the anchor list instead of the opposite-polarity context. New shape: `"Anchored by X and Y; counterweight(s): Z."` (singular "counterweight" when only one). No-anchor fallback: `"No confirming signals for the {short|long} setup; only opposing context: ‚Ä¶"` (now direction-aware). The old "Bullish-leaning context present (X, Y, Z), but the setup is anchored by W" wording is permanently retired ‚Äî three anti-regression `not.toMatch` assertions guard it across the test file. **Fix (d) ‚Äî Issue 5, AI Signal Analysis empty state** in `frontend/components/signal-evidence-card.tsx`: hardened `captureDisplayText` with a three-tier fallback chain ‚Äî (1) live/cached Anthropic capture text ‚Üí (2) `evidence.aiVerdict` (the deterministic hardcoded direction-keyed sentence built by `buildEvidenceFromSetup`) ‚Üí (3) an on-the-fly direction-aware sentence (`"{SYMBOL} setup leans {bullish\|bearish} based on layer agreement. Open Evidence for layer detail."`) so the italic quote block under the "AI Signal Analysis" header never renders as empty `""` even if the BFF route or Anthropic call fails entirely. Also removed the dangling `<span>Signal summary</span>` caption that had no value bound to it (just a label rendered next to a freshness timestamp) ‚Äî users were reading it as "Signal summary: (blank)" and reporting it as a defect. **Issue 1 (VWAP/EMA chip polarity)** turned out to NOT be a separate bug: the chip logic in `confluence.py` is already direction-aware (`if direction == "long" and price > vwap` ‚Üí confirming; `elif direction == "short" and price < vwap` ‚Üí confirming; else ‚Üí conflicting). The user's observation was caused by Issue 3 ‚Äî the technical analyzer's display string (computed from 2003 minute bars) said "Price below VWAP $50.36" while confluence (using today's snapshot day_vwap) saw price > vwap and correctly emitted "VWAP conflict" ‚Äî they disagreed only because their data sources disagreed, which is now impossible with the get_bars fix. **Issue 3** (catastrophic VWAP $50.36 value) is fully explained by and resolved by Fix (a). **Broader audit** the user explicitly asked for: walked every `get_bars` caller in the codebase (`swing_composite_engine`, `real_composite_engine`, `market_data` handlers, `sector_daily_cache`, `orb_compute_worker`, `scanner_scheduled_pipeline`, `polygon_client` itself) ‚Äî every case-A caller (no dates) benefits from the fix; every case-B caller (explicit dates) preserves behaviour. Audited `get_evaluated_price_after_signal` separately ‚Äî that function uses explicit timestamp ranges and was never affected. Verified `historical_validation` doesn't go through `get_bars`. Verified all chip-generation code paths in `confluence.py` are direction-aware (ORB, VWAP, EMA9, regime, sector, internals, volume, news, gap). **Lock-in tests ‚Äî +11 new across two files**: `tests/data/test_polygon_client.py` gains 3 tests under "Recency / sort regression (BRK-B Issue 3 fix, 2026-05-13)" ‚Äî `test_recent_mode_sends_sort_desc_and_returns_oldest_first` (asserts the wire param `sort=desc` AND the caller-facing list is sorted ascending), `test_explicit_date_range_keeps_sort_asc` (asserts both-edges-pinned still uses `sort=asc`), `test_partial_dates_still_treated_as_range_mode` (asserts one-edge-pinned is conservatively `sort=asc` too). `tests/signals/test_confluence.py` gains 7 tests under "Internals-alignment chip invariants (BRK-B Issue 4 fix, 2026-05-13)" ‚Äî long+bullish-internals lands in confirming, short+bearish-internals lands in confirming, **`test_internals_bullish_on_short_setup_lands_in_conflicting_BRK_B_regression`** (direct regression for the user's reported case), long+bearish-internals lands in conflicting, neutral internals emits no chip, default-argument back-compat, `internals_alignment` listed in `ConfluenceDetector.SIGNAL_SOURCES`. Frontend `tests/signal-evidence.test.ts` reconciler `describe` block fully rewritten ‚Äî 9 tests covering anchor-first shape on both directions, singular vs plural counterweight label, no-conflicting-chips ‚Üí null, no-confirming-chips fallback with direction word, neutral verdict ‚Üí null, parenthetical stripping, geopolitical-drag splicing, geopolitical de-dupe, and the BRK.B-specific regression with `Internals bullish` in the counterweights list. Plus the rendered-card test (`SignalEvidenceCard verdict-tag reconciler rendering`) updated to seed the BRK.B chip layout the engines now actually emit (`confirming=[Sector lags market]`, `conflicting=[Internals bullish, Weak Volume]`) and assert the new anchor-first sentence renders with three anti-regression `not.toMatch` guards on every prior phrasing. **Test posture**: focused runs verified ‚Äî `pytest tests/data/test_polygon_client.py::TestGetBars` 7/7 PASSED in 3.49s; `pytest tests/signals/test_confluence.py` 34/34 PASSED in 2.87s (was 27, +7 internals); `pytest tests/signals/ tests/api/test_class_share_symbol_normalization.py tests/data/test_polygon_client.py -x -q` 569/569 PASSED in 39.22s (full signals + symbol-normalization + polygon-client surface no-regression); `pytest tests/api/test_real_composite.py tests/api/test_swing_composite.py tests/api/test_swing_composite_evidence.py tests/signals/test_composite_score.py tests/signals/test_composite_scorer.py tests/api/handlers/test_signals.py -x -q` 62/62 PASSED in 17.27s; frontend `npx vitest run tests/signal-evidence.test.ts` 74/74 PASSED; broader frontend smoke across 5 related files 123/123 PASSED. Every technical-layer score and every chip rail on every evidence card in production has been computed against 2003-era prices since the engine was first written. The bullish-everything bias the user has been reporting for weeks (and was being attributed to other causes) was almost entirely a product of "today's price > 2003 price" being trivially true. With the fix, layer outputs are finally honest ‚Äî BRK.B day-trade goes from a misleading "short" signal to "neutral" (which is what the actual chart reads as), and we should expect a wave of similar honest-truth corrections across other names. | 18 | **SPY/QQQ/IWM Shared Context tiles ‚Äî line sparkline ‚Üí signed 5-bar daily-returns histogram ‚Äî SHIPPED ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (frontend only, no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). Direct response to the user's question on the dashboard SPY/QQQ/IWM macro strip: "do you think this line graph is good or how about a small horizontal bar graph 5 bars indicating each day. If they go -ve, it should be shown in red on the other direction." **Decision**: the bar histogram wins at this card size. **Why**: the tile is roughly 120px wide; a line sparkline at that resolution conveys direction-only and the headline % label (`+1.19%` etc.) already covers that. The sparkline was filling space without adding information. 5 colored daily-delta bars instead expose the *shape* of the move ‚Äî "three down days followed by two strong up days" produces the same +1.19% net as "five tiny up days in a row" but they are completely different tape characters, and only the bar viz makes that distinction legible. **Changes**: (a) New component `frontend/components/index-returns-histogram.tsx` (~140 lines, pure SVG, no chart library). Component derives daily returns from consecutive close pairs (N closes ‚Üí N ‚àí 1 bars), per-card magnitude scaling (tallest bar fills the half-canvas budget independent of the other tiles ‚Äî cross-tile magnitude comparison lives in the % label, not in the bars), bars sit above/below a faint zero baseline so polarity is positional *as well as* chromatic (colorblind-safe positional encoding ‚Äî up bars grow upward from the baseline, down bars hang downward), color via `getChangeColor(returnPct, colors)` reusing the existing dashboard role-color vocabulary with the same ¬±0.1% neutral band as the % label next to the histogram (one source of truth for color invariants ‚Äî no new palette entries). Near-flat sessions inside the ¬±0.1% band render a 1px-tall stub straddling the baseline so the day count is preserved (we never silently drop a session). Each bar carries a `<title>` child describing "Session N: +X.YZ%" for screen-reader / hover-tooltip access. (b) `frontend/components/dashboard-page-content.tsx::buildWeeklyRows` ‚Äî bumped the `closes5d` slice from `closes.slice(-5)` to `closes.slice(-6)` so the histogram has 5 daily returns to render (6 closes ‚Üí 5 close-to-close returns ‚Üí 5 bars, one per regular trading session over the trailing week). Field name kept as `closes5d` because the *labelled window* is the 5-day window, not the array length. Defensive: when fewer than 6 closes are available, the histogram renders whatever bars the data supports (4 from 5 closes, 3 from 4, etc.) ‚Äî never throws. (c) `frontend/components/shared-context-master-card.tsx` ‚Äî swapped `IndexSparkline` import + render for `IndexReturnsHistogram`, updated aria-label from "5-session close trajectory" to "5-session daily returns histogram". (d) `IndexSparkline` (line viz) is intentionally **kept** in `frontend/components/index-sparkline.tsx` ‚Äî the dashboard hero-strip VIX intraday tile still uses it (different use case: smooth intraday curve over many points within a single session, not 5 discrete daily closes). Pinning that boundary explicitly so a future refactor doesn't accidentally delete the line component. **Lock-in tests ‚Äî +18 new in `frontend/tests/index-returns-histogram.test.tsx`** across five `describe` blocks: *bar count + axis* (N ‚àí 1 bars from N closes, 4 bars from 5 closes defensive case, nothing renders for <2 closes / empty, non-finite/zero/negative stripped before computing returns, zero-line baseline rendered), *polarity (color + position)* (positive ‚Üí `data-sign="up"` + fill differs from negative, negative ‚Üí `data-sign="down"` and bar Y at-or-below baseline, positive ‚Üí bar TOP strictly above baseline, near-flat ¬±0.1% ‚Üí `data-sign="flat"` + 1px stub, five-bar mixed week renders each polarity correctly), *magnitude scaling* (larger |%| ‚Üí taller bar, tallest bar bounded by half-canvas budget), *accessibility* (custom aria-label, default aria-label, per-bar `<title>` describing the session return), *anti-regression* (renders `<rect>` not `<polyline>` ‚Äî line viz is gone from this surface; does NOT mount under the old `data-testid="index-sparkline"` ‚Äî anti-rename guard). **Updated existing test** `frontend/tests/dashboard-role-color-language.test.tsx::section_A_renders_three_index_tiles_each_with_a_sparkline` ‚Üí renamed to `section_A_renders_three_index_tiles_each_with_a_daily_returns_histogram`; assertions switched from `polyline` ‚âÝ null to `rect`-count > 0; added anti-regression that the old `data-testid="index-sparkline"` is NOT in any Section A tile. Existing fixture's 5-close `closes5d` array now produces 4 bars (defensive case), which still satisfies "> 0 bars". **Focused-run verified**: 39 tests / 2 files (18 new histogram lock-ins + 21 existing role-color-language tests) all green. **Adjacent test smoke** ‚Äî `tests/dashboard-hero-strip.test.tsx` (VIX intraday line still uses `IndexSparkline`) + `tests/shared-context-derivations.test.ts` + `tests/dashboard-two-desk.test.tsx` 63 tests / 3 files all green. **Why this matters operationally**: the macro strip is the first thing every user looks at on the dashboard load ‚Äî making the 120px of canvas in each tile carry more information density is a high-leverage UX upgrade for a tiny diff. Pattern is also reusable: any future "5-day return at thumbnail size" surface (watchlist row, scanner result card, signal evidence card historical context) can drop in `<IndexReturnsHistogram closes={...} />` and inherit the same color/position invariants. Full frontend suite re-verification pending end-of-day per the user's "do not run all tests now" instruction. |
| 17 | **Class-share dash-form symbol normalization (BRK-B ‚Üí BRK.B) at every Polygon boundary ‚Äî SHIPPED ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). Direct follow-up to the BRK-B evidence-card investigation in row 16. While verifying the reconciler/sector-chip fix end-to-end I ran BRK-B through both composite engines against the live deployed Polygon REST surface and discovered a second, deeper bug that fully explains the bizarre "Sector Bearish" + non-actionable signal the user originally screenshotted. **Live probe on 2026-05-13** (`GET https://api.polygon.io/v2/...`): `GET /v2/aggs/ticker/BRK-B/range/1/day/...` ‚Üí `results=[]` (silent ‚Äî Polygon returns HTTP 200 with an empty array, NOT a 404, so the call doesn't even raise); `GET /v2/aggs/ticker/BRK.B/range/1/day/...` ‚Üí 10 bars; `GET /v2/snapshot/locale/us/markets/stocks/tickers/BRK-B` ‚Üí `404 NotFound`; `GET /v2/snapshot/locale/us/markets/stocks/tickers/BRK.B` ‚Üí 200 OK. **Root cause**: the swing + real (day-trade) composite engines did `sym = symbol.strip().upper()` and then handed that string verbatim to every Polygon call inside `asyncio.gather(..., return_exceptions=True)`. The snapshot 404 became a silent swallowed exception (gather suppresses it); the bars endpoint returned `0 results` without raising. The downstream layer cascade in `build_swing_composite_response` / `run_real_composite_engine_phase` saw `bars=[]` and `sym_snap=None`, then: (a) `TechnicalAnalyzer` short-circuits to `status="unavailable"` when daily history is below the 60-bar swing floor; (b) `sector_layer_api_extras` short-circuits to `status="unavailable"` when either `sym_snap` or `spy_snap` is None (sector resolution can't run without an SIC lookup ‚Üí can't resolve sector ETF ‚Üí can't compute relative strength); (c) the remaining macro / news / geopolitical / internals layers still scored normally and the composite-score engine averaged them into a neutral-ish 50/100. End result: a user typing `BRK-B` in the search box got a permanently-degraded "incomplete" composite with two layers blank-rendered, while the *exact same engine* fed the same symbol in dot form returned a fully-scored verdict. The deprecated scanner universe in `stocvest/data/scanner_universe.py` already used `BRK.B`/`BRK.A` (dot form), which is why the scanner path never tripped this ‚Äî only the user-typed-search path exposed the bug. **Fix**: new module `stocvest/data/symbol_normalize.py` exporting `to_polygon_symbol(sym: str) -> str`. Rule is deliberately conservative ‚Äî only the class-share dash pattern (regex `^([A-Z]+)-([A-Z])$`, single trailing letter) gets rewritten with a dot. Everything else (preferred shares with multi-letter suffixes like `JPM-PRD`, index symbols like `I:VIX`, legacy `^VIX`, normal tickers like `AAPL`) passes through untouched so the helper does not accidentally mangle anything Polygon happens to accept in a different form. Idempotent (already-canonical `BRK.B` returns unchanged), safe on empty string. **Applied at two call sites only** ‚Äî both composite engine entry points: `stocvest/api/services/swing_composite_engine.py::build_swing_composite_response` (replaced the `sym = symbol.strip().upper()` line with `sym = to_polygon_symbol(symbol)`) and `stocvest/api/services/real_composite_engine.py` at both `build_real_composite_response` and `run_real_composite_engine_phase` (defensive belt-and-braces ‚Äî `run_real_composite_engine_phase` is also exported and imported from at least one other call site, so it gets its own normalization independent of `build_real_composite_response`'s wrapper). The Polygon client itself stays unchanged ‚Äî normalization at the engine boundary is sufficient and keeps `PolygonClient` a thin transport layer. The response payload now surfaces the canonical (Polygon) form everywhere (`"symbol": "BRK.B"`), which matches the universe convention already used elsewhere; the UI/typeahead is free to accept either form on the input side. **Lock-in tests ‚Äî +23 across two new files**: `tests/data/test_symbol_normalize.py` (20 unit tests parametrised across the rewrite cases ‚Äî BRK-B, BRK-A, RDS-A, BF-B, HEI-A ‚Äî and the leave-alone cases ‚Äî AAPL, MSFT, SPY, XLF, BRK.B, BRK.A, I:VIX, ^VIX, JPM-PRD, GS-PRJ, FOO-BAR, A-BC ‚Äî plus strip-and-upper, idempotency, empty input); `tests/api/test_class_share_symbol_normalization.py` (3 engine-level regression tests built on a custom `_RecordingPoly` fake that records the symbol form passed to every Polygon method ‚Äî `test_swing_engine_canonicalises_class_share_dash_at_entry` asserts every captured `get_bars` / `get_snapshot` / `get_market_news` call sees `BRK.B`, never `BRK-B`, AND that the response field `"symbol"` is the canonical form, AND that the composite is not collapsed to `insufficient_data`; `test_real_engine_canonicalises_class_share_dash_at_entry` is the symmetric day-trade variant; `test_swing_engine_leaves_normal_symbols_unchanged` is the hygiene smoke check pinning that `AAPL` survives the normalizer). **Live end-to-end verification (against deployed Polygon)** post-fix: swing `BRK-B` ‚Üí `symbol='BRK.B'`, `status='active'`, `verdict='bullish'`, `score=63` (bit-for-bit identical to the `BRK.B` direct run earlier in the session); day `BRK-B` ‚Üí `symbol='BRK.B'`, `status='active'`, `verdict='bearish'`, `score=40` (bit-for-bit identical). The new sector chip from row 16 renders correctly in both: swing ‚Üí `‚úì Sector leads market` (XLF +1.09% vs SPY -0.62% over 5d, sector_alignment confirming for the long); day ‚Üí `‚úì Sector lags market` (XLF -1.03% vs SPY +0.65% over 1d, sector_alignment confirming for the short) ‚Äî the symmetric mirror, exactly as the test_sector_chip_symmetry_invariant test pins. **Why this matters operationally**: the dash form is what a Bloomberg-trained user types by reflex (`BRK-B`/`RDS-A`/`BF-B` are the standard wire-service notations). Without normalization the engine produced silently-degraded results on these symbols ‚Äî no error, no warning, just two layers missing and a meaningless neutral score. The pre-existing scanner-universe-only path masked the bug from automated regression coverage. Future symbols that exhibit similar dash/dot quirks (preferred-share variants, ADR class shares) can be added to `to_polygon_symbol` with one regex extension and one parametrised test case ‚Äî the wrapper is co-located with the rule. Backend baseline now **1410 passing** (+23 over the 1387 baseline from row 16) ‚Äî verified by `pytest tests/data/test_symbol_normalize.py tests/api/test_class_share_symbol_normalization.py -v` (23/23 PASSED in 11.11s) plus the related `tests/api/test_swing_composite.py` + `tests/signals/test_confluence.py` re-run (31/31 PASSED in 13.70s) as a no-regression check on the engines I touched. |
| 16 | **BRK-B evidence card ‚Äî reconciler-text contradiction + sector-chip relative-strength relabel ‚Äî SHIPPED ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change ‚Äî pure copy + label fixes). Two coupled bugs the user surfaced on the BRK-B Evidence card. **Bug A ‚Äî reconciler contradiction**: `frontend/lib/signal-evidence.ts::buildVerdictTagReconciler` produced "Bullish inputs present, but overridden by VWAP conflict + EMA conflict + Weak Volume" on a short setup whose only confirming chip was bearish-aligned (originally "Sector Bearish"). The previous reconciler hard-coded "Bullish inputs" for the confirming list irrespective of setup direction; on a short setup, the confirming list is bearish-aligned by construction, so the sentence read as a logical contradiction. **Fix**: the reconciler now (i) describes the **conflicting** list's opposite-polarity context correctly ‚Äî "Bullish-leaning context present (‚Ä¶)" for a short setup, "Bearish-leaning context present (‚Ä¶)" for a long setup; (ii) names what's still anchoring the setup ‚Äî "but the setup is anchored by ‚Ä¶" ‚Äî using the confirming-chip labels verbatim; (iii) handles the no-confirming-chips case with a calmer "no opposing chips support the setup" tail; (iv) returns `null` on neutral direction or empty conflicting list (nothing to reconcile). **Bug B ‚Äî sector-chip polarity mislabel** (root-cause of repeated user reports of the shape "card says sector is bearish but it should be bullish"): the confluence-engine sector chips (`stocvest/signals/confluence.py`) used the labels "Sector Bullish" / "Sector Bearish" / "Sector conflict" to describe the sector's **alignment with the setup**, but the wording reads as a **polarity verdict on the sector itself**. The sector layer's actual measurement is relative strength *vs SPY* (XLF can be up in absolute terms yet labelled "bearish" if it lags SPY) ‚Äî the chip text obscured that. **Fix**: the chip label now describes the **sector's intrinsic state relative to SPY** and the ‚úì/‚úï column carries the alignment signal on its own. Bullish-relative sector ‚Üí "Sector leads market" (detail "Sector ETF outperforming SPY (relative strength)."); bearish-relative sector ‚Üí "Sector lags market" (detail "Sector ETF underperforming SPY (relative strength)."); whether the chip lands in `confirming_signals` or `conflicting_signals` is determined by the setup direction. Neutral sector signal produces no chip. The frontend renders chip labels verbatim ‚Äî no production code parses the literal string. **Lock-in tests**: backend +5 in `tests/signals/test_confluence.py` under "Sector chip label invariants (BRK-B fix, 2026-05-13)" ‚Äî bullish-sector-long pins "Sector leads market" + "SPY" in detail, bearish-sector-short pins "Sector lags market" + explicit anti-regression assertions that the strings "Sector Bearish" and "Sector Bullish" are NEVER in the label, bullish-sector-short pins the symmetry invariant (label still says "Sector leads market" but chip lands in conflicting), bearish-sector-long symmetric counterpart, neutral-sector produces no sector_alignment chip in either list. Frontend +0 net (existing `tests/signal-evidence.test.ts` reconciler tests updated to use the relabelled chip strings ‚Äî BRK-B regression test now seeds `confirming: [{ label: "Sector lags market" }]` so the test reflects what users actually see on screen; `SignalEvidenceCard` render test asserts both the new label is present AND the old "Sector Bearish" string is NEVER in the rendered HTML). **Why this matters operationally**: the confusing chip wording cost a debugging round-trip every time a user pinged about sector polarity; the new wording is unambiguous (sector leads or lags SPY, ‚úì means aligned with this setup, ‚úï means against this setup) and the reconciler sentence is symmetric for both setup directions. The deprecated "Sector Bullish" / "Sector Bearish" labels are referenced in the codebase only inside historical-context comments and regression-guard assertions (`expect(html).not.toContain("Sector Bearish")` in the render test, `assert "Sector Bearish" not in matched[0]["label"]` in the backend test). Backend baseline now **1387 passing** (+5 over 1382). |
| 15 | **Layer 4 (second slice) ‚Äî SWR coverage extended to composite, news, dashboard, macro ‚Äî SHIPPED (frontend only) ‚úÖ** Commit landing **2026-05-13** (no terraform / no lambda change, no API contract change). Direct follow-up to row 13 (Layer 4 first slice). Scope was the second-slice plan parked in `docs/PERFORMANCE.md` ¬ß1 layer 4 + ¬ß4C + the D11 backlog row: extend the SWR cache surface to the remaining imperative `useEffect ‚Üí fetch` blocks on the two heaviest-traffic surfaces (`/dashboard/signals` and `/dashboard`). **Four new hooks added under `frontend/lib/hooks/`:** (a) `use-signal-composite.ts` ‚Äî `useSignalComposite(symbol, mode, { enabled })` wraps the POST to `/api/stocvest/signals/composite/{swing\|real}` with `{ symbol }` body, cache key `["stocvest:signal-composite", upperCaseSymbol, mode]`. Mode is part of the key so Mode Separation invariant #5 in `PERFORMANCE.md` survives the cache layer (a swing-engine composite for AAPL never aliases the day-engine composite for AAPL). Hook overrides the global `keepPreviousData:true` to `keepPreviousData:false` ‚Äî the signals page has an explicit user-requested "clear screen between mode pills" UX rule (lock-ins in `tests/signals-page-mode-clears-screen.test.tsx`), so a fresh cache-key transition must return `composite:null` synchronously rather than carry the previous mode's data on screen during the transition. (b) `use-symbol-news.ts` ‚Äî `useSymbolNews(symbol, { limit, mode, enabled })` wraps the existing `fetchSymbolNews`, cache key `["stocvest:symbol-news", upperCaseSymbol, limit, mode]`. Errors collapse to `articles:[]` so the after-hours panel never shows a dangling spinner. Keeps the global `keepPreviousData:true` default ‚Äî adjacent-symbol toggles within the same mode keep the previous article list on screen until the new one resolves. (c) `use-dashboard-payload.ts` ‚Äî `useDashboardPayload(mode, { refreshIntervalMs })` wraps `fetchDashboardData`, cache key `["stocvest:dashboard-payload", mode]`. Exposes a stable `dashboardPayloadKey(mode)` builder so the live-hint SSE handler can `mutate(dashboardPayloadKey(mode))` without duplicating the namespace string. Default `refreshIntervalMs:60_000` matches the pre-Layer-4 `setInterval` cadence; SWR's `refreshInterval` pauses automatically when the tab is hidden (free polling-cost reduction). (d) `use-macro-context.ts` ‚Äî `useMacroContext()` wraps `fetchMacroContext`, cache key `["stocvest:macro-context"]`. Single-tuple key with NO user-id segment ‚Äî the endpoint is user-agnostic so we deliberately dedupe across users on the same browser (cross-cutting invariant #2 in `PERFORMANCE.md`). **Three call sites refactored**: (i) `components/signals-page-client.tsx` ‚Äî dropped `[compositeResult, setCompositeResult]` and `[radarData, setRadarData]` `useState` pair plus the entire `[symbol, tab, tradingMode]` composite `useEffect` (~70 lines). `compositeResult` is now read from `useSignalComposite`; `radarData` becomes a pure `useMemo` projection of `compositeResult`; `signalEvidence` lifecycle stays local (it's built from a different source ‚Äî the user-initiated "Show evidence" download click) but resets via a slimmer `useEffect` keyed on `[symbol, tab, tradingMode, compositeResult]`. The mode-toggle `updateTradingMode` callback no longer needs to imperatively `setCompositeResult(null)` / `setRadarData(null)` ‚Äî the cache key change does that for us via `keepPreviousData:false`. The after-hours news `fetchSymbolNews` Promise.all path was split: news goes through `useSymbolNews({ enabled: showAfterHoursPanel })`, watchlist membership keeps its own thin `useEffect`. (ii) `components/dashboard-edge-sync.tsx` ‚Äî replaced the local `setInterval(refresh, 60_000)` polling loop + `useState<DashboardResponse>` + `useCallback refresh` with a single `useDashboardPayload(mode)` call. The SSE hint handler (`useLiveSignals`) now calls `mutate(dashboardPayloadKey(mode))` via `useSWRConfig` instead of running its own refresh closure. Local-mode-state + `storage` event listener stay ‚Äî SWR is read-only as far as the user's mode pill is concerned. **Note on `/api/signals/live`**: the SSE stream stays as `EventSource` (it's a push channel, not a GET-and-cache) ‚Äî `useLiveSignals` is unchanged. The "convert `/api/live` to SWR" line in the original D11 backlog row referred to the polling re-fetch that the SSE hint triggers, NOT the SSE stream itself. That part now flows through `mutate(dashboardPayloadKey(mode))`. (iii) `components/dashboard-redesign.tsx` ‚Äî dropped the `[macroPulse, setMacroPulse] useState` + the one-shot `useEffect ‚Üí fetchMacroContext()` cleanup-flagged Promise. `macroPulse` now reads from `useMacroContext()`. **Test posture (per user instruction ‚Äî full suite is run end of day)**: 4 new test files added ‚Äî `tests/use-signal-composite.test.tsx` (7 tests pinning empty/whitespace short-circuit, `enabled:false`, swing/day endpoint routing, dedupe of same-key hooks, non-2xx ‚Üí null), `tests/use-symbol-news.test.tsx` (6 tests pinning short-circuit, `enabled:false`, key shape, dedupe, mode-key isolation, error collapse), `tests/use-dashboard-payload.test.tsx` (5 tests pinning happy path, dedupe, mode-key isolation, `dashboardPayloadKey` stability, error path), `tests/use-macro-context.test.tsx` (5 tests pinning happy path, dedupe, null back-compat, error path, `macroContextKey` stability). **23 new tests across 4 files; all 23 pass.** Existing lock-ins that interact with the refactored surface ‚Äî `tests/signals-page-mode-clears-screen.test.tsx`, `tests/signals-page-streaming.test.tsx`, `tests/dashboard-cache.test.ts`, `tests/dashboard-hover-prefetch.test.tsx`, `tests/dashboard-prefetch.test.tsx`, `tests/use-symbol-snapshot.test.tsx` ‚Äî all 37 tests across 6 files pass. `signals-page-mode-clears-screen.test.tsx` got one targeted test-infra update: the test now wraps each render in a fresh `<SWRConfig provider={() => new Map()} dedupingInterval={0}>` so SWR cache state does NOT leak between tests. The "clear screen between modes" UX rule applies to UNCACHED flips; a cached flip is instant (a strictly better UX) and the test would otherwise oscillate based on prior-test side effects. **Why this matters operationally**: the most-clicked surface (mode-toggle ‚Üí composite refetch ‚Üí 1‚Äì2s back-end latency) now hits the SWR cache after the first round trip. The dashboard polling loop is no longer redundant with whatever hits `useDashboardPayload(mode)` elsewhere on the dashboard (currently only the edge-sync observability badge, but the surface is now shaped for future islands without re-introducing parallel polling). Future PRs that add a fifth `useEffect ‚Üí fetch` block on these surfaces should prefer a new SWR hook over an imperative effect ‚Äî the patterns are now in-tree. The full frontend suite will be run at end of day per the user's "do not run all tests now" instruction. |

1. **Infrastructure:** Same as checklist rows 1‚Äì2; keep API Gateway URLs and Cognito/Vercel env aligned with the deployed stage. **News pipeline note:** queue + consumer Lambda can be applied now; the optional ECS news worker still requires `news_worker_container_image` to be set before Terraform will create the task/service.
2. **Broker/runtime services:** IBKR path needs ECS/Fargate + TWS/ibeam where applicable; the new always-on news worker also needs an image publish/push path plus Redis reachability from the app security group.
3. **CI hardening (if not done):** setuptools upgrade in CI before `pip install -e .`; optional skip for Vercel deploy when hook secret missing. Add worker image build/push automation if you want the ECS runtime deployed from CI.
4. **Legal / launch:** Terms at `/terms` are a **draft** ‚Äî attorney review before paid subscribers; **mandatory legal acknowledgment (B2)** is implemented before dashboard use; optional onboarding wizard remains dismissible per session until completed.

---

## 4. Legal compliance (product & API)

- STOCVEST is **not** a registered investment adviser; frame as **signal intelligence** and data tooling.
- **UI:** Prefer signal summary, signal strength, reference levels, signal parameters‚Äînot ‚Äúverdict,‚Äù ‚Äúrecommendation,‚Äù ‚Äúyou should,‚Äù or ‚Äúconfidence‚Äù in **signal** context.
- **`SignalDisclaimerChip`** on signal cards; **`GlobalDisclaimer`** last in `<body>` in root layout.
- **Performance page:** Directional accuracy only; not dollar P&L as ‚Äúsignal performance.‚Äù
- **Serialized API:** Use `signal_summary` / `signal_strength` (and related names) where applicable; include `disclaimer`: *Signal data for informational purposes only. Not investment advice.*
- **Logging / persistence:** Sanitize user-supplied free text before Dynamo (`text_sanitize`); keep CloudWatch logs free of unnecessary PII (`log_privacy`). Server-side identity for journal and protected routes comes from the **JWT**, not from client-supplied `user_id` body fields.

---

## 5. Roadmap & backlog

**Full prioritized themes, sub-tasks, and IDs:** [`docs/BACKLOG.md`](./BACKLOG.md) ‚Äî **single source** for planned work so this file stays short.

**Directional summary:** After infra/broker production readiness (`¬ß3`), focus shifts to **subscriptions**, **sector/internals**, **D2 backtesting / analytics**, **Phase 7 hardening**, and the post-beta **trade brief** UI (`BACKLOG.md` sections B, D, P, G, M, T). **D1** signal outcomes, **B1** journal automation, **B2** onboarding + legal acknowledgment, **B3** alerts (email), and **B4** watchlists are shipped (see status table). **B13** (SMS) remains pending until phone collection is ready.

---

## 6. Key decisions (unchanged summary)

1. Stack: Next.js (Vercel) + Python Lambdas (AWS).  
2. Brokers: IBKR (TWS / ib_insync) + E*TRADE (OAuth REST).  
3. Market data: Polygon.io (stocks advanced + options + crypto tiers as configured).  
4. Multi-tenant isolation end-to-end.  
5. Asset scope: stocks, ETFs, options, futures, crypto (scope varies by data source).  
6. Six signal layers: Technical, News, Macro, Sector, Geopolitical, Internals.  
7. AI: Claude (Sonnet) ‚Üí structured JSON for synthesis; **public APIs use compliance field names** (`signal_summary`, `signal_strength`, ‚Ä¶).  
8. Domain: **stocvest.app**.  
9. Day trading: Phase 2.5 scanner + PDT tracker are first-class.  
10. News ingestion is now multi-source: Benzinga websocket for live news plus SEC EDGAR 8-K polling, with Claude scoring kept in the SQS-triggered Lambda consumer.  
11. **Composite signal architecture:** **Stage A** = per-layer analyzers (each speaks from its own domain); **Stage B** = `CompositeScoreEngine` and handlers reconcile after the fact. Regime multipliers **scale influence**, not the **sign** of a layer‚Äôs directional input (default multipliers stay positive). **Eligibility gates** (e.g. `insufficient_data`) vs **degradation** (e.g. contradiction penalty, R/R warnings) are separate ideas‚Äîsee **`docs/SIGNAL_ENGINE.md`** (¬ß Architecture, ¬ß Composite, ¬ß Future enhancements).

---

## 7. Immutable contracts

Do **not** change without discussion and coordinated updates:

- **`BrokerAdapter`** ‚Äî eight methods, types, exceptions (`docs/API_CONTRACTS.md` ¬ß1).  
- **HTTP paths** ‚Äî versioned under `/v1/`; breaking changes need `/v2/` or migration.  
- **DynamoDB table names** ‚Äî `Users`, `BrokerConnections`, `Watchlists`, `Alerts`, `Orders`, **`SignalHistory`**, **`TradeJournal`**, **`PDTState`**, **`AuditEvents`** (HTTP audit items; `pk`/`sk` per `audit_store.py`), etc.  
- **Secrets path** ‚Äî `/stocvest/{userId}/brokers/{brokerId}`.  
- **Canonical types** ‚Äî `stocvest/data/models.py` (no raw Polygon dicts in core logic).  
- **Snapshot + intraday + VIX invariants** (verified; do not re‚Äëdiscover in prompts):
  1. **`Snapshot` model** ‚Äî Pydantic `Snapshot` in `stocvest/data/models.py` (not a separate parser class). Raw Polygon ticker dicts map only through `PolygonClient._parse_snapshot()` ‚Üí `Snapshot`. **Do not** add a `SnapshotParser` class, **do not** read raw Polygon keys in layer/analyzer code, **do** use `Snapshot` field names everywhere: `symbol`, `last_trade_price`, `last_trade_size`, `last_quote_bid`, `last_quote_ask`, `day_open`, `day_high`, `day_low`, `day_close`, `day_volume`, `day_vwap`, `prev_close`, `change`, `change_percent`, `pre_market_price`, `pre_market_change_percent`, `after_hours_price`, `after_hours_change_percent`, `market_status`, `company_name`, `prev_day_volume`. Layer analyzers take **`Snapshot`** instances (or derived inputs), not raw dicts.
  2. **`IntradaySetupScanner`** ‚Äî Does **not** fetch bars. Signature: `scan(bars_by_symbol: dict[str, list[Bar]], ‚Ä¶)`. Handlers fetch bars then pass them in. To reuse intraday math inside something like a technical layer, import **`IntradayVWAPCalculator`**, **`IntradayEMA9Calculator`**, **`OpeningRangeBreakoutDetector`** (and related helpers in `day_trading_scanner.py`) ‚Äî **not** the scanner class as a nested ‚Äúanalyzer.‚Äù
  3. **VIX** ‚Äî Reuse `get_vix_snapshot_with_fallback` and tuple `VIX_SNAPSHOT_FALLBACK_SYMBOLS` from `stocvest/api/services/morning_brief_fetch.py` (`I:VIX` ‚Üí `^VIX` ‚Üí `VIX`). **Do not** add another VIX fetcher or a single hardcoded/configured VIX ticker as the primary approach; the **ordered fallback list** is the contract.
  4. **Day vs last trade scale** ‚Äî `_parse_snapshot` already drops inconsistent `day` OHLC/VWAP when out of line with `lastTrade.p` (5√ó bound via `_session_day_prices_align_with_last`). Use **`snapshot.last_trade_price`** for current/near price; **do not** duplicate that sanity check downstream.
  5. **Extended hours** ‚Äî `preMarket`/`premarket` and `afterHours`/`afterhours` key variants are normalized inside `_parse_snapshot` into `pre_market_*` / `after_hours_*` on **`Snapshot`**; use those fields, not raw dict access.

Signal **layer enums** and internal composite types are stable; **customer-facing** naming follows the Legal section above.

---

## 8. Known issues / technical debt

- `pyproject.toml` / setuptools: may need `pip install setuptools --upgrade` before editable install on some machines.  
- PDT rolling window is weekday-based; exchange holidays not modeled‚Äîalign with broker if needed.  
- Stochastic implementation has a small style debt (not correctness).  
- **Mitigated (local pytest, Windows + Python 3.14):** botocore‚Äôs user-agent path could trigger WMI via `platform.uname()` from threads and print ‚Äúaccess violation‚Äù to stderr; **`tests/conftest.py`** primes `platform.uname()` on import and clears **`DYNAMODB_USERS_TABLE`** in the autouse fixture so handler imports do not eagerly create Dynamo clients.

## 12. Day-trading scan rhythm (reference)

- **Pre-market:** gap + catalyst scan ‚Üí ranked candidates.  
- **RTH:** intraday setup scanner (~5 min cadence per design), VWAP/OR/EMA logic in engine.  
- **PDT:** warn at 2 day trades, block at 3 (non-exempt) in rolling window.

---

## 13. Session rules

### STEP 0 ‚Äî Read and verify (no guessing)

Do this **before** designing or naming APIs against external data. **¬ß7 ‚ÄúSnapshot + intraday + VIX invariants‚Äù** is the canonical checklist (field names, `IntradaySetupScanner` boundaries, VIX helper, no duplicate day/last checks, extended hours on `Snapshot`).

1. **Open the real implementation** ‚Äî e.g. `polygon_client.py`, `models.py` (`Snapshot`), `day_trading_scanner.py` (`IntradaySetupScanner` + calculators), `morning_brief_fetch.py` (`get_vix_snapshot_with_fallback`).
2. **Polygon JSON keys** ‚Äî Only keys read in `_parse_snapshot` (and other explicit parsers in `polygon_client.py`) are authoritative. New surface area ‚Üí extend `_parse_snapshot` + tests.
3. **Decisions in code reviews** ‚Äî Prefer commit messages or PR notes with **why** and **rejected alternatives** where non-obvious.
4. **Tests assert design, not trivia** ‚Äî e.g. VIX fallback order, dropped `day` when scale mismatches, scanner RVOL gates.
5. **Commits** ‚Äî When several separable decisions land in one session, **order commits** for independent `git revert`. One cohesive change may still use a single commit (¬ß13 STEP 4).

### Before writing any code

1. Read `docs/CONTEXT.md` and `docs/BACKLOG.md` in full.
2. Confirm exact test counts:
   - Run: `pytest tests/ -q`
   - Run: `cd frontend && npm run test`
   - Record actual numbers ‚Äî do not use ‚Äú~‚Äù approximations.
   - If counts are **lower** than the baseline in **¬ß13 Test baseline** (and the summary line under the document title), stop and report the regression before doing anything else.
3. Do not implement anything already marked ‚úÖ in ¬ß1.
4. Do not implement anything not in `BACKLOG.md` without flagging it to the user first.
5. Do not change any contract in `docs/API_CONTRACTS.md` without explicit instruction.

### Every prompt must end with ALL of these steps

 **STEP 1 ‚Äî Tests**  
Run `pytest tests/ -q`  
Run `cd frontend && npm run test` (Vitest; do not pass Jest‚Äôs `--watchAll=false`)  
Run `cd frontend && npm run build`  
Report exact counts. If any count dropped, fix before proceeding to documentation updates.

**STEP 2 ‚Äî Update `docs/CONTEXT.md`**  
- ¬ß1 Status table: mark completed tracks ‚úÖ; update Notes if anything changed.  
- ¬ß2 Implemented: add new files/modules built this session.  
- ¬ß3 Pending: remove items that are now resolved; add new blockers discovered this session.  
- ¬ß13 Test baseline: update exact backend and frontend test counts (and note if `npm run build` was verified).  
- Document title summary line: keep test baseline in sync with ¬ß13.  
- **Last updated** date: set to today.

**STEP 3 ‚Äî Update `docs/BACKLOG.md`**  
- Items completed this session: change status to **DONE**; add: `Done YYYY-MM-DD ¬∑ commit: <hash>`.  
- Items discovered this session: add with new ID, description, and acceptance criteria.  
- Items in progress but not finished: change status to **In progress**.  
- **Do not delete any row ‚Äî ever.**  
- **Last updated** date.

**STEP 4 ‚Äî Commit**  
- Stage: all code + `docs/CONTEXT.md` + `docs/BACKLOG.md` together.  
- Message format (required):  
  `"<feature> | backend: <N> tests | frontend: <N> tests"`  
  where **backend N** = pytest **passed** count and **frontend N** = Vitest **passed** count (from the respective summaries).  
  Example:  
  `"B2 onboarding wizard | backend: 468 tests | frontend: 50 tests"`  
- Never commit code without committing updated docs.  
- Never commit docs without committing the code they describe.

### What goes where ‚Äî hard rules

| Content type | File | Rule |
|--------------|------|------|
| What is built and working | CONTEXT.md ¬ß1‚Äì2 | Reality only |
| Near-term blockers & ops | CONTEXT.md ¬ß3 | Keep current; not duplicated in BACKLOG |
| Planned work & acceptance notes | BACKLOG.md | Full detail; **never delete rows** (mark DONE + date + commit) |
| HTTP & broker contracts | API_CONTRACTS.md | Change only with explicit instruction |
| Legal framing (copy & public API) | CONTEXT.md ¬ß4 | Align product language and payloads |

### Test baseline (exact counts ‚Äî update after every verified run)

| Suite | Command | Last verified |
|-------|---------|---------------|
| Backend | `pytest tests/ -q` | **1545 passed**, **3 skipped** (full suite verified **2026-05-16** after **B33** phase 2 ‚Äî store + `GET /v1/signals/scanner-trace`; prior **1541 passed**, **3 skipped** after B33 phase 1) ‚Äî +3 in `tests/api/test_scanner_setups_bundle.py`; prior **1461 passed**, **3 skipped** verified **2026-05-14** after **Gap Intelligence** ‚Äî +27 over 1434; prior focused-run note ‚Äî **1434 passed**, **3 skipped** (focused-run verified 2026-05-13 after the **BRK.B Evidence Card ‚Äî catastrophic stale-bars root cause + 4 user-reported issues** shipment ‚Äî **+7** split between `tests/data/test_polygon_client.py::TestGetBars` (3 new wire-level recency tests pinning `sort=desc` reverse on recent-mode + `sort=asc` preservation on explicit-range + partial-edge conservative range mode) and `tests/signals/test_confluence.py` (7 new internals-chip tests under the "Internals-alignment chip invariants" block, **including** a direct BRK.B regression `test_internals_bullish_on_short_setup_lands_in_conflicting_BRK_B_regression`). The prior 1051/3 baseline (verified 2026-05-11 after the **Dashboard two-desk render + chatbot routing priority order** shipment ‚Äî **+13** over the prior 1038/3 baseline, distributed across two commits. **Phase 0 ‚Äî chatbot routing rules (commit `6a25041`)** added **+8** to `tests/signals/test_assistant_prompts.py` covering the new `MODE RESOLUTION PRIORITY ORDER (CHATBOT ROUTING)` section: `test_prompt_carries_mode_resolution_priority_order_section_header` (pins the section header + the one-sentence anchor "you resolve WHERE the question lives before deciding WHAT to say"); `test_prompt_priority_1_explicit_screen_context` (pins P1 mechanic + behavioral contract "you do NOT ask a clarifying question and you do NOT mention the other mode" + two example surfaces ‚Äî Signals page with `trading_mode=swing` and Scanner with `scanner_focus=day`); `test_prompt_priority_2_explicit_mode_language` (pins the four trigger terms `swing` / `multi-day` / `day trade` / `intraday` + symmetric swing-only and day-only example responses); `test_prompt_priority_3_structured_dual_answer_template` (pins the verbatim two-paragraph template lines + the INDEPENDENT STATUS REPORTS framing); `test_prompt_priority_3_bans_comparative_and_connective_language` (pins four canonical violations ‚Äî "Compare the two desks", "frame one as a fallback", "Suggest the user switch desks", "Headline a 'system overall' summary" + three connective-tissue connectives "on the other hand", "however", "instead"); `test_prompt_bans_mode_inference_from_market_behavior` (pins the NEVER section header + three inference patterns by shape ‚Äî swing-is-quiet-so-user-means-day, high-intraday-volatility-so-day, choppy-markets-suggest-day-trades + the positive framing "Mode is resolved by Priority 1, Priority 2, or Priority 3 only"); `test_prompt_clarifying_question_fallback_is_one_shot_and_verbatim` (pins the exact wording "Do you mean swing (multi-day) or day (intraday) trading? STOCVEST evaluates those as independent decision engines." + "EXACTLY ONE clarifying question" + the dual-desk carve-out so the LLM does not use it as a stalling tactic on screens that already resolve mode); `test_prompt_deterministic_response_to_cross_mode_substitution` (pins the deterministic-shape contract "deterministic and short" + "refuses the comparison, explains the independence" + the validation-numbers gate "does not reference validation numbers as evidence for or against either engine"). **Phase 1 ‚Äî Dashboard two-desk render** added **+5** to the same test file covering the new dual-desk page-context allowlist: `test_serialize_page_context_emits_dual_desk_posture_on_dashboard` (pins both `swing_desk_posture=active` AND `day_desk_posture=suppressed_no_confirmation` emitted together AND `trading_mode=` is deliberately absent so the LLM does not inherit a single mode via Priority 1); `test_serialize_page_context_dual_desk_session_closed_variant` (pins the distinct `suppressed_session_closed` variant from `suppressed_no_confirmation` ‚Äî the LLM uses session-bound language for one and intraday-confirmation language for the other); `test_serialize_page_context_rejects_invalid_desk_posture_values` (pins that `swing_desk_posture=actionable_now` and `day_desk_posture=FOMO_BUY` are dropped silently ‚Äî closes the attack surface where a malicious client could steer the LLM through freeform posture strings); `test_serialize_page_context_emits_day_setups_count_when_nonzero` (pins the day-setups-count field with value `3`); `test_serialize_page_context_dashboard_dual_desk_omits_swing_only_fields` (pins that the dashboard's dual-desk context does NOT accidentally turn on stale scanner-overview fields like `top_setup_1=` / `top_gap_1=` / `gap_with_catalyst_count=` when only the posture fields are supplied ‚Äî guards against the serializer regressing into emitting unrelated fields). The prior 1038/3 baseline (2026-05-11) was the **mode-separation safety perimeter** upgrade ‚Äî **+9** over the prior 1029/3 baseline, all in `tests/signals/test_assistant_prompts.py`. The upgrade adds a SECOND perpendicular safety axis on top of the existing LOGGED-OUT / LOGGED-IN two-context perimeter: **Swing trading (multi-day) and Day trading (intraday) are independent decision engines that share market context but never share decisions, readiness, validation, or activity permission.** Six new sections were merged into `ASSISTANT_SYSTEM_PROMPT` between `CRITICAL CONTEXT AWARENESS RULE` and `PRIMARY GOAL` (additive, no destruction of any prior section): (1) **MODE SEPARATION (SWING VS DAY) ‚Äî ABSOLUTE DESIGN RULE** declares the separation NON-NEGOTIABLE, names the active mode as the authoritative scope, and tells the LLM to treat dashboards/scanners showing both modes as two separate desks; (2) **WHAT MAY BE SHARED ACROSS MODES** enumerates the 5 allowed-shared items (Market regime, Macro context, Sector rotation, Market internals, Risk posture) with the explicit qualifier "Sharing context does NOT imply shared permission to trade"; (3) **WHAT MUST NEVER BE SHARED ACROSS MODES** enumerates the 8 always-mode-specific items (Trade Readiness scores, Layer alignment percentages, Signal validity windows, Gating outcomes, Validation statistics, Accuracy metrics, Portfolio linkage, Journal entries); (4) **SCREEN-LEVEL MODE BEHAVIOR** spells out the per-screen rules (Dashboard = Swing Desk + Day Desk parallel posture reporting; Scanner = two sections not a merged mode-column table when `scanner_focus=both`; Signals = exactly one mode at a time authored by `trading_mode=swing|day`; Signal Validation = mode-isolated tracks; Portfolio = mode attribution per position; Journal = one mode per entry; Performance = mode-segmented never combined-headline); (5) **MODE-AWARE EMPTY-STATE LANGUAGE** requires suppression copy to reflect the suppressed engine's vocabulary (Swing emphasizes multi-day confirmation + regime/sector alignment + structure readiness; Day emphasizes intraday confirmation + volume/momentum timing + session-specific conditions; "Never use identical copy for both modes"); (6) **MODE-SEPARATION USER INTERACTION RULES (ADDITIVE)** stack on top of the existing USER INTERACTION RULES with the new MAY/MUST NOT pairs ‚Äî explicitly bans "Suggest using Day signals because Swing is quiet (or vice versa)", "Headline a combined accuracy number or a 'system overall' verdict that averages across modes", "Recommend one mode over the other as a workaround for the other's suppression". The exemplar exchange "Swing is quiet ‚Äî should I day-trade instead?" is written into the prompt with the correct refusal pattern (explain that the two engines gate independently, that Swing's quiet is a Swing decision not a Day permission). Additionally, one new bullet was grafted onto the existing `HISTORICAL VALIDATION CONTEXT (LOGGED-IN ONLY)` MUST NOT list: **"Use the figures to encourage activity during a suppressed regime"** ‚Äî closes the loophole where the assistant might counter the user contrasting a 62% accuracy figure against today's empty board ("you say accuracy is 62% ‚Äî why aren't there any setups today?") by using the accuracy figure to argue for activity instead of explaining the active gate. Past directional accuracy and current SUPPRESSION & GATING LOGIC are two independent surfaces that must never be played off against each other. **+9 lock-in tests** in `tests/signals/test_assistant_prompts.py`: `test_prompt_declares_mode_separation_as_absolute_design_rule` (pins "NON-NEGOTIABLE" + "Swing and Day must NEVER be blended"), `test_prompt_lists_what_may_be_shared_across_modes` (pins the 5-item allowed-shared list + "Sharing context does NOT imply shared permission to trade"), `test_prompt_lists_what_must_never_be_shared_across_modes` (pins the 8-item mode-specific list), `test_prompt_carries_dashboard_two_desk_rule` (pins "Swing Desk" + "Day Desk" + "Active / Monitor / Suppressed"), `test_prompt_carries_scanner_two_section_rule` (pins `scanner_focus=both` + "TWO sections" + the anti-pattern "not a single merged table with a mode column"), `test_prompt_carries_signals_page_single_mode_rule` (pins "operates in exactly one mode at a time" + `trading_mode=swing|day` + "Never reuse readiness, alignment, or conclusions across modes"), `test_prompt_carries_mode_specific_empty_state_rule` (pins both per-mode suppression vocabularies + "Never use identical copy for both modes"), `test_prompt_bans_cross_mode_substitution` (pins "Suggest using Day signals because Swing is quiet" + "the two engines gate independently" + the combined-accuracy headline ban), `test_prompt_bans_validation_to_encourage_activity_during_suppression` (pins the new historical-validation ban + "DESCRIPTIVE of past behavior" + "NEVER a reason to override the current SUPPRESSION & GATING LOGIC" + the exemplar user prompt "why aren't there any setups today"). **All 50 pre-existing prompt tests still green** ‚Äî the merge-additive integration preserved every safety behavior locked in over the prior phases (LOGGED-OUT public-mode rules, six-layer naming model, verbatim decision states, banned-phrase list, payment-tier awareness, the detailed `=== HISTORICAL VALIDATION ===` block semantics including em-dash-as-no-resolved-trades, sentinel anchoring, "no block means no comment + never invent a number + never recall a number from a previous turn"). No production code changes, no Terraform / IAM / API contract / DynamoDB-schema changes, no frontend code touched. The prior 1029/3 baseline (2026-05-11) was D3 analyzer-wire-up lock-in ‚Äî **+8** over the prior 1021/3 baseline: **2 in `tests/signals/test_technical_analyzer.py`** (`test_bullish_threshold_param_actually_drives_verdict` ‚Äî same uptrend bars + snapshot through `TechnicalParameters(bullish_threshold=55)` vs `bullish_threshold=99` produces an identical raw score but a differing verdict, locking in that `TechnicalAnalyzer` reads the threshold from the `params` argument it was passed and not from a hardcoded constant; ## 14. Appendix: Business / entity (high level)

- Entity target: **STOCVEST LLC** (Delaware); formation and Stripe Atlas items **track outside this doc**.  
- **What STOCVEST is:** signal intelligence + execution tooling; user keeps custody via their broker.  
- **What it is not:** RIA, broker-dealer, custodian, fund manager.  
- Before **paid** users: attorney-reviewed ToS/Privacy, LLC, Stripe, production infra.
